 
an̪aːmat̪eːjaɾin pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk minput̪t̪akam

in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akam en̪t̪a iʈat̪t̪ilum en̪t̪a t͡ʃelaʋum illaːmal eʋaɾum pajanpaʈut̪t̪akkuːʈijat̪u
kiʈʈat̪t̪aʈʈa en̪t̪a kaʈʈuppaːʈukaɭum illaj n̪iːŋkaɭ at̪aj n̪akaleʈukkalaːm kaொʈukkalaːm allat̪u kaொʈukkalaːm
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk uɾimat̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭin kiːɻ at̪aj miːɳʈum pajanpaʈut̪t̪aʋum
in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akat̪t̪uʈan allat̪u  il aːnlajnil


t̪alajppu pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪aj

aːt͡ʃiɾijaɾ an̪aːmat̪eːja

maொɻipejaɾppaːɭaɾ t͡ʃaɾ eʈʋin aɾnaːlʈ

iʈukaj t̪eːt̪i d͡ʒuːn   minput̪t̪akam #
ʋeɭijaːna t̪eːt̪i n̪aʋampaɾ 
mut̪al iʈukaj d͡ʒanaʋaɾi  

aːŋkila moɻi

eɻut̪t̪u t̪aொkuppu kurijaːkkam 

*** in̪t̪at̪ t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in aːɾampam kuʈʈanpeɾk minput̪t̪akam pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪aj ***




d͡ʒeːt͡ʃi pajjaɾs t̪ajaːɾit̪t̪uɭɭaːɾ al hejinsin  pat̪ippu










t̪i
paːʈal t͡ʃelasʈal
allat̪u
pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪aj
makaːpaːɾat̪at̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u
aɾd͡ʒunan iʈajjeː oɾu uɾajjaːʈal
in̪t̪ijaːʋin iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ marrum ujaɾn̪t̪aʋaɾ
kiɾuʂɳaɾin ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪in kiːɻ


t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a uɾajjiliɾun̪t̪u maொɻipejaɾkkappaʈʈat̪u
muːlam
t͡ʃaɾ eʈʋin aɾnaːlʈ
  
n̪ijuːjaːɾk
ʈɾuːslaோʋ haːnt͡ʃan & kaோmpaː limiʈeʈ
 ajn̪t̪aːʋat̪u aʋenjuː




aɾppaɳippu

in̪t̪ijaːʋirku

in̪t̪a arput̪amaːna marrum urt͡ʃaːkamaːna uɾajjaj n̪aːn paʈit̪t̪iɾukkireːn
kiɾuʂɳaː marrum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ aɾd͡ʒun oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾukkum oʋʋaொɾu t͡ʃaொrpaொɻiʋu n̪aʈat̪t̪inaːɾ
at̪anaːl n̪aːn at̪an ɲaːnat̪t̪aj iŋkeː eɻut̪ukireːn  at̪an marajn̪t̪iɾukkum maɾmam
iŋkilaːn̪t̪ukku eŋkaɭ in̪t̪ijaːʋeː aʋaɭajp paோlaʋeː enakkup piɾijamaːnaʋaɭ

eʈʋin aɾnaːlʈ





munnuɾaj
in̪t̪a pukaɻperra marrum arput̪amaːna t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a kaʋit̪aj makaːpaːɾat̪at̪t̪in oɾu at̪t̪ijaːjamaːka aːraːʋat̪u  allat̪u piːʂmaː  peɾija hin̪t̪u kaːʋijat̪t̪in paɾʋaːʋil ʋaɾukirat̪u it̪u in̪t̪ijaːʋil apaɾimit̪amaːna pukaɻajjum at̪ikaːɾat̪t̪ajjum perruɭɭat̪u aŋku it̪u t̪eːʋan̪aːkiɾi ilakkijat̪t̪in ajn̪t̪u n̪akajkaɭil paɲt͡ʃaɾat̪nani  onraːkak kaɳakkiʈappaʈukirat̪u eɭija aːnaːl unnat̪amaːna maொɻijil it̪u oɾu t̪at̪t̪uʋa amajppaj ʋiɾiʋupaʈut̪t̪ukirat̪u it̪u inruʋaɾaj n̪aʈajmurajjil uɭɭa piɾaːmaɳamaːka uɭɭat̪u n̪ampikkaj kapilaɾ pat̪aɲt͡ʃali marrum ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭin kaோʈpaːʈukaɭajp paோlaʋeː onriɳajt̪t̪al at̪an pala ariʋippukaɭ mikaʋum ujaɾn̪t̪aʋaj at̪an apilaːʂajkaɭ mikaʋum t̪uːjmajjaːna marrum menmajjaːna at̪an pakt̪i sklekal t̪anat̪u kaʋit̪ajjajp paʈit̪t̪a piraku uʈajkiraːɾ at̪an arijappaʈaːt̪a aːt͡ʃiɾijaɾajp parrija in̪t̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi marrum paːɾaːʈʈu maːd͡ʒisʈɾaோɾam ɾeʋaɾeɳʈijaː e piɾaːkmanis inʈaɾ t͡ʃaːnt͡ʃit͡ʃimaː piːʈaːʈis aஃpiʂijaː ɾeஃpaɾʈuɾ eɾkaோ ʈe pɾimam ʋaːʈs t͡ʃaːnt͡ʃit͡ʃim n̪ijuːminisk hajppaோஃpeʈʈaː                            in̪t̪a arput̪amaːna aɲt͡ʃalijaj et̪iɾaொlikkirat̪u uɳmajjil iŋku pukut̪t̪appaʈʈa t͡ʃila oɻukkan̪erikaɭ mikaʋum ʋijakkat̪t̪akkaʋaj meːlum at̪an paோt̪anajkaɭukkum put̪ija eːrpaːʈʈirkum iʈajjeː uɭɭa iɳajn̪ilaj  peɾumpaːlum uɳmajjil ʋaːjmaொɻi  paɳʈiʈkaɭukkum miʂanaɾikaɭukkum iʈajjeː oɾu t͡ʃaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃaj eɻun̪t̪uɭɭat̪u aːt͡ʃiɾijaɾ kirist̪aʋa muːlaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u kaʈan ʋaːŋkijaːɾaː allat̪u t͡ʃuʋit͡ʃeːʂakaɾkaɭ marrum appaோst̪alaɾkaɭ aʋaɾiʈamiɾun̪t̪u kaʈan ʋaːŋkinaːɾ

it̪u at̪an t̪eːt̪i parrija keːɭʋijaj eɻuppukirat̪u at̪aj n̪eːɾmarajjaːka t̪iːɾkka muʈijaːt̪u it̪u at͡ʃal makaːpaːɾat̪at̪t̪aj ʋiʈa oɾu kaːlat̪t̪il puɾaːt̪ana it̪ikaːt͡ʃat̪t̪il pat̪ikkappaʈʈiɾukka ʋeːɳʈum aːnaːl t̪iɾu kaːt͡ʃin̪aːt̪ t̪elaːŋ it̪u kirist̪aʋa t͡ʃakaːpt̪at̪t̪irku mun̪t̪ijat̪aːka n̪iɾuːpikka t͡ʃila n̪ijaːjamaːna ʋaːt̪aŋkaɭaj munʋajt̪t̪uɭɭaːɾ eʋʋaːraːjinum t͡ʃaːnrukaɭin eʈaj kirist̪uʋukkup piraku t͡ʃumaːɾ muːnraːm n̪uːrraːɳʈil at̪an kalaʋajjaj ʋajkka munajkirat̪u oɾuʋeːɭaj in̪t̪a piɾaːmaɳak kaʋit̪ajjil kalilijin paːʈaŋkaɭ marrum t͡ʃiɾija aʋat̪aːɾam parrija et̪iɾaொlikaɭ uɳmajjil uɭɭana

at̪an kaːʈt͡ʃi d͡ʒumnaː marrum t͡ʃaɾt͡ʃuːʈʈi n̪at̪ikaɭukku iʈajjeː uɭɭa t͡ʃamamaːna n̪aːʈut̪arpaோt̪u kuɾnul marrum d͡ʒiːn̪t̪ it̪an eɭija t͡ʃat̪i mannan jut̪iʂʈiɾanin t͡ʃakaோt̪aɾanaːna iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ aɾd͡ʒunan t̪eːɾaோʈʈijin ʋeːʈamiʈʈu ut͡ʃt͡ʃa t̪ejʋamaːna kiɾuʂɳanuʈan n̪aʈat̪t̪ija uɾajjaːʈalajk kaொɳʈuɭɭat̪u kaௌɾaʋaɾkaɭ marrum paːɳʈaʋaɾkaɭin paʈajkaɭukku iʈajjeː oɾu peɾija paோɾ ʋaɾaʋiɾukkirat̪u meːlum in̪t̪a uɾajjaːʈal et̪iɾet̪iɾ puɾaʋalaɾkaɭukku iʈajjeː ʋaɾajjappaʈʈa oɾu paோɾ ɾat̪at̪t̪il paɾaːmaɾikkappaʈukirat̪u

kaʋit̪ajjaj paɾnuːஃp piɾaɲt͡ʃu maொɻijilum laːt͡ʃenaːl lat̪t̪iːn maொɻijilum sʈaːnislaːʋ kaʈʈijaːl it̪t̪aːlija maொɻijilum kalaːnaோsaːl kiɾeːkka maொɻijilum t̪iɾu t̪aːmt͡ʃan marrum t̪iɾu ʈeːʋis aːkijaோɾaːl aːŋkilat̪t̪ilum kaʈajt͡ʃijaːkap pejaɾiʈappaʈʈaʋaɾin uɾajn̪aʈaj uɾajn̪aʈajp piɾat̪ijaːka maːrrappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u at̪an n̪ampakat̪t̪anmaj marrum t̪eɭiʋu t̪iɾu t̪elaːŋ pampaːjil peːt͡ʃt͡ʃuʋaɻakku t̪aːɭat̪t̪il oɾu pat̪ippaj ʋeɭijiʈʈaːɾ t͡ʃiran̪t̪a karrarin̪t̪a marrum put̪t̪it͡ʃaːli aːnaːl at͡ʃalin kaɳɳijam allat̪u kaɾuɳajjaj ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪aʋillaj pala t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ariɲaɾkaɭukkup piraku arput̪amaːna kaʋit̪ajjin maொɻipejaɾppaj n̪aːn ʋaɻaŋkat̪ t̪uɳin̪t̪aːl at̪u aʋaɾkaɭin uɻajppiliɾun̪t̪u perappaʈʈa ut̪aʋijaj n̪anrijuʈan aŋkiːkaɾippat̪aːkum meːlum aːŋkila ilakkijam mikaʋum anpaːna kaʋit̪aj marrum t̪at̪t̪uʋap paʈajppajk kaொɳʈiɾukkaːmal n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka muɻumajjaʈajjaːt̪u in̪t̪ijaːʋirku

paːʈal ʋiɳɳulakam t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː ʋiɭakkaʋillaj enru kuːruʋat̪arku ʋeːru et̪uʋum illaj t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a muːlamaːnat̪u anuʂʈup miːʈʈaɾil eɻut̪appaʈʈuɭɭat̪u it̪u meːrkat̪t̪ija kaːt̪ukaɭukku ʋerrikaɾamaːka maruuɾuʋaːkkam t͡ʃejja muʈijaːt̪u enaʋeː n̪aːn at̪aj eŋkaɭ n̪ekiɻʋaːna ʋerru ʋat͡ʃanat̪t̪il pat̪it̪t̪uɭɭeːn at̪eː paோl uɾaj uʈajn̪t̪u paோkum paːʈal ʋaɾikaɭaːka maːrrineːn peɾumpaːlum pinʋaɾum pakkaŋkaɭil uɳaɾʋu uɳmajjaːkap paːt̪ukaːkkappaʈa ʋeːɳʈum enru n̪aːn n̪ampukireːn aːnaːl sklekal aʋaɾkaɭeː iʋʋaːru kuːra ʋeːɳʈum in ɾiːkaːɳʈijaோɾipas miː t͡ʃempaɾ paொjaʈaːஃpaːsʈaɾ meɳʈem ɾekʈeː ʈiʋinaːsseː aஃpaɾmaɾeː n̪aோn aːt͡ʃim kaʋit̪ajjin t̪at̪t̪uʋat̪t̪ajp parri at̪ikam paʈikka ʋiɾumpuʋaோɾ messaɾs ʈɾuːpnaɾ & kaோʋaːl at͡ʃt͡ʃiʈappaʈʈa misʈaɾ ʈeːʋis t̪aொkut̪ijil paːɾaːʈʈat̪t̪akka arimukat̪t̪ajk kaːɳalaːm

eʈʋin aɾnaːlʈ t͡ʃiesaj





uɭɭaʈakkaŋkaɭ

 t̪i ʈisʈɾes aːஃp aɾd͡ʒunaː
 kaோʈpaːʈukaɭin put̪t̪akam
 ʋeːlajjil aram
 ariʋin mat̪am
 ʋeːlajkaɭaj kajʋiʈum mat̪am
 t͡ʃuja kaʈʈuppaːʈu muːlam mat̪am
 pakut̪t̪ariʋu muːlam mat̪am
 t͡ʃupɾiːm t͡ʃeːʋaj muːlam mat̪am
 aɾat͡ʃa ariʋu marrum aɾat͡ʃa maɾmam muːlam mat̪am
 paɾalaோka paɾipuːɾaɳaŋkaɭaːl mat̪am
 onru marrum panmukat̪t̪anmajjin ʋeɭippaːʈu
 n̪ampikkaj mat̪am
 paொɾuɭ marrum aːʋijajp piɾippat̪an muːlam mat̪am
 kuɳaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u piɾippat̪an muːlam mat̪am
 ut͡ʃt͡ʃan̪ilajjaj aʈajʋat̪an muːlam mat̪am
 t̪ejʋiːka marrum t̪ejʋiːkat̪t̪in t̪anit̪t̪anmaj
 mummaʈaŋku n̪ampikkajjaːl mat̪am
 ʋaɻaŋkut̪al marrum t̪urat̪t̪al muːlam mat̪am




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
t̪ɾit̪iɾaːʂʈiɾa
punit̪a t͡ʃamaʋeɭijil paோɾiʈuʋat̪arkaːka iʋʋaːru ʋaɾit͡ʃajppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u
kuɾukʂeːt̪t̪iɾat̪t̪ilt͡ʃaொl t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː t͡ʃol
en makkaɭajjum paːɳʈaʋaɾkaɭajjum enna t͡ʃejt̪at̪u
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃaja
aʋan paːɳʈaʋaɾkaɭin t͡ʃeːnajjajp paːɾt̪t̪apaோt̪u
ɾaːd͡ʒaː t̪uɾijaோt̪anan t̪uɾaோɳan ʋaɾajn̪t̪u
meːlum in̪t̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭaj t͡ʃaொnnaːɾ aː kuɾuʋeː in̪t̪a ʋaɾijajp paːɾuŋkaɭ
paːɳʈu paோɾ ʋiːɾaɾkaɭin paɾappaɭaʋu eʋʋaɭaʋu
t̪uɾupat̪anin makanaːl t͡ʃaɳʈajjiʈappaʈʈat̪u
paோɾil un ariɲaɾ at̪il t̪aɾaʋaɾit͡ʃajjil n̪irkirat̪u
aɾd͡ʒunan paோnra t̪alajʋaɾkaɭ piːman paோnra t̪alajʋaɾkaɭ
ʋillin ʋaɭajʋukaɭ ʋiɾaːʈan jujut̪an
t̪uɾupat̪aː aʋaɾat̪u kaːɾil pukaɻperraʋaɾ
t̪iɾuʂʈakeːt̪ t͡ʃeːkit̪an kaːt͡ʃijin urut̪ijaːna irajʋan
puɾud͡ʒit̪ kun̪t̪ipaோd͡ʒ marrum t͡ʃajʋjaː
jut̪aːmanju marrum ut̪t̪amaௌd͡ʒ uʈan
t͡ʃupat̪ɾaːʋin kuɻan̪t̪aj marrum t̪uɾupat̪ijinanajt̪t̪u pukaɻ
anajʋaɾum oɭiʋiːt͡ʃum t̪eːɾkaɭil eːrrappaʈʈanaɾ
eŋkaɭ pakkat̪t̪ilum  piɾaːmaɳaɾkaɭil t͡ʃiran̪t̪aʋaneː paːɾkka
t͡ʃiran̪t̪a t̪alajʋaɾkaɭ en ʋaɾit͡ʃajjin t̪aɭapat̪ikaɭ
jaːɾuʈajja pejaɾkaɭaj eɳɳuʋat̪il makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi aʈajkireːn n̪iːjeː mut̪al
pinnaɾ piːʂmaɾ kaɾɳan kiɾupaː aːkijaோɾ paோɾil kaʈumajjaːka iɾun̪t̪anaɾ
ʋikaɾɳan asʋat̪t̪aːman iʋarrukku aʈut̪t̪at̪aːka
ʋalimajjaːna t͡ʃaௌmat̪at̪t̪i innum palaɾuʈan
ʋiːɾamum mujart͡ʃijum irappat̪arku in̪t̪a n̪aːɭ t̪ajaːɾaːka uɭɭat̪u
ennajp paொrut̪t̪aʋaɾaj aʋaɾkaɭin ɾaːd͡ʒaː oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾum aʋaɾaʋaɾ aːjut̪at̪t̪ajp parrik kaொɳʈaːɾkaɭ
oʋʋaொɾu t̪urajjilum t̪iramajjaːnaʋaɾkaɭ palaʋiːnamaːnaʋaj
piːʂmaɾ eŋku kaʈʈaɭajjiʈukiraːɾ enpat̪aj n̪amat̪u paோɾ kaːʈʈukirat̪u
marrum piːman aʋanukku munnaːl eːt̪aோ ʋalimajjaːnat̪u
piːʂmaɾin ʋaɾit͡ʃajkku aɾukil n̪am t̪alajʋaɾkaɭ iɾukka ʋeːɳʈum
aʋaɾkaɭ enna ut̪aʋi t͡ʃejjalaːm enpat̪aj t̪ajaːɾ t͡ʃejjuŋkaɭ ippaோt̪u ​​en ʂellaj uːt̪uŋkaɭ
pinnaɾ ʋajat̪aːna mannaɾin t͡ʃamikɲajjil
iɾat̪t̪at̪t̪aj eɻuppum kat̪araluʈan t͡ʃurri uɾuɭum
oɾu t͡ʃiŋkat̪t̪in kaɾd͡ʒanaj paோla ekkaːɭam
peɾija t͡ʃaŋku uːt̪inaːɾ marrum at̪an t͡ʃat̪t̪at̪t̪il
ekkaːɭaŋkaɭ marrum meːɭam t͡ʃaŋkukaɭ marrum kaொmpukaɭ marrum kaொmpukaɭ
t̪iʈiːɾ kuːt͡ʃt͡ʃal ʋeʈit̪t̪at̪u kuɳʈuʋeʈippukaɭ ena
t̪aɭaɾn̪t̪a pujalil at̪t̪akajja kaொn̪t̪aɭippu t̪aோnrijat̪u
appaோt̪u ​​aʋaɾkaɭin t̪aŋkak kaːɾil kaːɳappaʈalaːm
ʋeɭɭaj kut̪iɾajkaɭaːl n̪ukat̪t̪aʈi paோɾ kuɳʈukaɭaj ʋiːt͡ʃukirat̪u
kaʈaʋuɭ kiɾuʂɳaɾ aʋaɾ pakkat̪t̪il aɾd͡ʒunan
muʈit͡ʃt͡ʃup puːʈʈukaɭuʈan kiɾuʂɳaɾ t̪anat̪u peɾija t͡ʃaŋkaj uːt̪inaːɾ
ɾaːʈt͡ʃat̪a elumpu t͡ʃet̪ukkappaʈʈat̪u aɾd͡ʒunan uːt̪inaːn
in̪t̪iɾanin uɾat̪t̪a paɾit͡ʃu piːman pajaŋkaɾamaːna 
oːn̪aːjʋajirruʈajja piːmanoɾu n̪iːɳʈa n̪aːɳalt͡ʃaŋku uːt̪inaːn
kun̪t̪ijin kurramarra makan jut̪iʂʈiɾan
ʋerrijin kuɾal
meːlum n̪akulan t̪an t͡ʃaŋkin miːt̪u t͡ʃapt̪at̪t̪aj uːt̪inaːn
inimajjaːna oli enru pejaɾiʈappaʈʈat̪u t͡ʃahaːt̪eːʋ aʋaɾat̪u miːt̪u
maːɳikkat̪t̪aːl alaŋkaɾikkappaʈʈa marrum kaːt͡ʃijin iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃan aʋaɾat̪u miːt̪u
t͡ʃikaɳʈi t̪an kaːɾil t̪iɾuʂʈat̪jumnan
ʋiɾaːʈaː t͡ʃaːt̪jaki aʈakkappaʈaːt̪aʋan
t̪uɾupat̪aː t̪an makankaɭuʈan oː puːmijin irajʋaneː
n̪iːɳʈa kajkaɭajjuʈajja t͡ʃupat̪ɾaːʋin kuɻan̪t̪ajkaɭ t͡ʃat̪t̪amaːka uːt̪inaːɾkaɭ
at̪anaːl kiɭaŋkaɾ aʋaɾkaɭin et̪iɾikaɭin it̪ajaŋkaɭaj ulukkijat̪u
n̪ila n̪aʈukkam marrum iʈijuʈan kuːʈija ʋaːnat̪t̪uʈan
pinnaɾ it̪u
t̪iɾut̪iɾaːʂʈiɾanin paோɾkkaɭat̪t̪ajp paːɾt̪t̪u
aːjut̪aŋkaɭ aʋiɻkkappaʈut̪al munnaோkki iɻukkappaʈʈa ʋil paோɾ
uʈanaʈijaːka uʈajkkaɾd͡ʒun jaːɾuʈajja t͡ʃinnampeːʈd͡ʒ
hanumaːn kuɾaŋkaː it̪ajp peːt͡ʃu
t̪ejʋiːkamaːna kiɾuʂɳaɾukku aʋaɾat̪u t̪eːɾaோʈʈi
ʈiɾajʋ t̪ajɾijamillaːt̪aʋaɾ t̪iran̪t̪a n̪ilat̪t̪irkut͡ʃ t͡ʃelluŋkaɭ
paʈajkaɭukku iʈajjeː n̪aːn innum aɾukil paːɾkkireːn
n̪ammuʈan paோɾiʈupaʋaɾkaɭaj n̪aːm kaொlla ʋeːɳʈum
inru paோɾin n̪aʈuʋaɾ manrat̪t̪il n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka
in̪t̪a t͡ʃamaʋeɭijil t̪iɾaɭum anajʋaɾum iɾat̪t̪am t͡ʃin̪t̪ijat̪il ʋaɭajn̪t̪uɭɭanaɾ
t̪iɾut̪iɾaːʂʈiɾanin paːʋa makanukkuk kiːɻppaʈit̪al
iʋʋaːru aɾd͡ʒunan ʋeːɳʈikkaொɳʈaːn oː paːɾat̪aː
puɾaʋalaɾkaɭukku iʈajjeː an̪t̪a paɾalaோka t̪eːɾ
at̪an paːlʋeɭɭaj kut̪iɾajkaɭaj kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪i piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːna kaːɾaj oːʈʈinaːɾ
piːʂmaɾ ʋaɻin̪aʈat̪t̪ija iʈam t̪uɾaோɳaɾ marrum aʋaɾkaɭin irajʋan
paːɾ aʋan aɾd͡ʒunaniʈam aʋaɾkaɭ n̪irkum iʈat̪t̪il
uŋkaɭ kuɾukkaɭin uraʋinaɾ marrum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ
oʋʋaொɾu kajjilum aʋaɾat̪u ʋiːʈʈin uraʋinaɾkaɭ kurikkappaʈʈuɭɭanaɾ
peːɾanmaːɾkaɭ marrum ajjaːkkaɭ maːmaːkkaɭ marrum t͡ʃakaோt̪aɾaɾkaɭ marrum makankaɭ
uraʋinaɾkaɭ marrum maɾumakankaɭ marrum maɾumakankaɭ kalappu
n̪aɳpaɾkaɭ marrum maɾijaːt̪ajkkuɾija peɾijaʋaɾkaɭuʈan t͡ʃilaɾ in̪t̪ap pakkam
t͡ʃilaɾ an̪t̪ap pakkam alajn̪t̪anaɾ marrum et̪iɾt̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭajk kaɳʈu
at̪t̪akajja kiʈ ʋaɭaɾn̪t̪a et̪iɾikaɭ  aɾd͡ʒunanin it̪ajam
iɾakkat̪t̪aːl uɾuki aʋaɾ it̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃaொllumpaோt̪u
aɾd͡ʒunaː
kiɾuʂɳaː n̪aːn paːɾkkireːn iŋkeː kaொʈʈuʋat̪arku ʋaː
aʋaɾkaɭin paொt̪uʋaːna iɾat̪t̪am eŋkaɭ uraʋinaɾkaɭin kuːʈʈam
en uruppukaɭ t̪aோlʋijaʈajkinrana en n̪aːkku en ʋaːjil ulaɾn̪t̪u paோkirat̪u
oɾu n̪aʈukkam en uʈalajjum en t̪alajmuʈijajjum t͡ʃiliɾkka ʋajkkirat̪u
t̪ikil kaொɳʈa muʈkaɭ en palaʋiːnamaːna kaj n̪aɻuʋalil iɾun̪t̪u
kaːɳʈiːʋ n̪alla ʋil oɾu kaːjt͡ʃt͡ʃal eɾikirat̪u
en t̪aோl ʋaraɳʈu paோkum n̪aːn n̪irka muʈijaːt̪u
enakkuɭ iɾukkum ujiɾ n̪iːn̪t̪i majakkam paோl t̪aோnrukirat̪u
ajjaோ marrum pulampalajk kaːppaːrra n̪aːn et̪ajjum et̪iɾpaːɾkkaʋillaj
it̪u n̪allat̪alla keːt͡ʃaʋ n̪allat̪alla
paɾaspaɾa paʈukaொlajjiliɾun̪t̪u eɻalaːm it̪aோ n̪aːn ʋerukkireːn
ʋerri marrum aːt̪ikkam t͡ʃelʋam marrum eɭimaj
it̪anaːl t͡ʃaோkamaːka ʋenraːɾ aːhaோ enna ʋerri
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi t̪aɾalaːm kaோʋin̪t̪aː enna paɳakkaːɾan keʈukkiraːn
laːpam iːʈʈalaːm enna ʋit̪i iːʈu enna iʈajʋeɭi
ʋaːɻkkajjeː inimajjaːkat̪ t̪eɾikirat̪u at̪t̪akajja iɾat̪t̪at̪t̪aːl ʋaːŋkappaʈʈat̪aː
iʋajkaɭ irappat̪arkut̪ t̪ajaːɾaːka n̪irpat̪ajk kaɳʈu
jaːɾuʈajja ʋaːɻkkaj n̪ijaːjamaːka iɾun̪t̪at̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːka iɾun̪t̪at̪u
meːlum t͡ʃakt̪i mat̪ippumikkat̪aːka ʋaɭaɾn̪t̪at̪u  peːɾankaɭ t͡ʃiɾeːʂʈaɾkaɭ marrum makankaɭ
t͡ʃakaோt̪aɾaɾkaɭ marrum maːmijaːɾ marrum maɾumakankaɭ
peɾijaʋaɾkaɭeː n̪aɳpaɾkaɭeː iʋarril n̪aːn maɾaɳat̪t̪aj et̪iɾkaொɭʋeːnaː
aʋaɾkaɭ n̪ammajk kaொlla murpaʈʈaːlum oɾu aʈi illaj
oː mat̪ut͡ʃuːt̪anan aːt̪aːjat̪t̪irkaːka n̪aːn ʋeːlajn̪irut̪t̪am t͡ʃejʋeːn
muːnru ulakaŋkaɭin aːʈt͡ʃi pinnaɾ eʋʋaɭaʋu kurajʋaːka
puːmikkuɾija ɾaːd͡ʒjat̪t̪ajk kajpparra iʋarrajk kaொlʋat̪u
inappeɾukkam t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum aːnaːl ʋeːt̪anajppaʈa ʋeːɳʈum kiɾuʂɳaː aʋaɾkaɭ iɾun̪t̪aːl
kurraʋaːɭikaɭ aʋaɾkaɭin maɾaɳat̪t̪aːl n̪aːm kurraʋaːɭikaɭaːka ʋaɭaɾʋaோm
n̪aːm kaொlʋaோmaːnaːl aʋaɾkaɭuʈajja paːʋaŋkaɭ n̪ammiːt̪u oɭiɾum
t̪iɾut̪iɾaːʂʈiɾanin an̪t̪a makankaɭum eŋkaɭ uraʋinaɾkaɭum
it̪anaːla enna amajt̪i kiʈajkkum maːt̪aʋaː
eːnenil kaːmat̪t̪aːlum kaோpat̪t̪aːlum kuɾuʈaːkkappaʈʈiɾun̪t̪aːl
iʋaɾkaɭaːl paːʋat̪t̪ajp paːɾkka muʈijaːt̪u allat̪u paːɾkka muʈijaːt̪u
t̪uːkki erijappaʈʈa marrum uraʋinaɾkaɭ kaொllappaʈʈa aɾat͡ʃaɾkaɭil
ippaʈippaʈʈa kurrat̪t̪ajp paːɾkkum n̪aːm eppaʈit̪ t̪aʋiɾkkakkuːʈaːt̪u
kurrat̪t̪aj uɳaɾn̪t̪u aʋamaːnat̪t̪aj uɳaɾum n̪aːm
oː n̪iː ʈilajʈ aːஃp men d͡ʒanaːɾt̪anaː
ʋiːʈukaɭ kaʋiɻppat̪aːl aɻijum
aʋaɾkaɭin inimajjaːna t̪aொʈaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna kuʈumpa pakt̪i
marrum t͡ʃaʈaŋkukaɭ purakkaɳikkappaʈʈana pakt̪i aɻin̪t̪uʋiʈʈat̪u
an̪t̪a ʋiːʈʈil t̪uɾaோkam n̪uɻajkirat̪u
at̪an peɳkaɭ peɳɳinri ʋaɭaɾkiraːɾkaɭ eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪a kaːlam
ʋerit̪t̪anamaːna uɳaɾʋukaɭum t͡ʃaːt̪ikaɭin kalappum
an̪t̪a kuʈumpat̪t̪aj n̪aɾaka paːt̪ajkku anuppi
paொllaːt̪a kaோpat̪t̪aːl at̪an aɻiʋajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪aʋan
illaj marrum maɾijaːt̪ajkkuɾija muːt̪aːt̪ajjaɾkaɭin aːnmaːkkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭin amajt̪ijaːna iʈat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋiːɻn̪t̪u ʋiʈuŋkaɭ
irut̪i t͡ʃaʈaŋku keːkkukaɭ marrum ʋaːn ʈet̪ʋaːʈʈaɾ#
enaʋeː n̪amat̪u punit̪ap paːʈalkaɭajk karruk kaொʈuŋkaɭ iʋʋaːru n̪aːm kaொnraːl
puːmikkuɾija t͡ʃakt̪ijaj n̪eːt͡ʃippat̪arkaːka uraʋinaɾkaɭ marrum n̪aɳpaɾkaɭ
ahaோʋat̪ at̪u enna oɾu maோt͡ʃamaːna t̪aʋaru
en uraʋinaɾkaɭ ʋeːlajn̪irut̪t̪am t͡ʃejt̪aːl at̪aj n̪aːn t͡ʃirappaːkak kaɾut̪ukireːn
aːjut̪am illaːmal aʋaɾkaɭaj et̪iɾkaொɭɭa en maːɾpakat̪t̪aj
t̪aɳʈu marrum iːʈʈikku pat̪il aʈijaj ʋiʈa
enaʋeː peːt͡ʃukajjil an̪t̪a iɾaɳʈu puɾaʋalaɾkaɭin mukat̪t̪il
aɾd͡ʒunan t̪an t̪eːɾ iɾukkajjil muːɻkinaːn
marrum ʋil marrum ampukaɭ ʋiɻaʈʈum it̪ajat̪t̪il uʈampu t͡ʃaɾijillaj
iŋkeː pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunʋiʂaːt̪ enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u aɾd͡ʒunanin t̪ujaɾat̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
aʋaɾ at̪t̪akajja iɾakkat̪t̪aːlum at̪t̪akajja t̪ukkat̪t̪aːlum n̪iɾappappaʈʈaːɾ
kaɳkaɭil kaɳɳiːɾ maŋki ʋiɾakt̪ijuʈan kaʈumajjaːna ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭil
ʈiɾajʋaɾ mat̪ut͡ʃuːt̪anan kuːrijat̪aːʋat̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
in̪t̪a palaʋiːnam unnaj eppaʈi aːʈkaொɳʈat̪u eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪aŋkaɭ
iɻiʋaːna piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃanaj t̪uɳit͡ʃt͡ʃalaːnaʋaɾkaɭukku aʋamaːnam
arat̪t̪in paːt̪ajjajt̪ t̪aʋiɾt̪t̪aː illaj aɾd͡ʒun
palaʋiːnat̪t̪irku unnajt̪ t̪aʈaj t͡ʃej at̪u t͡ʃeʋʋaːj
un paோɾʋiːɾan pejaɾ kaோɻaj paொɾut̪t̪at̪t̪aj t̪uːkki erijuŋkaɭ
eɻun̪t̪iɾu n̪iː n̪iːjaːka iɾu eɻun̪t̪iɾu un et̪iɾikaɭin kat͡ʃaj
aɾd͡ʒunaː
n̪aːn eppaʈi paோɾil t̪aɳʈukaɭaːl t͡ʃuʈa muʈijum
piːʂmaɾ miːt̪u allat̪u t̪uɾaோɳaɾ miːt̪u  oː t̪alajʋaneː
iɾuʋaɾum ʋaɻipaʈupaʋaɾkaɭaː iɾuʋaɾum kaௌɾaʋamaːna manit̪aɾkaɭaː
pit͡ʃt͡ʃajkkaːɾanin ɾaொʈʈijil ʋaːɻʋat̪u n̪allat̪u
n̪aːm ujiɾuʈan n̪eːt͡ʃippaʋaɾkaɭuʈan
paɾaʋalaːna ʋiɾun̪t̪ukaɭil aʋaɾkaɭin iɾat̪t̪at̪t̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃuʋajppat̪aj ʋiʈa
marrum kurra uɳaɾʋuʈan ujiɾ piɻajkka
aː at̪u maோt͡ʃamaːka iɾun̪t̪at̪aː  jaːɾukkut̪ t̪eɾijum
iŋkeː ʋikʈaɾ allat̪u ʋerri perraʋaɾ
aʋaɾkaɭ n̪ammaj kaோpamaːka et̪iɾkaொɳʈaːl
jaːɾuʈajja maɾaɳam ʋaːɻʋil at͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪aj eːrpaʈut̪t̪ukirat̪u
iɻan̪t̪a paɾit̪aːpat̪t̪il t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkaŋkaɭaːl t̪uːkki erijappaʈʈa
en eɳɳaŋkaɭ t̪it͡ʃajt̪iɾuppappaʈʈana
n̪aːn mikaʋum mat̪ikkum ʋaɻikaːʈʈijaːna uŋkaɭukku
n̪aːn karruk kaொɭɭa aːlaோt͡ʃanaj kuːralaːm
t̪ukkat̪t̪aj et̪u aːrrum enru enakkut̪ t̪eɾijaʋillaj
aːnmaːʋilum uɳaɾʋilum eɾin̪t̪at̪u
n̪aːn puːmijin t͡ʃaʋaːlarra t̪alajʋanaːka iɾun̪t̪aːl 
oɾu kaʈaʋuɭiʋaɾkaɭ aŋkiɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃenruʋiʈʈaːɾkaɭ
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
enaʋeː aɾd͡ʒunan it̪ajaŋkaɭin irajʋaniʈam t͡ʃaொnnaːn
meːlum peɾumuːt͡ʃt͡ʃu ʋiʈʈu n̪aːn t͡ʃaɳʈajjiʈa maːʈʈeːn appaோt̪u amajt̪i kaːt̪t̪aːɾ
jaːɾiʈam menmajjaːna punnakajjuʈan oː paɾat̪aː
iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ ʋiɾakt̪ijil aɻut̪u kaொɳʈiɾun̪t̪a paோt̪u ​​an̪t̪a puɾaʋalaɾkaɭin iɾumuraj
kiɾuʂɳaɾ t̪ejʋiːka ʋat͡ʃanat̪t̪il pat̪ilaɭit̪t̪aːɾ
kiɾuʂɳaː
t̪ukkam illaːt̪a iʈat̪t̪il n̪iː t̪ukkappaʈukiraːj n̪iː peːt͡ʃu
ɲaːnam illaːt̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ it̪ajat̪t̪il uɭɭa ɲaːnikaɭukku
ʋaːɻpaʋaɾkaɭukkaːkaʋum iran̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭukkaːkaʋum t̪ukkappaʈaːt̪iːɾkaɭ
n̪aːnaோ n̪iːjaோ iʋaɾkaɭil eʋaɾum illaj
eppaொɻut̪um iɾun̪t̪at̪illaj iɾukkappaோʋat̪umillaj
eppaொɻut̪um marrum enrenrum
ʋaːɻum anajt̪t̪um eppaோt̪um ʋaːɻkinrana manit̪anin t͡ʃaʈʈat̪t̪irku
kuɻan̪t̪aj paɾuʋamum iɭamajjum ʋajat̪um ʋaɾumpaோt̪u
enaʋeː aŋku ɾajt͡ʃiŋap marrum leːjiŋʈaʋun ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ
marra marrum pira ujiɾkaɭin iɾuppiʈaŋkaɭ
ariʋuɭɭaʋaɾkaɭ ariʋaːɾkaɭ pajappaʈa ʋeːɳʈaːm it̪u eɾit͡ʃt͡ʃaluːʈʈukirat̪u 
uŋkaɭ uɳaɾʋuʋaːɻkkaj kuːrukaɭukku t͡ʃiliɾppaːnat̪u
uŋkaɭukku ʋeppat̪t̪ajjum kuɭiɾajjum t̪ukkaŋkaɭajjum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajjum t̪aɾukirat̪u
it̪u t͡ʃuɾukkamaːnat̪u marrum maːrakkuːʈijat̪u paொrut̪t̪ukkaொɭɭuŋkaɭ iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
put̪t̪it͡ʃaːli kaɾaʈi paோla at͡ʃajjaːt̪a aːnmaː
ʋaluʋaːna marrum n̪ilajjaːna amajt̪i kaொɳʈa aːnmaː
t̪ukkat̪t̪ajjum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajjum alaʈt͡ʃijamaːka eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭkiraːɾ
aɻijaːt̪a ʋaːɻʋil ʋaːɻkiraːn at̪u
oɾupaோt̪um n̪irut̪t̪a muʈijaːt̪u illaːt̪at̪u
iɾukkaːt̪u iɾaɳʈin in̪t̪a uɳmajjajp paːɾkka
ʋipat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u piɾin̪t̪aʋaɾ aʋaɾkaɭaː
n̪iɻalil iɾun̪t̪u paொɾuɭ aɻijaːt̪a
n̪iː karrukkaொɭ ʋaːɻkkaj enpat̪u ellaːʋarrilum ʋaːɻkkajjajp paɾappuʋat̪u
at̪u eŋkum en̪t̪a ʋakajjilum muʈijaːt̪u
eppaʈijum kurajt̪t̪u t̪aŋkijiɾuŋkaɭ allat̪u maːruŋkaɭ
aːnaːl at̪u t̪eɾiʋikkum in̪t̪a ʋiɾajʋaːna piɾeːmkaɭukku
aːnmaːʋuʈan maɾaɳamarra muʈiʋarra ellajjarra
aʋaj aɻikinrana aʋaɾkaɭ aɻijaʈʈum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː marrum t͡ʃaɳʈaj
it̪aோ n̪aːn oɾu manit̪anajk kaொnruʋiʈʈeːn
it̪aோ n̪aːn kaொllappaʈʈuʋiʈʈeːn enru n̪inajppaʋan an̪t̪a iɾaɳʈum
onrum t̪eɾijaːt̪u ujiɾ kaொlla muʈijaːt̪u ujiɾ kaொllappaʈaʋillaj
aːʋi piran̪t̪at̪illaj aːʋi oɾupaோt̪um n̪ilajt̪t̪u n̪irkum
n̪eːɾamillaj at̪u illaj muʈiʋum aːɾampamum kanaʋukaɭ
pirappum irappum maːraːt̪at̪u enrenrum aːʋijaːkaʋeː uɭɭat̪u
maɾaɳam at̪ajt̪ t̪aொʈaʋeː illaj iran̪t̪uʋiʈʈat̪aːkat̪ t̪aோnrinaːlum
t͡ʃaோɾʋarra t̪annirajʋaːna at̪aj jaːɾ ariʋaːɾ
aɻijaːt̪at̪u aɻijaːt̪at̪uat̪t̪akajjat̪u
n̪aːn oɾu manit̪anajk kaொnreːnaː allat̪u kaொllat͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪eːnaː
illaj aːnaːl oɾuʋaɾ paʈukkumpaோt̪u
aʋaɾat̪u t̪eːjn̪t̪u paோna aːʈajkaɭ ʋilaki

enaʋeː aːʋijaːl ʋajkkirat̪u

marrum maɾapuɾimajkku t͡ʃelkirat̪u
put̪it̪aːka oɾu kuʈijiɾuppu
aːjut̪aŋkaɭ ujiɾaj aʈajjaːt̪u enru n̪aːn unakkut͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlkireːn
t͡ʃuʈaɾ at̪aj eɾikkaːt̪u n̪iːɾaːl aɳajkka muʈijaːt̪u
ʋaraɳʈa kaːrrum ʋaːʈuʋat̪illaj uːʈuɾuʋa muʈijaːt̪a
n̪uɻajjaːt̪a t̪aːkkappaʈaːt̪a paːt̪ippillaːt̪a t̪iːɳʈappaʈaːt̪a
aɻijaːt̪a anajt̪t̪u ʋaɾum n̪ilajjaːna urut̪i
kaɳɳukku t̪eɾijaːt̪a ʋiʋaɾikka muʈijaːt̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjaːl
marrum eɳɳarrat̪u eppaோt̪um t̪aːneː
iʋʋaːru aːnmaː ariʋikkappaʈʈat̪u n̪iː eppaʈi iɾuppaːj

eppaʈi manit̪an put̪it̪aːka iran̪t̪aːn enru keːʈʈaːl

at̪eː iɾukkum aːʋi  n̪iːŋkaɭ aɻuʋiːɾkaɭaː
pirappin muʈiʋu irappu maɾaɳat̪t̪in muʈiʋu
pirappu it̪u ʋit̪ikkappaʈʈat̪u n̪iː t̪ukkappaʈukiraːj
urut̪ijaːna kaɾat̪t̪in t̪alajʋaɾeː enna n̪aʈakkirat̪u enpat̪arkaːka
marrapaʈi et̪u n̪aʈakkaːt̪u pirappu
ujiɾinaŋkaɭ uɳaɾappaʈaːmal ʋaɾukinrana maɾaɳam
uɳaɾaːmal ʋaɾukirat̪u aʋarrukkiʈajjeː ujiɾinaŋkaɭ uɳaɾkinrana
anpuɭɭa iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː it̪il enna ʋaɾut̪t̪am iɾukkirat̪u
arput̪am aːʋaluʈan t͡ʃin̪t̪ikka

oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾukkum maːja keːʈʈal

t͡ʃat̪ajjin pan̪t̪aŋkaɭaːl t̪iːjaʋarrajjum n̪anmajjajjum eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɭkirat̪u
aʋan̪ampikkajjaோ makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaோ illaj
ɲaːnat̪t̪in t̪eɭiʋaːna aʈajjaːɭat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪aːŋkukirat̪u aʋaɾ ʋaɾajja ʋeːɳʈum
put̪t̪it͡ʃaːli aːmaj t̪anat̪u n̪aːnku aʈikaɭaj paːt̪ukaːppaːka iɻuppat̪u paோla
at̪an kaʋat͡ʃat̪t̪in kiːɻ aʋaɾat̪u ajn̪t̪u palaʋiːnamaːna uɳaɾʋukaɭ t̪iɾumpukinrana
ulakil iɾun̪t̪u aːʋijin kaொkkijin kiːɻ
ʋeːru et̪u aʋaɾkaɭajt̪ t̪aːkkum appaʈippaʈʈaʋaɾ en iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ɲaːnat̪t̪in mut̪t̪iɾaj uɭɭat̪u uɳaɾʋajt̪ t̪uːɳʈum ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ
t͡ʃujaɾaːd͡ʒjat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u ʋilaki iɾuŋkaɭ illaj at̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u
appaːl ʋaːɻpaʋaɾin pat͡ʃi
purappaʈuini eɻuppaʋillaj innum ʋaːjppu iɾukkalaːm
kun̪t̪ijin makaneː enru oɾu aːɭappaʈʈa manam
t͡ʃila n̪eːɾam pulanpujalkaɭ ʋiːt͡ʃuʋat̪ajjum t͡ʃaɳʈajjiʈuʋat̪ajjum uɳaɾa ʋeːɳʈum
ʋeːɾkaɭ muːlam ʋaluʋaːna t͡ʃuja kaʈʈuppaːʈu aʋan miːɳʈu ʋaɾaʈʈum
aʋaɾuʈajja ɾaːd͡ʒjam aʋan it̪aj ʋenru uʈkaːɾaʈʈum
en n̪aோkkat̪t̪il an̪t̪a manit̪an oɾuʋaneː put̪t̪it͡ʃaːli
t̪annajt̪ t̪aːneː aːɳit̪t̪aɾamaːka ʋajt̪t̪uk kaொɭpaʋan onru enraːl
uɳaɾʋin paொɾuɭkaɭajp parri t͡ʃin̪t̪ikkirat̪u aŋkeː n̪iːɾuːrrukaɭ
iːɾppu iːɾppiliɾun̪t̪u aːt͡ʃaj ʋaɭaɾkirat̪u
kaʈumajjaːna peːɾaːɾʋam peːɾaːɾʋam inaŋkaɭukku aːt͡ʃaj t̪iːppiɻampukaɭ
paொrupparra t̪anmaj pinnaɾ n̪inajʋu  anajt̪t̪um kaːʈʈik kaொʈukkappaʈʈat̪u 
unnat̪a n̪aோkkam t͡ʃellaʈʈum manat̪aj t͡ʃalanappaʈut̪t̪aʈʈum
n̪aோkkam manam marrum manit̪an anajt̪t̪um t͡ʃejaliɻakkum ʋaɾaj
aːnaːl oɾuʋaɾ uɳaɾʋin paொɾuɭkaɭajk kajjaːɭʋat̪u enraːl
n̪eːt͡ʃippat̪illaj marrum ʋerukkaʋillaj aʋarraj uɾuʋaːkkut̪al
aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃut̪an̪t̪iɾa aːnmaːʋukku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjuŋkaɭ at̪u amajt̪ijaːna aːɳʈaʋaɾeː
it̪aோ at̪t̪akajja manit̪an amajt̪ikku ʋaɾukiraːn
an̪t̪a amajt̪ijiliɾun̪t̪u eɻum
aʋaɾat̪u puːmikkuɾija ʋalikaɭin muʈiʋu marrum kuɳappaʈut̪t̪ut̪al
eːnenraːl aːnmaːʋaj aːɭappaʈum ʋiɾuppam amajt̪ijaʈajjat͡ʃ t͡ʃejkirat̪u
aːʈt͡ʃi t͡ʃejjappaʈaːt̪aʋaɾin aːnmaː aʋaɾuʈajjat̪u alla
t̪annajp parrija ariʋum illaj illaːt̪at̪u
amajt̪i eʋʋaːru ʋaɭaɾkirat̪u marrum at̪aj ʋiɾumpuʋat̪u
aʋaɾ makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaj eŋkiɾun̪t̪u et̪iɾpaːɾkka ʋeːɳʈum
manam
at̪u uɳaɾʋu n̪ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭajp pinparrat̪ t̪annajt̪ t̪aɾukirat̪u
at̪an ɲaːnat̪t̪in t̪alajmaj t̪uɳʈikkappaʈuʋat̪ajp paːɾkkirat̪u
meːlum t͡ʃuːraːʋaɭijin alajkaɭil oɾu kappal paோla oːʈʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃit̪ajʋu marrum maɾaɳam aʋaɾuʈan maʈʈumeː peɾija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ
jaːɾuʈajja pulankaɭ pulankaɭaːl at͡ʃajkkappaʈuʋat̪illaj 
t̪an t̪eːɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijajp perraʋanuʈan maʈʈumeː
muɻumajjaːna ɲaːnat̪t̪ajk kaːʈʈukirat̪u n̪aɭɭiɾaʋuiɾuɭ enraːl enna
ɲaːnam peraːt̪a aːnmaːkkaɭukku ʋiɻippu n̪aːɭ piɾakaːt͡ʃikkirat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u t̪eɭiʋaːna paːɾʋajkku ʋiɻit̪t̪iɾukkum n̪aːɭ paோl t̪eɾikirat̪u
arijaːmajjin aʈaɾn̪t̪a iɾaʋu iɾaʋu enru arijappaʈukirat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u uɳmajk kaɳkaɭukku appaʈippaʈʈaʋaɾt̪aːn punit̪aɾ
meːlum kaʈalajp paோla n̪aːɭukku n̪aːɭ perukirat̪u
ellaː n̪ilaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um ʋeɭɭam oɾupaோt̪um n̪iɾampi ʋaɻiʋat̪illaj
at̪an ellajk kaோʈu t̪aːʋaʋum illaj ʋeɭijeːraʋum illaj
aːrukaɭaːl uɳaʋaɭikkappaʈukirat̪u aːnaːl aʋajkaɭaːl peɾukaʋillaj
enaʋeː t͡ʃaɾijaːna onru aʋaɾat̪u aːnmaːʋin kaʈalukku
pulan ulakam t͡ʃuːnijat̪t̪in n̪iːɾaோʈajkaɭaj uːrrukirat̪u
aʋaɾkaɭ kaɳʈupiʈit̪t̪apaʈi aʋaɾaj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈʈu kalakkamillaːmal
aʋaɾkaɭin kaːɳikkaj eʈut̪t̪u aːnaːl miːt̪amuɭɭa kaʈal
aːm jaːɾaோ t͡ʃat̪aj n̪ukat̪t̪aj at͡ʃajkkiraːɾkaɭ
ʋaːɻkiraːɾ irajʋan ʋeːlajkkaːɾan alla aʋanat̪u it͡ʃt͡ʃajkaɭin ʋiʈut̪alaj t͡ʃej
peɾumajjiliɾun̪t̪u aːɾʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃuja paːʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u
amajt̪ijajt̪ t̪aொʈum piɾut̪ajjin makaneː
at̪uʋeː piɾammat̪t̪in n̪ilaj en̪t̪a at͡ʃt͡ʃamum illaj
an̪t̪a kaʈajt͡ʃi kaʈʈat̪t̪aj eʈʈumpaோt̪u aʋaɾ ʋiɾumpum iʈat̪t̪il ʋaːɻa
aʋaɾ irakkum paோt̪u ​​at̪u ellaːʋarriliɾun̪t̪um kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃelkirat̪u
n̪iɾʋaːɳat̪t̪aj aːt͡ʃiːɾʋat̪ikka kaʈaʋuɭkaɭuʈan aʈajt̪al
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
t͡ʃaːŋkjajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u kaோʈpaːʈukaɭin put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
ellaː manit̪aɾkaɭum paோrrum d͡ʒanaːɾt̪anaː
t̪ijaːnam enraːl unnat̪amaːna ʋiʂajam
t͡ʃejalaj ʋiʈa at̪anaːl peɾija keːt͡ʃaʋaː
in̪t̪a pajaŋkaɾamaːna t͡ʃaɳʈajkku ennajt̪ t̪uːɳʈukiraːjaː
ippaோt̪u un t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkap peːt͡ʃt͡ʃaːl n̪aːn kalaŋkiʋiʈʈeːn
enakku onru t͡ʃaொlluŋkaɭ n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːkat͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlluŋkaɭ
en̪t̪a ʋaɻijil n̪aːn t͡ʃiran̪t̪a muʈiʋajk kaɳʈupiʈippeːn
kiɾuʂɳaː
n̪aːn unniʈam t͡ʃaொnneːn kurramarra aːɳʈaʋaɾeː iɾaɳʈu paːt̪ajkaɭ iɾukkum
in̪t̪a ulakukkuk kaːʈʈappaʈʈat̪u iɾaɳʈu ɲaːnap paɭɭikaɭ
mut̪alil
ʋeːlajkaɭin ʋaɻijil t͡ʃeːmikkum t͡ʃaːŋkijaɾkaɭ
kaːɾaɳat̪t̪aːl paɾin̪t̪uɾajkkappaʈʈat̪u# aʈut̪t̪at̪u eːlam eʈukkum jaோk
t̪ijaːnat̪t̪in muːlam aːnmiːka ɾiːt̪ijil aʈajjuŋkaɭ
aːnaːlum iʋaj onrut̪aːn en̪t̪a manit̪anum t͡ʃejalil iɾun̪t̪u t̪appa muʈijaːt̪u
t͡ʃejalajt̪ t̪aʋiɾppat̪an muːlam illaj jaːɾum ʋaɾamaːʈʈaːɾkaɭ
muɻumajkkaːna ʋerum t̪uraʋukaɭaːl
illaj en̪t̪a n̪eːɾat̪t̪ilum en̪t̪a n̪eːɾamum illaj
en̪t̪a n̪aʈaʋaʈikkajjum illaːmal oːjʋeʈukkirat̪u aʋaɾat̪u ijarkajjin t͡ʃaʈʈam
ʋiɾumpaːʋiʈʈaːlum aʋaɾajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejalil iːʈupaʈut̪t̪ukirat̪u
t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj enpat̪u aːʈampaɾamaːna t͡ʃejal amaɾn̪t̪iɾuppaʋaɾ
t͡ʃat̪ajjin anajt̪t̪u kaɾuʋikaɭajjum aʈakki
aːnaːlum aʋan t͡ʃejalarra it̪ajat̪t̪il aʋaɾkaɭajp parrijeː n̪inajt̪t̪uk kaொɳʈiɾun̪t̪aːn
t̪iramajjarra marrum kurramuɭɭa n̪ajaʋaɲt͡ʃakaɾaːka n̪aʈikkiraːɾ
aːnaːl ʋalimajjaːna uʈalukku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjum manat̪uʈan
t̪akut̪ijaːna ʋeːlajkkaːka t̪anat̪u maɾaɳa t͡ʃakt̪ikaɭaj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈukiraːɾ
aːt̪aːjam t̪eːʈaʋillaj aɾd͡ʒunaː at̪t̪akajja oɾu
maɾijaːt̪ajkkuɾijat̪u uŋkaɭukku ot̪ukkappaʈʈa paɳijajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejjuŋkaɭ
t͡ʃummaː iɾuppat̪aj ʋiʈa ʋeːlaj t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
uʈalin ujiɾ t̪aொʈaɾkirat̪u ʋeːlaj illaːt̪at̪u
t͡ʃejja punit̪amaːna oɾu paɳi uɭɭat̪u
ulakap piɳajppu uɻajppajp paோlallaːmal at̪u piɳajkkaːt̪u
uɳmajjuɭɭa aːnmaː at̪t̪akajja puːmikkuɾija kaʈamaj t͡ʃejja
aːt͡ʃajjiliɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈuŋkaɭ n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃirappaːka t͡ʃejalpaʈuʋiːɾkaɭ
uŋkaɭ paɾalaோka n̪aோkkam piɾad͡ʒaːpat̪i peːt͡ʃinaːɾ 
aːɾampat̪t̪il ellaː manit̪aɾkaɭum paʈajkkappaʈʈapaோt̪u
meːlum manit̪akulat̪t̪uʈan t̪ijaːkam it̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃej
ʋeːlaj t̪ijaːkam at̪ikaɾikkaʋum peɾukkaʋum
t̪ijaːkat̪t̪uʈan it̪u kamat̪uk
uŋkaɭ n̪irajja maːʈu t̪an paːlaj t̪iɾuppik kaொʈukkirat̪u
anajt̪t̪u mikut̪ijaːka at̪an muːlam t̪ejʋaŋkaɭaj ʋaɻipaʈuŋkaɭ
t̪ejʋaŋkaɭ unakku aɾuɭum n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋiɾumpum an̪t̪a irajt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ
kaʈaʋuʈkaɭ uɻajppukku paɳam kaொʈukkumpaோt̪u kaொʈuppaːɾkaɭ
palipiːʈat̪t̪il t̪at͡ʃamapaːkamt͡ʃuʈaɾ aːnaːl oɾuʋaɾ t͡ʃaːppiʈʈaːl
puːmijin paɻaŋkaɭ anpaːna t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪irku ʋaɻaŋkukinrana
uɻajppukku paɾit͡ʃu illaj an̪t̪a t̪iɾuʈan aʋanat̪u ulakat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u t̪iɾuʈukiraːn
t̪aŋkaɭ t̪ijaːkat̪t̪irkup piraku uɳaʋaj uɳpaʋaɾkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ t̪aʋaru ʋiʈʈu aːnaːl aʋaɾkaɭ oɾu ʋiɾun̪t̪u paɾappinaɾ
ellaːm t̪aŋkaɭukkaːka paːʋat̪t̪aj uɳɳuŋkaɭ paːʋat̪t̪aj kuʈijuŋkaɭ
uɳaʋaːl ujiɾ ʋaːɻkirat̪u uɳaʋu maɻajjiliɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u
puɳɳija t̪ijaːkat̪t̪aːl maɻaj ʋaɾum
meːlum t̪ijaːkam uɻajppin t̪at͡ʃamapaːkam t͡ʃelut̪t̪appaʈukirat̪u
iʋʋaːru t͡ʃejal onraːna piɾammaːʋin t͡ʃejalaːkum
oɾeː anajt̪t̪u ʋijaːpit̪t̪uɭɭa ellaː n̪eːɾaŋkaɭilum
jaːkat̪t̪il munnilaj ot̪uŋkijiɾuppaʋaɾ
in̪t̪a maːpeɾum ulakin uɾuɭum t͡ʃakkaɾaŋkaɭukku ut̪aʋa
t̪anat̪u t͡ʃejalarra uɳaɾʋaj uriɲt͡ʃi iɻan̪t̪a ʋaːɻkkajjaj ʋaːɻkiraːɾ
ʋeʈkakkeːʈaːna marrum ʋiːɳ t̪anakkaːka iɾuppat̪u
t͡ʃuja kaʋanam t̪anakkut̪t̪aːneː t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejt̪al
aʋanukku et̪ilum paŋku illaj et̪uʋum aʈajjaʋillaj
en̪t̪at͡ʃ t͡ʃejalum t͡ʃejjaːt̪at̪um aʋanajt̪ t̪aொʈaːt̪u n̪ampikkaj illaj
puːmijil uɭɭa anajt̪t̪u ujiɾinaŋkaɭukkum ut̪aʋijaːka iɾukkum
aʋaɾaj t͡ʃaːɾn̪t̪at̪u# enaʋeː uŋkaɭ paɳi paɾin̪t̪uɾajkkappaʈʈat̪u
iɳajkkappaʈaːt̪a aːʋijuʈan makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijuʈan t͡ʃejalpaʈuŋkaɭ
t͡ʃaːt̪aːɾaɳa kaʈamaj manit̪anin t͡ʃejalt̪iranil iɾun̪t̪u
aʋaɾat̪u ujaɾn̪t̪a peːɾinpat̪t̪irku eːrraːɾ ʋeːlajkaɭaːl maʈʈumeː
d͡ʒanak marrum paɻaŋkaːla t̪uraʋikaɭ paːkkijam aʈajn̪t̪anaɾ
meːlum uŋkaɭ ʋakajjaj n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪uʋat̪arkaːka
n̪iːŋkaɭ eːrrukkaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈija t͡ʃejal put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlikaɭ et̪ajt̪ t̪eːɾn̪t̪eʈuppaːɾkaɭ
ɲaːnamarra makkaɭ eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭkiraːɾkaɭ t͡ʃiran̪t̪a aːɳkaɭ enna t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
kuːʈʈam t̪aொʈaɾum ennajp paːɾ
piɾut̪ajjin makaneː muːnru paɾan̪t̪a ulakaŋkaɭil
n̪aːn en̪t̪a uɻajppukkum ujaɾat̪t̪irkum kaʈʈuppaʈaʋillaj
aɭaʋiʈa kaːt̪t̪iɾukkirat̪u pera en̪t̪a paɾit͡ʃum illaj
aːnaːlum n̪aːn iŋkeː n̪aʈikkireːn marrum n̪aːn t͡ʃejalpaʈaʋillaj enraːl
aːɾʋamuɭɭa marrum kaʋanat̪t̪uʈan  ennajp paːɾppaʋaɾkaɭ
ʋaɻikaːʈʈut̪alukkaːka miːɳʈum t͡ʃaோmpeːrit̪t̪anat̪t̪il muːɻkuʋat̪u
n̪aːn t̪uːŋkijat̪aːl n̪allat̪aj ʋiʈʈu ʋilakuʋeːn
n̪aːn puːmijin oɻuŋkaj uʈajt̪t̪u urut̪ijaɭikka ʋeːɳʈum
aʋaɭat̪u t͡ʃan̪t̪at̪i aɻijum paɾat̪aː
arijaːmal uɻajt̪t̪aːlum uɳaɾʋaோʈu maɳan̪t̪aːlum
enaʋeː ariʋaொɭi uɻajkkaʈʈum uɳaɾʋuʋiʈut̪alaj aːnaːl amajkka
ulaka ʋiʈut̪alajjajjum at̪an peːɾinpat̪t̪ajjum kaொɳʈuʋaɾa
an̪t̪a eɭija pisijaːna it̪ajaŋkaɭil ʋit̪ajkkaʋillaj
ʋiɾakt̪ijin ʋit̪aj aːm oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾum aʋaɾaʋaɾ paŋkajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejjaʈʈum
anajt̪t̪ilum aʋaɾ iɳajkkappaʈaːt̪a aːnmaːʋuʈan t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum
ellaːmeː ijarkajjaːl ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum uɭɭana
kuɳaŋkaɭin t̪aொʈaɾpukaɭil
t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː eːmaːrrikkaொɳʈa muʈʈaːɭ it̪aj n̪aːn t͡ʃejt̪eːn enru n̪inajkkiraːn
meːlum n̪aːn t͡ʃejt̪eːn aːnaːlaː ʋalimajjaːna aːjut̪am kaொɳʈa iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
t͡ʃiran̪t̪a paːʈam perra manam n̪aːʈakat̪t̪aj arin̪t̪aʋaɾ
pulan ulakil kaːɳakkuːʈija ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ
meːlum kuɳaŋkaɭ eʋʋaːru t̪akut̪i pera ʋeːɳʈum
t̪an t͡ʃejalkaɭil iɾun̪t̪um ot̪uŋki n̪irkiraːn it̪u karpikkappaʈaʋillaj
ijarkajjin ʋaɻijaj arijaːmal aʋaɾkaɭuʈan kalan̪t̪u ʋaːɻuŋkaɭ
arijaːmalum met̪uʋaːkaʋum man̪t̪amaːkaʋum ujaɾn̪t̪a n̪aோkkaŋkaɭ
aʋajkaɭ unnaj iʈaralaʈajjat͡ʃ t͡ʃejjum
aːnaːl en paொɾuʈʈu unat̪u kaʈamajkaɭ anajt̪t̪um n̪irajʋeːrrappaʈukinrana
t̪ijaːnat̪t̪aj uɭn̪aோkki majjamaːkak kaொɳʈu
laːpam t̪eːʈaːmal t̪iɾupt̪ijaːka amajt̪ijaːka
piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃinajjaj kaʋanikkaːmal  t͡ʃaɳʈaj aʋaɾkaɭ ʋajt̪t̪iɾukka ʋeːɳʈum
enat̪u kaʈʈaɭaj iʋʋaːru ɲaːnamuɭɭa marrum ʋiɾuppamuɭɭa it̪ajaŋkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭin t͡ʃejalkaɭin anajt̪t̪u piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃinajkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um ʋilakuŋkaɭ
aːnaːl en kaʈʈaɭajjaj alaʈt͡ʃijam t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭ
t̪aŋkaɭukkut̪ t̪eɾijum et̪uʋum t̪eɾijaːt̪u n̪aʂʈat̪t̪il ʋiɻum enru n̪inajt̪t̪u
kuɻappam marrum muʈʈaːɭ t͡ʃuːt̪ ariʋurut̪t̪appaʈʈaʋaɾ
aʋaɾat̪u ʋakajjaːna ʈaோt̪ aʋaɾukku mikaʋum paொɾun̪t̪uʋat̪ajp pinparrukiraːɾ
meːlum aʋarrin ʋakajjilaːna t̪aːɻn̪t̪a ujiɾinaŋkaɭ ʋiːɳ
t͡ʃaʈʈat̪t̪ajp peruŋkaɭ at̪u iɾukka ʋeːɳʈum
uɳaɾʋin paொɾuɭkaɭ uɳaɾʋajk kiɭariʋiʈum
ʋiɾumpuʋat̪u marrum ʋiɾumpaːt̪at̪u innum ariʋaொɭi perra manit̪an
et̪iɾikaɭaj arin̪t̪um iʋaɾkaɭukku aʈipaɳiʋat̪illaj
irut̪ijaːka it̪u t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u at̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪u n̪allat̪u
aʋaɾ t̪aோlʋijaʈajn̪t̪aːlum aʋaɾaʋaɾ paɳijaj
t̪anakkut͡ʃ t͡ʃaொn̪t̪amaːna paɳikaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejjaːmal aʋaj n̪anraːkat̪ t̪aோnrinaːlum aʋarraj eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭʋat̪aj ʋiʈa
kaʈamajjajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪u irappat̪u n̪aோjalla
aːnaːl ʋeːru ʋaɻikaɭajt̪ t̪eːʈupaʋaɾ innum alajn̪t̪u t̪iɾiʋaːɾ
aɾd͡ʒunaː
innum t͡ʃaொlluŋka ʈiːt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾ en̪t̪a t͡ʃakt̪ijaːl manit̪an t͡ʃejkiraːn
aʋanuʈajja uʈampu paோka ʋiɾuppamillaːmal onru paோla
aʋaɾaj an̪t̪a t̪iːja paːt̪ajjil t̪aɭɭijat̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
kaːmaː at̪u
peːɾaːɾʋam at̪u iɾuɭil piran̪t̪aʋaɾ
et̪u aʋanajt̪ t̪aɭɭukirat̪u pat͡ʃijin ʋalimaj
paːʋam ʋalimajjaːnat̪umanit̪anin et̪iɾi
ʋeɭɭaj n̪eɾuppaj pukaj aɻippat̪u paோla oʈʈikkaொɳʈiɾukkum t̪uɾu paோla
t͡ʃeʋʋaːj piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːna kaɳɳaːʈi kaɾuppaj t͡ʃuːɻn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
pirakkaːt̪a kuɻan̪t̪aj ʋiʂajaŋkaɭin ulakamum appaʈit̪t̪aːn
in̪t̪a t͡ʃat̪aj aːt͡ʃajjil paʈaɾn̪t̪at̪u aɻukkaʈajn̪t̪at̪u muːʈappaʈʈat̪u
put̪t̪it͡ʃaːli ʋiɻum at̪il akappaʈʈu amajt̪ijarra et̪iɾi
it̪u ɲaːnam eɳɳarra ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭaj aɳin̪t̪u
n̪ijaːjamaːna aːnaːl ʋaɲt͡ʃakamaːna t͡ʃuʈaɾ paோnra n̪uʈpamaːna
uɳaɾʋu manam marrum kaːɾaɳam  iʋaj kun̪t̪ijin makaneː
at̪arkaːka kaொɭɭajp paொɾuɭaː iʋarruʈan at̪an n̪aːʈakat̪t̪il
at̪u manit̪anaj ʋerit̪t̪anamaːkkukirat̪u eːmaːrrukirat̪u kuɾuʈaːkkukirat̪u
enaʋeː paɾat̪anin unnat̪ap piɭɭajjeː
un it̪ajat̪t̪aj aːɭa t͡ʃikkija uɳaɾʋajk kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪u
kat͡ʃappaːna menmajjaːna paːʋat̪t̪aj et̪iɾkkaʋum
ariʋum t̪iːɾppum aːm ulakam ʋalimajjaːnat̪u
aːnaːl et̪u at̪aj ʋalimajjaːnat̪aːkaʋum manat̪ajjum kaɳʈarikirat̪u
ʋaluʋaːna marrum anajt̪t̪u aːɭum aːnmaː ujaɾ
aːt̪alaːl unnat̪amaːna aːʈt͡ʃi t͡ʃejpaʋaɾaj uɳaɾn̪t̪u
aːnmaːʋin muɻu t͡ʃakt̪ijajjum uŋkaɭ t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a aːnmaːʋil t͡ʃelut̪t̪uŋkaɭ
t͡ʃaɳʈaj et̪iɾikaɭajjum t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkaŋkaɭajjum murijaʈi anpeː hiːɾaோ kaொllu
anpaːna ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil unnajt̪ t̪unpurut̪t̪uʋat̪u kaːʈʈik kaொʈuppat̪u
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
kaɾmajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u ʋeːlajjil n̪allaொɻukkat̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
in̪t̪a maɾaɳamillaː jaோkam in̪t̪a aːɻamaːna t͡ʃaŋkamam
n̪aːn ʋiʋasʋat̪a# oɭijin irajʋan
manuʋukku ʋiʋasʋat̪am kaொʈut̪t̪at̪u aʋaɾ
ikʂʋaːkuʋiʈam enaʋeː at̪aj ʋaɾikku kiːɻeː kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃenrat̪u
en aɾat͡ʃa ɾiʂikaɭ anajt̪t̪ilum pinnaɾ pala aːɳʈukaɭaːka
uɳmaj maŋki aɻin̪t̪at̪u unnat̪a iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ippaோt̪u miːɳʈum uŋkaɭukku ariʋikkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
in̪t̪a paɻaŋkaːlak kat̪aj in̪t̪a maɾmam ut͡ʃt͡ʃam
n̪aːn unnaj ʋaːkkaːɭaɾaːkaʋum n̪aɳpanaːkaʋum kaːɳkireːn
aɾd͡ʒunaː
uŋkaɭ pirappu anpeː in̪t̪a pirkaːla n̪aːʈkaɭil
marrum piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːna ʋiʋasʋat̪at̪t̪in mun̪t̪ajja n̪eːɾam
n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃaொlʋat̪aj n̪aːn eppaʈi puɾin̪t̪ukaொɭʋeːn
aːɾampat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪eː n̪aːnt̪aːn karruk kaொʈut̪t̪eːn
kiɾuʂɳaː
en pirappin put̪uppit̪t̪alkaɭaj panmaʈaŋku
iɾun̪t̪iɾukkiraːj aɾd͡ʒunaː marrum un piraʋikaɭ kuːʈa
aːnaːl ennuʈajjat̪u enakkut̪ t̪eɾijum unnuʈajjat̪u unakkut̪ t̪eɾijaːt̪u
unat̪u et̪iɾikaɭajk kaொnraʋaneː n̪aːn iɾun̪t̪aːlum
pirakkaːt̪a aɻijaːt̪a aɻijaːt̪a
ujiɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪irkum irajʋan kurajʋaːka illaj 
maːjaːʋaːl n̪aːn mut̪t̪iɾajjiʈum en man̪t̪iɾat̪t̪aːl
mit̪akkum ijarkaj ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil mut̪anmajjaːna paɾan̪t̪a
n̪aːn ʋaɾukireːn t͡ʃelkireːn ʋaɾukireːn eppaோt̪u n̪iːt̪i
n̪iɾaːkaɾikkirat̪u oː paːɾat̪aː paோt̪u akkiɾamam
ʋalimajjaːnat̪u n̪aːn ʋajat̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋajat̪ukku ujaɾn̪t̪u eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭkireːn
t̪eɾijum ʋaʈiʋam marrum oɾu manit̪anaj aːɳkaɭuʈan n̪akaɾt̪t̪aʋum
n̪allat̪aj aːt̪aɾit̪t̪al t̪iːjaʋaɾkaɭaj mut̪ukil t̪aɭɭut̪al
miːɳʈum t̪an iɾukkajjil n̪allaொɻukkat̪t̪aj amajt̪t̪aːɭ
puːmijil en piraʋikaɭajt̪ t̪aொʈum uɳmajjaj jaːɾ ariʋaːɾkaɭ
en t̪ejʋiːka ʋeːlaj aʋaɾ t͡ʃat̪ajjaj ʋiʈʈu ʋeɭijeːrumpaோt̪u
at̪an t͡ʃumajjaj inimeːl eːrruʋat̪illaj kiːɻeː ʋiɻuʋat̪illaj
puːmikkuɾija pirappukku aʋaɾ enniʈam ʋaɾukiraːɾ anpeː iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ʋan̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ palaɾ pajat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈu
kaோpat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u aːt͡ʃajjiliɾun̪t̪u aʋaɾkaɭin it̪ajaŋkaɭaj ʋajt̪t̪u
en miːt̪u n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪appaʈʈa  en ʋit͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃi  t͡ʃut̪t̪ikaɾikkappaʈʈa
ariʋin punit̪at͡ʃ t͡ʃuʈaɾaːl iʋaj paோnraʋaj
en iɾuppuʈan kalakkaʋum jaːɾ ennaj ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾkaɭaோ
aʋaɾkaɭaj n̪aːn ujaɾt̪t̪ukireːn aːnaːl ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum ellaː manit̪aɾkaɭum
en paːt̪ajjil ʋiɻum iɾun̪t̪aːlum an̪t̪a aːt̪maːkkaɭ
t͡ʃejalkaɭukku ʋekumat̪i t̪eːʈum t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃej
ippaோt̪u ​​kiːɻ t̪ejʋaŋkaɭukku n̪aːn unakkut͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlkireːn
it̪aோ aʋaɾkaɭin ʋekumat̪i aːnaːl n̪aːn aʋaɾ
n̪aːnku t͡ʃaːt̪ikaɭaj uɾuʋaːkki aʋaɾkaɭukku oɾu iʈat̪t̪ajp piɾit̪t̪u kaொʈut̪t̪aːɾ
aʋaɾkaɭin kuɳaŋkaɭ marrum paɾit͡ʃukaɭukkup piraku aːm aj
uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈat̪u iɭajppaːrut̪al n̪aːn ʋaːɻkireːn
aɻijaːmal an̪t̪a maɾaɳap pirappukaɭ anajt̪t̪ajjum uɳʈaːkkijat̪u
paʈajppukaɭukku maɳ en t͡ʃaːɾam alla paʈajppukaɭaːka iɾuppat̪u
t͡ʃampan̪t̪amillaːmal t͡ʃejt̪eːn# n̪aːn ippaʈi n̪aʈikkireːnnu jaːɾukkut̪ t̪eɾijum
t͡ʃejalaːl piɳajkkappaʈaːt̪a t͡ʃejal aʋanaj piɳajkkaːt̪u
marrum mikaʋum uɳaɾn̪t̪u paɻajja anajt̪t̪u punit̪aɾkaɭ
uɻajt̪t̪aːɾ ʋiʈut̪alaj t̪eːʈi n̪iː ʋeːlaj t͡ʃej
kaʈan̪t̪a n̪aːʈkaɭil uŋkaɭ pit̪aːkkaɭ t͡ʃejt̪aːɾkaɭ
n̪iːŋkaɭ kuɻappat̪t̪uʈan t͡ʃaொlkiriːɾkaɭ it̪u munpeː keːʈkappaʈʈat̪u
paːʈakaɾkaɭaːlum ɲaːnikaɭaːlum t͡ʃejal enraːl enna
marrum enna t͡ʃejalarra t̪anmaj it̪aj n̪aːn unakkuk karpippeːn
meːlum t̪eɾin̪t̪ukaொɭʋat̪aːl en̪t̪a ʋeːlajjajt͡ʃ t͡ʃeːmippat̪u enpat̪aj n̪iːŋkaɭ karrukkaொɭʋiːɾkaɭ
t̪eːʋajkaɭ an̪t̪a muːnrajjum t͡ʃaɾijaːka t̪ijaːnikka ʋeːɳʈum
t͡ʃejʋat̪ut͡ʃejjaːmalmarrum t͡ʃejalt̪aʋiɾppat̪u iŋkeː
muɭɭum iɾuɭum n̪irajn̪t̪a paːt̪aj paːɾppaʋan
n̪aʈaʋaʈikkaj eppaʈi oːjʋu oːjʋu n̪aʈaʋaʈikkaj  aʋaɾ
put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anamaːna aʋaɾat̪u ʋakajjaːna mat̪t̪ijil aʋaɾiʈam uɳmaj iɾukkirat̪u
aʋaɾ n̪anraːka n̪aʈikkiraːɾ allat̪u oːjʋeʈukkiraːɾ ʋiʈuʋikkappaʈʈat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u anajt̪t̪u paʈajppukaɭilum aːt͡ʃajjin kut̪t̪alkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u
t͡ʃat̪t̪ijat̪t̪in ʋeɭɭaj n̪eɾuppaːl t͡ʃejalil t͡ʃut̪t̪amaːka eɾikkappaʈʈat̪u
ɲaːnikaɭ an̪t̪a manit̪anaj ɲaːni enru aɻajkkiraːɾkaɭ marrum at̪t̪akajja onru
t͡ʃejalkaɭin palanajt̪ t̪uran̪t̪u eppaோt̪um t̪iɾupt̪i
eppaொɻut̪um t͡ʃuja t̪iɾupt̪ijuʈan aʋaɾ ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejt̪aːl
aʋanuʈajja t̪ani aːnmaːʋaj karajpaʈut̪t̪um et̪ajjum t͡ʃejjaːt̪eː
et̪u  pajam marrum n̪ampikkajjaj ʋiʈʈu  t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː aʈakkik kaொɭʋat̪u 
ʋeɭippura t̪uːɳʈut̪alaj n̪iɾaːkaɾit̪t̪al  ʋiɭajt͡ʃt͡ʃal
uʈalukkut̪ t̪eːʋaj uʈalajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa ʋat͡ʃikkirat̪u
ellaː paːʋaŋkaɭukkum mat̪t̪ijil paːʋamarraʋaɾ t͡ʃamamaːna amajt̪ijuʈan
t̪ukkam at͡ʃajjaːmal eːrpaʈakkuːʈijat̪aj eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭʋat̪u
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːl at͡ʃajkkappaʈaːt̪a paொraːmajjinri at̪eː
n̪alla marrum t̪iːja at̪iɾʂʈat̪t̪il ippaோt̪u piɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
t͡ʃejalkaɭin piɳajppinaːl illaj aːnaːl at̪t̪akajja oɾuʋaɾin
jaːɾuʈajja aːt͡ʃaj paோjʋiʈʈat̪u jaːɾuʈajja aːnmaː ʋiʈut̪alajjaːnat̪u
eʋaɾuʈajja it̪ajam t͡ʃat̪t̪ijat̪t̪in miːt̪uat̪t̪akajja oɾuʋaɾuʈajjat̪u
aʋaɾ t͡ʃejjum ʋeːlaj t̪ijaːkat̪t̪in ʋeːlaj
it̪u murrilum t͡ʃaːmpal marrum pukajkkuɭ t͡ʃelkirat̪u
palipiːʈat̪t̪in miːt̪u n̪ukaɾappaʈum appuram ellaːm kaʈaʋuɭ
jaːkam enpat̪u piɾammam n̪ej marrum t̪aːnijam
piɾammam enraːl n̪eɾuppu piɾammam at̪u uɳɳum t͡ʃat̪aj
piɾammameː piɾammat̪t̪aj aʈajkiraːɾ
at̪t̪akajja aluʋalakat̪t̪il jaːɾ piɾammat̪t̪aj t̪ijaːnikkiraːɾkaɭ
t̪ejʋaŋkaɭukku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjum t͡ʃila ʋaːkkaːɭaɾkaɭ iɾukkiraːɾkaɭ
t͡ʃat̪aj marrum palipiːʈa pukajjuʈan aːnaːl marra t͡ʃila
jaːɾ n̪uʈpamaːna n̪eɾuppaj eːrri t̪uːjmajjaːna t͡ʃaʈaŋkajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
ʋaɻipaːʈʈin ʋiɾuppat̪t̪uʈan aʋarril aʋaj
jaːɾ kaɳʈat̪t̪in ʋeɭɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃuʈaɾil n̪ukaɾkinranaɾ
uɳaɾʋin makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi kaɳ marrum kaːt̪ukaɭin makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
menmajjaːna peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu marrum paːʈal olijaj kajʋiʈut̪al
meːlum t͡ʃat̪t̪ija d͡ʒaோt̪ijaːl n̪eɾuppaj muːʈʈupaʋaɾkaɭ
marajn̪t̪iɾukkum palipiːʈak kallil aːnan̪t̪at̪t̪aj eɾijuŋkaɭ
iɭamaj marrum kaːt̪al makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajt̪ t̪urat̪t̪al
aŋkeː t̪aŋkaɭ t͡ʃelʋat̪t̪ajk kaːɳikkajjaːkap paʈut̪t̪iɾuppaʋaɾkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭin t̪aʋam t̪ijaːnam pakt̪i
t͡ʃuɾuɭkaɭin urut̪ijaːna ʋaːt͡ʃippu aʋaɾkaɭin puɾaːɳam
n̪iːɳʈa t͡ʃikkana n̪aʈaʋaʈikkajkaɭaːl ʋeːt̪anajjuʈan perappaʈʈat̪u
maௌna t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭ
t͡ʃin̪t̪anajt͡ʃ t͡ʃuʈaɾaj uːʈʈa aʋaɾkaɭin muːt͡ʃt͡ʃaj iɻukkaʋum
meːlum it̪ajat̪t̪aj ujaɾt̪t̪uʋat̪arkaːka at̪aj t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃikkaʋum
oʋʋaொɾu n̪uɻajjum kaːrrin ʋenʈeːd͡ʒaj n̪iɾʋakikkirat̪u
aːnmaːʋukku ut̪aʋaːt̪a oɾu peɾumuːt͡ʃt͡ʃu ʋiʈakkuːʈaːt̪u
meːlum n̪aːɭukku n̪aːɭ t̪eːʋajkaɭaj maruppaʋaɾkaɭ
d͡ʒiːʋanajjeː palipiːʈat̪t̪in t͡ʃuʈaɾin meːl ʋajt̪t̪u
uʈalaj eɾit̪t̪al it̪aோ iʋaj anajt̪t̪um ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkinrana
aʋaɾkaɭ kaொnrat̪u paோl piɾat͡ʃaːt̪am ʋaɻaŋkum t͡ʃaʈaŋku
paːt̪ikkappaʈʈaʋaɾkaɭ marrum anajt̪t̪u at̪an muːlam peɾum paːʋat̪t̪aj aɻikkum
aːm marrum aɻijaːt̪a uɳaʋaj uɳpaʋaɾkaɭ
at̪t̪akajja t̪ijaːkat̪t̪aj ʋiʈʈu piɾammaː kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃella
muʈiʋillaːt̪at̪u aːnaːl at̪u aʋaɾukku
t̪ijaːkam illaj aʋaɾukku paŋku allat̪u paŋku illaj
t̪arpaோt̪ajja ulakil kuːʈa aʋaɾ eppaʈi pakiɾn̪t̪u kaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈum
innaொnru oː n̪iː kɭaோɾi aːஃp juʋaɾ lajn
piɾammaːʋin paːɾʋajjil in̪t̪a piɾat͡ʃaːt̪aŋkaɭ anajt̪t̪um
paɾaʋi eːrrukkaொɭɭappaʈukinrana puɾin̪t̪ukaொɭ
aʋaj anajt̪t̪um t͡ʃejalin muːlam t̪aொʈaɾkinrana it̪aj arin̪t̪at̪arkaːka
n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈuʋiːɾkaɭ t̪ijaːkam
t͡ʃiran̪t̪a paɾit͡ʃukaɭaj ʋiʈa en̪t̪a ariʋu t͡ʃelut̪t̪ukirat̪u
t͡ʃelʋat̪t̪aːl ʋaɻaŋkappaʈukirat̪u eːnenil paɾit͡ʃukaɭin mat̪ippu  oː en iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
kaொʈukkum manat̪il uɭɭat̪u t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjum ʋiɾuppam
meːlum iʋaj pajapakt̪ijaːl ʋaluʋaːna t̪eːʈalaːl perappaʈukinrana
uɳmajjajk kaːɳpaʋaɾkaɭin paɳiʋaːna kaʋanat̪t̪aːl
marrum karpikkaʋum uɳmajjaj arin̪t̪aːl uŋkaɭ it̪ajam ini illaj
piɻajjaːl ʋalikkum eːnenraːl uɳmaj kaːɳpikkum
n̪iː enakku aʈipaɳin̪t̪at̪u paோl anajt̪t̪um unakkeː aʈipaɳin̪t̪ana
meːlum paːɳʈuʋin makaneː n̪iːŋkaɭ maோt͡ʃamaːka iɾun̪t̪iːɾkaɭ
ellaː t̪aʋaru t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭiʈamum t͡ʃat̪t̪ijat̪t̪in in̪t̪a n̪ijaːjamaːna kappal
unnaj paːt̪ukaːppaːkaʋum kaʈal muɻuʋat̪um ʋaraɳʈat̪aːkaʋum t̪aːŋka ʋeːɳʈum
unat̪u miːralkaɭaːl eɾin̪t̪a t͡ʃuʈaɾ paோla
eɾipaொɾuɭaj t͡ʃaːmpalaːkkum ʋaɾaj uɳɳum
enaʋeː t͡ʃaːmpalukku aɾd͡ʒunaː onrum illaj
ariʋin t͡ʃuʈaɾ ʋeːlajkaɭaj ʋiːɳaːkkukirat̪u
it̪u paோnra t͡ʃut̪t̪ikaɾippu illaj
in̪t̪a ulakam muɻuʋat̪ilum at̪ajt̪ t̪eːʈupaʋaɾ
at̪ajkat͡ʃt͡ʃit̪amaːka ʋaɭaɾt̪t̪uaʋanukkuɭɭeːjeː kaɳʈupiʈippaːn
n̪ampikkaj aʋaɾ at̪aj aːnmaːʋin paோt̪u perukiraːɾ
t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː t̪eːɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi perru uɳmajjajp parrik kaொɳʈu ʋaɾum
ariʋajp perriɾut̪t̪al  ujaɾn̪t̪a amajt̪ikku
muɻumajjaːna oːjʋu aːnaːl karpikkappaʈaːt̪aʋaɾkaɭ
meːlum muɻu n̪ampikkaj illaːt̪aʋaɾkaɭum aɲt͡ʃupaʋaɾkaɭum
aʋaj ʂenʈ amajt̪i iŋkeː allat̪u ʋeːru eŋkum illaj
t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkam uɭɭaʋaɾkaɭukku n̪ampikkajjum illaj makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijum illaj
t̪annaʈakkam kaொɳʈaʋan t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkat̪t̪ajp paோkkinaːn
t̪annaj t͡ʃeːʋajjiliɾun̪t̪um aːnmaːʋaj t͡ʃejalkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um piɾit̪t̪al
ariʋaːɭi marrum ʋiʈut̪alaj en iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ʋeːlajkaɭ aʋaɾaj ini piʈikkaːt̪u pinnaɾ ʋeʈʈuŋkaɭ
ɲaːna ʋaːɭaːl paɾat̪a makaneː
in̪t̪a t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkam uŋkaɭ it̪ajat̪ t̪uʈippajk kaʈʈukirat̪u piɳajppaj murit̪t̪ukkaொɭ
un arijaːmajjaːl piran̪t̪aʋan t̪ajɾijamaːkaʋum put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlijaːkaʋum iɾuŋkaɭ
ennuʈan ʋajalukku unnajk kaொʈu eɻun̪t̪iɾu
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
ɲaːna jaோkam enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u ariʋu mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
aːnaːlum kiɾuʂɳaː oɾu t͡ʃamajam n̪iː paோrrukiraːj
ʋeːlajkaɭin at̪ikaɾippu marrum marraொɾu n̪eːɾat̪t̪il
ʋeːlaj muːlam t͡ʃeːʋaj iʋaj iɾaɳʈajjum t̪eɭiʋaːkak kuːrukinrana
et̪u t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ʋaɻi
kiɾuʂɳaː
ʋeːlajkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u n̪irut̪t̪a ʋeːɳʈum
n̪allat̪u paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪at̪t̪il ʋeːlajkaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪u
n̪anraːka iɾukkirat̪u marrum iɾaɳʈum peːɾinpat̪t̪aj ut͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪irku n̪aʈat̪t̪ukinrana
aːnaːl in̪t̪a iɾaɳʈilum t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ʋaɻi aʋaɾuʈajjat̪u
pakt̪ijuʈan ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ t̪aʈukkamaːʈʈaːɾ
at̪uʋeː uɳmajjaːna maruppaːɭaɾ urut̪ijaːna marrum n̪ilajjaːna
jaːɾ  et̪ajjum t̪eːʈuʋat̪u et̪ajjum n̪iɾaːkaɾippat̪u  aːt̪aːɾam ʋaːɻkirat̪u
et̪iɾkaɭukku et̪iɾaːka# oː ʋiːɾam mikka iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
t͡ʃejjumpaோt̪u ​​ellaːt͡ʃ t͡ʃejalkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um leːt͡ʃaːka uʈajkirat̪u
put̪ija ariɲaɾ aʋaɾkaɭ iɾuʋaɾaːkap peːt͡ʃukiraːɾ
in̪t̪a t͡ʃaːŋkijamum in̪t̪a jaோkamum ɲaːnikaɭukkut̪ t̪eɾijum
kaɳaʋanaːkija oɾuʋaɾ iɾuʋaɾil iɾun̪t̪um t̪aŋkak kanikaɭajp parippaːɾ
t͡ʃaːŋkijaɾkaɭ aʈajjum at̪ika oːjʋu pakut̪i
jaோkikaɭ aʈajkiraːɾkaɭ in̪t̪a iɾuʋaɾajjum onraːka jaːɾ paːɾkkiraːɾkaɭ
t̪eɭiʋaːna kaɳkaɭaːl paːɾkkirat̪u innum appaʈijaொɾu t͡ʃuɾukkam t̪alajʋaɾeː
at̪ika punit̪am illaːmal ʋerri peruʋat̪u kaʈinam
paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪at̪t̪il n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾuppaʋaɾ t͡ʃujamaːka aːɭappaʈupaʋaɾ
t̪uːja it̪ajam pulankaɭ marrum t͡ʃujat̪t̪in irajʋan
ellaː ujiɾkaɭin paொt̪uʋaːna ʋaːɻkkajjil t̪aொlajn̪t̪u paோnat̪u 
oɾu jaோkajukt̪  aʋaɾ oɾu t̪uraʋi
piɾammat̪t̪irku n̪eːɾaːka appaʈippaʈʈaʋaɾ t̪aொʈappaʈuʋat̪illaj
t͡ʃejalkaɭin kaɭaŋkat̪t̪aːl n̪aːn t͡ʃejjaʋillaj
iʋʋaːru aʋaɾ n̪inajppaːɾ  uɳmajkaɭin uɳmajjaj jaːɾ ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkiraːɾkaɭ 
paːɾt̪t̪al keːʈʈal t̪aொʈut̪al maɳam t͡ʃejt̪al eppoɻut̪u
aʋaɾ t͡ʃaːppiʈukiraːɾ allat̪u t͡ʃelkiraːɾ allat̪u t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃikkiraːɾ t̪uːkkam allat̪u peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu
ʋeːkamaːkap piʈikkirat̪u allat̪u t̪aɭaɾt̪t̪ukirat̪u kaɳkaɭajt̪ t̪irakkirat̪u allat̪u muːʈukirat̪u
eppaோt̪um urut̪ijuʈan it̪u in̪t̪iɾija ulaka n̪aːʈakaŋkaɭ
pulankaɭuʈan piɾammat̪t̪aj n̪inajt̪t̪u t͡ʃejalpaʈupaʋaɾ
t͡ʃejal uɭɭaʈakkat̪t̪uʈan t͡ʃejaliliɾun̪t̪u muʈiʋajp piɾit̪t̪al
pulan ulakam aʋan aːnmaːʋaj ini karajppaʈut̪t̪a muʈijaːt̪u
n̪iːɾajk kaːʈʈilum maːɾt̪ part͡ʃippi t̪aːmaɾaj ilaj
ʋaːɻkkajjaோʈu it̪ajat̪t̪aோʈu manat̪uʈanillaj ut̪aʋijaோʈu
anajt̪t̪u ajn̪t̪u pulankaɭilum  t͡ʃujat̪t̪aj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈut̪al 
jaோkikaɭ t̪aŋkaɭ aːnmaːʋin ʋiʈut̪alajkkaːka eppaோt̪um uɻajkkiraːɾkaɭ
it̪t̪akajja ʋaːkkaːɭaɾkaɭ t͡ʃejalkaɭin palanajt̪ t̪uran̪t̪u
muʈiʋillaːt̪a amajt̪ijajp peruŋkaɭ t͡ʃat̪t̪ijam t͡ʃejjaːt̪aʋaɾ uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃikku kaʈʈuppaʈʈaʋaɾ
ʋeːlajkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u oɾu palanajt̪ t̪eːʈuʋat̪u kiːɻeː piɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
uɾuʋaːna muniʋaɾ t̪anat̪u uɭɭat̪t̪il pinʋaːŋkinaːɾ
oʋʋaொɾu t͡ʃejalilum kaʈaʋuɭajp paோla uːɾil amaɾn̪t̪iɾukkiraːɾ
it̪il onpat̪u n̪uɻajʋaːjilkaɭ uɭɭana# et̪uʋum t͡ʃejjaʋillaj
en̪t̪a t͡ʃejalajjum eːrpaʈut̪t̪aʋum illaj iʋʋulakin irajʋan paʈajkkiraːn
ʋeːlajjaோ ʋeːlajjin miːt̪aːna aːɾʋamaோ illaj
ʋeːlajjin palan miːt̪u aːt͡ʃajjum illaj manit̪anin t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a t͡ʃujam
iʋajkaɭukkut̪ t̪aɭɭukirat̪u in̪t̪a ulakat̪t̪in maːsʈaɾ
n̪alla allat̪u t̪iːja t͡ʃejalkaɭajt̪ t̪aːneː eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɭkirat̪u
en̪t̪a manit̪anum  appaːl ʋat͡ʃikkum manit̪akulam iŋkeː t̪aʋaru t͡ʃejkirat̪u
muʈʈaːɭt̪anat̪t̪aːl ariʋaj iɾuʈʈaːkkukirat̪u aːnaːl jaːɾukkaːka
aːnmaːʋin iɾuɭ oɭijaːl t̪uɾat̪t̪appaʈukirat̪u
arput̪amaːna marrum t̪eɭiʋaːna piɾakaːt͡ʃaŋkaɭ uɳmajjaj ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪ukinrana
ɲaːna t͡ʃuːɾijan ut̪it̪t̪at̪ajp paோla
at̪an ʋiʈijalin kat̪iɾkaɭ aʋaɾ innum t̪ijaːnat̪t̪il iɾukkiraːɾ
aʋaɾajt̪ t̪eːʈi aʋaɾuʈan kalan̪t̪i aʋaɾil t̪aŋkijiɾun̪t̪aːɾ
oɭijuːʈʈappaʈʈa aːnmaːkkaɭ an̪t̪a ʋaɻijil t͡ʃelkinrana
en̪t̪at̪ t̪iɾuppamum illaːt̪a  aʋaɾkaɭuʈajja paːʋaŋkaɭ paran̪t̪upaோjina
n̪ampikkajjin palat̪t̪aːl in̪t̪a oɭi jaːɾukku iɾukkalaːm
at̪aj uɭɭaʋan paːɾkkiraːn ɲaːnamaːkap paːɾppaʋaniʈam
piɾaːmaɳaɾ t̪anat̪u t͡ʃuɾuɭkaɭ marrum punit̪aŋkaɭuʈan
maːʈu jaːnaj at͡ʃut̪t̪amaːna n̪aːj
aʋuʈkaːsʈ kaɾd͡ʒiŋ n̪aːjin irajt͡ʃt͡ʃi anajt̪t̪um onrut̪aːn
ulakam ʋenrat̪u  aːm iŋkeː kuːʈa
orrumajjin miːt̪u t̪aŋkaɭ n̪ampikkajjaj n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪upaʋaɾkaɭ
paːʋamillaːt̪a piɾammaː oɾumajjil ʋat͡ʃikkiraːɾ
meːlum aʋaɾkaɭ piɾammat̪t̪il at̪ika makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi aʈajja ʋeːɳʈaːm
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaj aʈajt̪al meːlum t͡ʃaோkamaːka iɾukka ʋeːɳʈaːm
t̪ukkat̪t̪aj et̪iɾkaொɳʈaːlum piɾammaːʋin miːt̪u t̪aŋkijiɾun̪t̪aːn
t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾum n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾukkaʈʈum muniʋaɾ jaːɾuʈajja aːnmaː
t̪anakkuɭɭeːjeː ʋeɭippura t̪aொʈaɾpukaɭiliɾun̪t̪u ʋilaki n̪irkirat̪u
peːɾinpam kaːɳkirat̪u piɾammaːʋiʈam pakt̪i t͡ʃeːɾn̪t̪at̪u
aʋaɾuʈajja aːʋi n̪it̪t̪ija amajt̪ijajt͡ʃ t͡ʃuʋajkkirat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ
in̪t̪iɾijaʋaːɻkkajjil iɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾum ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪aŋkaɭ kaɾppappajkaɭaj ʋiɾajʋupaʈut̪t̪ukinrana
en̪t̪a inam n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka t̪ukkaŋkaɭajt̪ t̪aɾum an̪t̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ t̪aொʈaŋki muʈiʋaʈajkinrana
kun̪t̪ijin makaneː put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anamaːna manam makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaʈajjaːt̪u
at̪u paோnraʋarril aːnaːl oɾu manit̪an karrukkaொɳʈaːl
aʋan ʋaːɻum paோt̪um t̪an uʈalin t͡ʃaŋkilijajt̪ t̪aːŋkijum
kaːmam marrum kaோpat̪t̪il t̪eːɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi pera aʋaɾ paːkkijat͡ʃaːli
aʋaɾ jukt̪aː aʋaɾukku makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi iɾukkirat̪u
manan̪irajʋu oɭi uɭɭeː aʋaɾat̪u ʋaːɻkkaj iɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
piɾammaːʋin ʋaːɻkkajjil aʋaɾ n̪iɾʋaːɳat̪t̪aj t̪aொʈukiraːɾ
iʋʋaːru ɾiʂikaɭ oːjʋeʈukkat͡ʃ t͡ʃelkinranaɾ aʋaɾkaɭ ʋat͡ʃikkiraːɾkaɭ
paːʋaŋkaɭ n̪iːkkappaʈʈu muʈiʋil t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkaŋkaɭuʈan it̪ajaŋkaɭuʈan
aːʈt͡ʃi marrum amajt̪i aʋaɾkaɭ ʋaːɻum ellaː n̪anmajkaɭilum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
kaʈaʋuɭin amajt̪ikku aɾukil marrum ʋaːɻum anajʋaɾum
peːɾaːt͡ʃaj marrum kaோpat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈu t̪aŋkaɭ n̪aːʈkaɭajk kaʈappaʋaɾkaɭ
t̪annajjum pulankaɭajjum aʈakki aːnmaːʋaj ariʋat̪u
t̪anat̪u amajt̪ijaːna aːnmaːʋirku ʋeɭijeː muːʈum punit̪aɾ
uɳaɾʋu anajt̪t̪u t̪aொʈut̪al muːlam t̪aொʈaɾpu ʋiʈaːmal
jaːɾuʈajja amajt̪ijaːna kaɳkaɭ n̪ilajjaːna puɾuʋaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u n̪eːɾaːkap paːɾkkinrana
jaːɾuʈajja ʋeɭippura muːt͡ʃt͡ʃu marrum uɭ muːt͡ʃt͡ʃu iɻukkappaʈukirat̪u
n̪aːt͡ʃijin ʋaɻijaːka t͡ʃamamaːkaʋum met̪uʋaːkaʋum at͡ʃajjaʋum muːʈaʋum
an̪t̪a onruuruppukaɭ it̪ajam marrum manat̪ajk kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪ukirat̪u
ʋiʈuʋippat̪il ʋaɭajn̪t̪u t̪aɭɭi ʋajt̪t̪uʋiʈʈu
peːɾaːɾʋam pajam aːt̪t̪iɾamippaோt̪u kuːʈa
eppaொɻut̪um eppaொɻut̪um ʋiʈut̪alaj perappaʈʈa ʋiʈut̪alaj
aːm eːnenraːl aʋaɾ jaːɾ enru ennaj arin̪t̪iɾukkiraːɾ
t̪ijaːkam marrum ʋaɻipaːʈu kaʈaʋuɭ ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪inaːɾ
meːlum eʋan t͡ʃeʋit͡ʃaːjkkaʋillajjaோ aʋan ulakaŋkaɭukku at̪ipat̪ijaːka iɾukkiraːn
ujiɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪ajjum n̪eːt͡ʃippaʋaɾ kaʈaʋuɭ ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪aːt̪aʋaɾ
it̪il jaːɾ ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪at̪t̪ajjum keːʈajat̪t̪ajjum kaɳʈupiʈippaːɾkaɭ
pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin  at̪t̪ijaːjam iŋkeː muʈikirat̪u
kaɾmat͡ʃanjaːt͡ʃajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u ʋeːlajkaɭin palanajt̪ t̪urappat̪an muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
enaʋeː jaːɾ t͡ʃejja t̪akut̪ijaːna ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejkiraːɾ
ʋeːlajjiliɾun̪t̪u aːt̪aːjam t̪eːʈaʋillaj an̪t̪a manit̪an iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
t͡ʃanjaːt͡ʃi marrum jaோki  iɾuʋaɾum onraː
meːlum aʋan t͡ʃuʈaɾaj eːrraːt̪aʋanum alla
t̪ijaːkam allat̪u paɳikku kajkaொʈukkaːt̪u
t͡ʃejjum uɳmajjaːna t̪uraʋi enru kaɾut̪uŋkaɭ
t̪urakkaːt̪aʋaɾkaɭukkaːka paɳijaːl ʋaɻipaʈuŋkaɭ
jaோkinaːka ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejjaːt̪u enaʋeː it̪u n̪anraːka t͡ʃaொllappaʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃejalkaɭaːl ʋaːkkaɭippaʋaɾ n̪ampikkajkku ujaɾkiraːɾ
meːlum punit̪at̪t̪uʋam enpat̪u ellaː ʋeːlajkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um n̪inruʋiʈuʋat̪u
eːnenil t͡ʃaɾijaːna jaோkan t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːn  aːnaːl t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːn
uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭaːl at͡ʃajkkappaʈaːmal t͡ʃejalkaɭaːl kaʈʈuppaʈaːt̪a
muʈiʋaj ot̪ukki ʋajt̪t̪al
oʋʋaொɾu manit̪anum ujaɾt̪t̪aʈʈum
aːnmaːʋaːl t͡ʃujam t̪an t͡ʃujat̪t̪aj mit̪ikkaːmal
t͡ʃujat̪t̪in n̪aɳpanaːka iɾukkum aːnmaː t͡ʃujat̪t̪in et̪iɾijaːka ʋaɭaɾakkuːʈum
t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː aːɭumpaோt̪u aːnmaː t͡ʃujat̪t̪in n̪aɳpan
aːnaːl aːnmaː t̪annajjeː et̪iɾijaːka maːrrukirat̪u
t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː ʋerukkirat̪u t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː alla#
irajjaːɳmaj aːnmaː
t͡ʃujaɾaːd͡ʒjamaːkaʋum amajt̪ijaːkaʋum ʋaːɻpaʋaɾ
t̪annaj majjappaʈut̪t̪i oɾeː maːt̪iɾijaːka eʈut̪t̪ukkaொɭkirat̪u
inpam marrum t̪unpam ʋeppam kuɭiɾ peɾumaj marrum aʋamaːnam
aʋaɾ jaோki aʋaɾ jukt̪aː makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
oɭi marrum uɳmajjin makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijuʈan piɾin̪t̪u ʋaːɻkirat̪u
oɾu ut͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪il pulankaɭ aʈipaɳin̪t̪u
maɳɳaːŋkaʈʈi paːraj minnum t̪aŋkam eŋkeː
anajt̪t̪ajjum onraːkak kaːʈʈu in̪t̪a aʈajjaːɭat̪t̪in muːlam aʋaɾ arijappaʈukiraːɾ
t̪aோɻaɾkaɭukkum n̪aɳpaɾkaɭukkum t͡ʃamamaːna kaɾuɳajjuʈan iɾut̪t̪al
ʋaːjppu ʋaɾupaʋaɾkaɭ an̪n̪ijaɾkaɭ kaːt̪alaɾkaɭ et̪iɾikaɭ
ʋeɭin̪aːʈʈinaɾ marrum uraʋinaɾkaɭ anajʋaɾajjum oɾeː maːt̪iɾijaːka n̪eːt͡ʃikkireːn
t̪iːmaj allat̪u n̪allat̪u
aʋaɾ uʈkaːɾa ʋeːɳʈumaː
urut̪ijaːna t̪ijaːnam t̪animaj
aʋanuʈajja eɳɳaŋkaɭ kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈana aʋanuʈajja uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ kajʋiʈappaʈʈana
uʈamajkaɭaj ʋiʈʈu ʋeɭijeːrut̪al oɾu n̪ijaːjamaːna amajt̪ijaːna iʈat̪t̪il
aʋanat̪u n̪ilajjaːna ʋat͡ʃippiʈat̪t̪ajk kaொɳʈiɾuppat̪u  at̪ikamaːka ujaɾt̪t̪appaʈaʋillaj
innum kurajʋaːka illaj  aʋaɾ t̪aŋkaʈʈum aʋaɾat̪u paொɾuʈkaɭ
oɾu t̪uɳi oɾu maːn t̪aோl marrum kut͡ʃaːpul
aŋku t̪i on miːt̪u t̪anat̪u manat̪ajk kaʈinamaːkkinaːn
it̪ajat̪t̪ajjum pulankaɭajjum aʈakki amajt̪ijaːka amajt̪ijaːka
aʋaɾ jaோkaːʋajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪u t͡ʃaːt̪ikkaʈʈum
aːnmaːʋin t̪uːjmaj at͡ʃajjaːt̪u ʋajt̪t̪iɾut̪t̪al
uʈal marrum kaɻut̪t̪u marrum t̪alaj aʋaɾat̪u paːɾʋaj uriɲt͡ʃappaʈʈat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u muːkku munajjil # t͡ʃurrilum iɾun̪t̪u ɾeːʈ
aːʋijil amajt̪i pajam illaːt̪a uɭn̪aோkkam
aʋaɾat̪u piɾammat͡ʃt͡ʃaɾija t͡ʃapat̪am miːt̪u pakt̪i
ennajp parrija t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj ennajp parrija t͡ʃin̪t̪anajjil t̪aொlajn̪t̪u paோnat̪u
an̪t̪a jaோd͡ʒin mikaʋum aɾppaɳippuɭɭa mikaʋum kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈa
appaːl amajt̪i ʋaɾumen amajt̪i amajt̪i
ujaɾn̪t̪a n̪iɾʋaːɳat̪t̪in
aːnaːl puːmikkuɾija t̪eːʋajkaɭukkaːka
at̪ika ʋiɾat̪am iɾuppaʋaɾ mat̪am alla
allat̪u at̪ika ʋiɾun̪t̪ukaɭ allat̪u t̪uːŋkupaʋaɾ
t͡ʃejalarra manam ʋiːɳaːka aɳin̪t̪aʋanum alla
ʋiɻippuɳaɾʋil aʋaɾat̪u palam illaj aɾd͡ʒunaː aɻajppu
uɳmajjaːna irajjat͡ʃt͡ʃam mikaʋum n̪iːkkukirat̪u
puːmi ʋalikaɭ marrum n̪aோjkaɭ aŋku oɾuʋaɾ mit̪amaːnaʋaɾ
t͡ʃaːppiʈuʋat̪ilum oːjʋeʈuppat̪ilum ʋiɭajjaːʈʈilum
aːt͡ʃaj marrum t͡ʃejalil aɭaʋiʈappaʈukirat̪u t͡ʃila n̪eːɾaŋkaɭil t̪uːŋkuʋat̪u

irukkamaːka kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈa  uɭn̪aːʈʈil t̪iːɳʈappaʈaːt̪a
uɳaɾʋin aɻut̪t̪at̪t̪aːl  aʋaɾ jukt̪aː paːɾ
urut̪ijaːna oɾu ʋiɭakku kaːrriliɾun̪t̪u marajn̪t̪u eɾikirat̪u
jaோkijin manam appaʈippaʈʈat̪u
pulan pujalkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u muːʈi paɾalaோkat̪t̪irku piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːka eɾikirat̪u
manam amajt̪ijaʈajjum paோt̪u ​​punit̪amaːna paɳpaːʈʈuʈan amajt̪ijaʈajkirat̪u
t͡ʃujam t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː t͡ʃin̪t̪ikkum paோt̪u
haːt̪ aːrut̪al at̪u pejaɾarra makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaj arijum paோt̪u
uɳaɾʋin anajt̪t̪u ellajkaɭukkum appaːl aːnmaːʋirku ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u 
aːnmaːʋukku maʈʈumeː marrum t̪eɾin̪t̪um at͡ʃajʋat̪illaj
t̪uːɾamaːna uɳmajkku uɳmaj it̪aj ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkum paோt̪u
it̪u ʋeːru en̪t̪a paொkkiʂat̪t̪ajjum oppiʈa muʈijaːt̪u
aːnaːl aŋku aʈajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪aːl at͡ʃajkkaʋaோ at͡ʃajkkaʋaோ muʈijaːt̪u
en̪t̪aʋaொɾu kaʈumajjaːna t̪ukkat̪t̪ilum an̪t̪a maːn̪ilat̪t̪aj amajt̪i enru aɻajkkaʋum
an̪t̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna piɾiʋinaj jaோkam an̪t̪a manit̪anaj aɻajkkaʋum
t͡ʃaɾijaːna jaோkan
urut̪ijuʈan ʋiɾuppam
mujart͡ʃikaɭ eɭit̪aːka muʈijum ʋaɾaj at̪arkaːka uɻajkka ʋeːɳʈum
meːlum t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj t͡ʃin̪t̪anajjiliɾun̪t̪u kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃenrat̪u n̪aʈuŋkukirat̪u
ellaː eːkkaŋkaɭum pukaɻ marrum aːt̪aːja kanaʋukaɭaːl ʋaɭaɾkkappaʈukinrana
pulankaɭin kat̪aʋukaɭaj muːʈuʋat̪u
kaɳkaːɳippu ʋaːɾʈuʈan enaʋeː paʈippaʈijaːka at̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u
amajt̪i marrum urut̪ijaːna it̪ajat̪t̪aj paɾit͡ʃaːka ʋaɻaŋka
manam t͡ʃujamaːkap paோɾt̪t̪appaʈʈu aːnmaː aʈajkaːkkum paோt̪u
t͡ʃikkalarra aːnaːl aʈikkaʈi it̪ajam
aʈikkaʈi kaʈʈuppaːʈʈil iɾun̪t̪u muriʋukaɭ  kaːʈʈu marrum alajt͡ʃt͡ʃal
aʋaɾ at̪aj miːɳʈum kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪aʈʈum miːɳʈum kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪aʈʈum
aːnmaːʋin aːɭukajkku t͡ʃaɾijaːna peːɾinpat̪t̪irkaːka
amajt̪ijaːna maːɾpil maʈʈumeː ʋaɭaɾum
aːʋi uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijarrat̪u kurrat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃut̪t̪appaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u
ellajjarrat̪u enru t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejt̪aːɾ iʋʋaːru t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ
aʋaɾat̪u aːnmaː paɾamaːt̪maːʋiʈam paːʋat̪t̪aj ʋiʈʈu
muʈiʋillaː aːnan̪t̪at̪t̪irku t̪aʈajjinri t͡ʃelkirat̪u
piɾammaːʋuʈanaːna ajkkijam aʋaɾ aʋʋaːru t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejt̪aːɾ
at̪anaːl kalan̪t̪at̪u ujiɾaːnmaː kuʈijiɾuppajp paːɾkkirat̪u
ellaː ujiɾkaɭilum ellaː ujiɾkaɭilum
at̪il ujiɾaːnmaː aʈaŋkijuɭɭat̪u marrum jaːɾaோ iʋʋaːru
ellaːʋarrilum ennajp pakut̪t̪arijum ennil uɭɭa anajt̪t̪ajjum
n̪aːn aʋanaj paோka ʋiʈaʋeː illaj allat̪u aʋaɾaj t̪aɭaɾt̪t̪aʋum illaj
ennajp piʈit̪t̪ukkaொɭ aːnaːl aʋaɾ eŋku ʋeːɳʈumaːnaːlum ʋat͡ʃikkalaːm
aʋanuʈajja ʋaːɻkkaj et̪uʋaːka iɾun̪t̪aːlum ennil aʋan ʋaːɻkiraːn ʋaːɻkiraːn
eːnenil aʋaɾ ʋaːt͡ʃamaːjiɾukkum ennaj arin̪t̪u ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾ
ʋaːɻum ellaːʋarrilum ellaːʋarrilum ennuʈan oʈʈikkaொɳʈiɾukkirat̪u
aɾd͡ʒunaː oɾu manit̪an ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum paːɾt̪t̪aːl 
aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a uɾuʋakat̪t̪aːl karpikkappaʈʈat̪u  oɾu ʋaːɻkkaj
t̪iːmajjilum n̪anmajjilum oɾu t͡ʃaːɾam
aʋaɾaj oɾu jaோkijajp piʈit̪t̪uk kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ aːm n̪anku puːɾaɳamaːnat̪u
aɾd͡ʒunaː
mat̪uʋajk kaொnraʋan miːɳʈum in̪t̪a jaோkam
in̪t̪a amajt̪i t͡ʃaman̪ilajjiliɾun̪t̪u perappaʈʈat̪u
unnaːl arijappaʈʈat̪u  n̪aːn en̪t̪a n̪ilajjajjum kaːɳaʋillaj
at̪il oːjʋu illaj eːnenraːl manit̪aɾkaɭin it̪ajam
t͡ʃaɾijillaj kiɾuʂɳaː t͡ʃaொri kaொn̪t̪aɭippu
ʋiɾuppamum ʋalimajjum kaொɳʈaʋaɾ it̪u ellaːm onru n̪aːn n̪inajkkireːn

kiɾuʂɳaː
n̪iːɳʈa kaɾam kaொɳʈa ʋiːɾaneː maruppirku appaːl kaʈinamaːnat̪u
manit̪anin it̪ajam aʈakkuʋat̪um alajʋat̪um aːkum
innum at̪u paɻakkat̪t̪aːl kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈaʈʈum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
t͡ʃuja kaʈʈaɭajjin muːlam in̪t̪a jaோkam n̪aːn t͡ʃaொlkireːn
aːɭappaʈaːt̪aʋaɾkaɭiʈam ilakuʋaːka ʋaɾuʋat̪illaj
aːnaːl aʋaɾ t̪anakku ed͡ʒamaːnaɾaːka iɾuppaːɾ
aʋaɾ urut̪ijaːka paːʈupaʈʈaːl ʋerri peruʋaːɾ
aɾd͡ʒunaː
n̪ampikkaj kaொɳʈaʋan enna ʋaɻijil t͡ʃelkiraːn
t̪aோlʋi kiɾuʂɳaː mujart͡ʃijil miːɳʈum ʋiɻukirat̪u
paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪at̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃaɾijaːna ʋit̪ijaj kaːɳaʋillajjaː
aʋaɾ piɾammaːʋin oɭijiliɾun̪t̪u ʋilaki t̪aொlajn̪t̪u paோkaʋillajjaː
puːmijilum ʋaːnat̪t̪ilum mit̪akkum ʋiːɳaːna meːkam paோla
minnal at̪aj piɭakkumpaோt̪u ​​at̪u marajn̪t̪uʋiʈum
iŋkeː enakku n̪iːŋkaɭ pat̪ilaɭippat̪aj n̪aːn keːʈpeːn
mut̪al kiɾuʂɳaː uŋkaɭaːl t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkat̪t̪aj t̪iːɾkka jaːɾaːlum muʈijaːt̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
aʋaɾ t̪aொlajn̪t̪u paோkaʋillaj piɾut̪ajjin makaneː illaj
puːmijaோ t͡ʃaொɾkkamaோ aʋanukkaːkaʋum parikkappaʈuʋat̪illaj
eːnenraːl oɾu t͡ʃaɾijaːna aːt͡ʃajjaj ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkum it̪ajam illaj
iɻappin paːt̪ajjil t͡ʃelkirat̪u t̪aோlʋi aʈajja ʋeːɳʈijaʋan
n̪iːt̪ijaj ʋiɾumpi maɾaɳat̪t̪il ʋaɾum
n̪iːt̪imaːnkaɭin piɾaːn̪t̪ijat̪t̪irku aŋku ʋat͡ʃikkiraːɾ
aɭaʋiʈa muʈijaːt̪a aːɳʈukaɭ put̪it̪aːkap pirappat̪u
t͡ʃila n̪ijaːjamaːna ʋiːʈʈil miːɳʈum ʋaːɻkkaj t̪aொʈaŋkukirat̪u
leːt͡ʃaːna marrum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikku mat̪t̪ijil ʋaːjppu iɾukkalaːm
aʋaɾ oɾu jaோkinin ʋiːʈʈirkuɭ iraŋkukiraːɾ
arat̪t̪in maːɾpil aːnaːl at̪u aɾit̪u at̪t̪akajja pirappu
in̪t̪a puːmijil kiʈajppat̪u kaʈinam t̪alajʋaɾeː
enaʋeː aʋaɾ it̪ajat̪t̪in ujaɾaŋkaɭaj miːɳʈum t̪iɾumpap perruɭɭaːɾ
aʋaɾ t͡ʃaːt̪it̪t̪aːɾ at̪anaːl aʋaɾ put̪it̪aːka paːʈupaʈukiraːɾ
muɻumajkku t͡ʃiran̪t̪a n̪ampikkajjuʈan anpuɭɭa iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
eːnenraːl paɻajja aːt͡ʃajjaːl aʋan iɻukkappaʈukiraːn
arijaːmal marrum aːt͡ʃajkku maʈʈumeː
jaோkat̪t̪in t̪uːjmaj kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃelʋat̪aːkum
t͡ʃapt̪apiɾammat̪t̪irku appaːl peːt͡ʃappaʈum ʋeːt̪am
aːnaːl jaோkijaːka iɾun̪t̪u ʋaluʋaːkaʋum n̪iːɳʈa kaːlamaːkaʋum mujart͡ʃi t͡ʃejkiraːɾ
miːralkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃut̪t̪ikaɾikkappaʈʈat̪u pirappaːl puːɾaɳappaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u
pirappajt̪ t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u kaʈajt͡ʃijaːka aʋaɾ kaːlkaɭaj n̪aʈum
t̪aொlajʋaːna paːt̪ajjil oɾu t̪aɾaʋaɾit͡ʃaj paோnraʋaj
t̪uraʋikaɭukku meːl ɲaːnikaɭaj ʋiʈa ujaɾn̪t̪aʋaɾ
paɾan̪t̪a t͡ʃejalkaɭin t͡ʃaːt̪anajjaːɭaɾkaɭukku appaːl n̪iːjaːka iɾu
jaோki aɾd͡ʒunaː at̪t̪akajja n̪ampikkajjil
ennaj ʋaɳaŋkupaʋaɾeː uɳmajjaːnaʋaɾ marrum t͡ʃiran̪t̪aʋaɾ
uɭɭat̪t̪uʈan enat̪u maɾmat̪t̪il t̪aŋkijiɾun̪t̪eːn
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
aːt̪maːt͡ʃanjamajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u t͡ʃuja kaʈʈuppaːʈu muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam
at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
ippaோt̪u karrukkaொɭɭuŋkaɭ anpeː iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː uŋkaɭ aːnmaː n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾun̪t̪aːl eppaʈi
eppaொɻut̪um en miːt̪uinnum jaோk uʈarpajirt͡ʃi t͡ʃejkireːn
innum ennaj unat̪u aʈajkkalamaːkkik kaொɳʈiɾukkiraːj  n̪iː ʋaː
n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka ennaj muɻumajjaːkap piʈit̪t̪uk kaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈum
an̪t̪a unnat̪amaːna ɲaːnat̪t̪aj n̪aːn unakku ariʋikkireːn
muɻu marrum kurippaːka it̪u n̪iːŋkaɭ arin̪t̪aːl
iʋʋulakil t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa et̪uʋum illaj
pala aːjiɾam manit̪aɾkaɭil onru onru
t͡ʃat̪t̪ijat̪t̪irkaːka paːʈupaʈuŋkaɭ marrum paːʈupaʈum t͡ʃilaɾil
illaj meːlum ujaɾaʋum  onru maʈʈum  iŋkeːjum aŋkeːjum 
ennajp paோlaʋeː uɳmajjaːkaʋeː ennaj ariʋeːn
puːmi n̪iːɾ t͡ʃuʈaɾ kaːrru iːt̪aɾ ujiɾ marrum manam
marrum t̪anit̪t̪uʋam  an̪t̪a eʈʈu
ennaj meːniஃpesʈ kaːʈt͡ʃijaj uɾuʋaːkkaʋum
iʋaj en kiːɻ ijalpu ujaɾn̪t̪at̪ajk karrukkaொɭ
at̪anaːleːjeː n̪iː ʋiːɾan in̪t̪a piɾapaɲt͡ʃam
at̪an ʋaːɻkkajk kaொɭkajjaːl urpat̪t̪i t͡ʃejjappaʈukirat̪u
at̪an muːlam t̪eɾijum ʋiʂajaŋkaɭin ulakaŋkaɭ pirakkinrana
oɾu jaோnijil iɾun̪t̪u t̪eɾijum n̪aːnt̪aːn an̪t̪a kaɾuppaj
n̪aːn in̪t̪a piɾapaɲt͡ʃat̪t̪aj uɾuʋaːkkukireːn marrum uɾuʋaːkkukireːn
ennajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa ʋeːru eʋaɾum illaj iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ʋeːru t̪ajaːɾippaːɭaɾ illaj iʋaj anajt̪t̪um en miːt̪u t̪aொŋkikkaொɳʈiɾukkinrana
at̪an t͡ʃaɾat̪t̪il mut̪t̪u ʋaɾit͡ʃaj t̪aொŋkuʋat̪u paோla
n̪aːn t̪aɳɳiːɾin put̪ija t͡ʃuʋaj n̪aːn
t͡ʃan̪t̪iɾanin ʋeɭɭi t͡ʃuːɾijanin t̪aŋkam
ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭil ʋaɻipaːʈʈu ʋaːɾt̪t̪aj t͡ʃiliɾppu
at̪u iːt̪aɾ marrum ʋalimajjil t͡ʃelkirat̪u
manit̪an kaொʈʈija ʋit̪aj n̪aːn n̪alla inimajjaːna ʋaːt͡ʃanaj
iːɾamaːna puːmijil n̪aːn n̪eɾuppin t͡ʃiʋappu ʋiɭakku
n̪akaɾum ellaːʋarrilum mukkija kaːrru n̪akaɾum
punit̪amaːna aːt̪maːkkaɭin punit̪am ʋeːɾ
aɻijaːt̪at̪u eŋkiɾun̪t̪u t̪uɭiɾt̪t̪at̪u et̪uʋaோ
ɲaːnikaɭin ɲaːnam put̪t̪i
ariʋaːɭijin peɾumaːnin peɾumaj
piɾamaːt̪am kun̪t̪ijin makaneː
iʋaj n̪aːn peːɾaːɾʋam marrum aːt͡ʃaj illaːt̪aʋan
aːjinum eːŋkukira anajʋaɾiʈamum n̪aːn ʋiɾumpuʋat̪u t͡ʃaɾijaːnat̪aː
paːɾat̪at̪t̪in t̪alajʋaɾeː an̪t̪a ellaː manan̪ilajkaɭukkum
amajt̪ijaːna allat̪u uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi allat̪u arijaːmaj
enna ijarkajjin t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭ enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u perukinrana aːnaːl anajt̪t̪u
ennuɭ iɳajkiraːɾkaɭ  n̪aːn alla ulakam
an̪t̪a muːnru kuɳaŋkaɭaːl eːmaːn̪t̪u 
aʋaɾkaɭ anajʋaɾukkum ʋeɭijeː jaːɾ iɾukkiraːɾkaɭ enpat̪aj n̪aːn kaʋanikkaʋillaj
ellaːʋarrirkum meːlaːka n̪it̪t̪ijam kaʈinamaːnat̪u
palʋeːru n̪ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭin t̪ejʋiːka an̪t̪a mukkaːʈʈajt̪ t̪uɭajkka
at̪u ennaj marajkkirat̪u innum ennaj ʋaɳaŋkupaʋaɾkaɭ
at̪ajt̪ t̪uɭajt̪t̪u kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃelluŋkaɭ
n̪aːn arijappaʈaʋillaj
t̪iːmaj t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭukkum muʈʈaːɭkaɭukkum
allat̪u aʈippaʈaj marrum  t͡ʃejja aʋaɾkaɭukkum illaj
eʋanuʈajja manam ʋaɲt͡ʃikkappaʈukirat̪aோ at̪ajk kaːʈʈi
at͡ʃuɾaɾkaɭin ʋaɻijaj eʈuppaʋaɾkaɭum alla#
n̪aːnku ʋakajjaːna manit̪aɾkaɭ ennaj ariʋaːɾkaɭ aɻukiraʋan
aɾd͡ʒunaː arija eːŋkum manit̪anum
meːlum ut̪aʋi t͡ʃejja uɻajppaʋaɾ marrum amaɾn̪t̪iɾuppaʋaɾ
ennajp parri t͡ʃila ariʋaːɭi
in̪t̪a n̪aːnkil
in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː mika ujaɾn̪t̪a aɾukil t͡ʃiran̪t̪a
at̪u kaʈajt͡ʃi pakt̪ijuɭɭa aːt̪maː ɲaːnam n̪aோkkam
t̪i on miːt̪u anpeː ellaːʋarrirkum meːlaːka n̪aːn
aʋanukku meːlum aʋaɾ enakku mikaʋum piɾijamaːnaʋaɾ
n̪aːlʋaɾum n̪allaʋaɾkaɭ ennajt̪ t̪eːʈuŋkaɭ aːnaːl ennuʈajjat̪u
it̪ajat̪t̪in uɳmaj uɳmajjuɭɭa  ennil t̪aŋkijiɾun̪t̪at̪u
t̪aŋkaɭin meːlaːna aːt͡ʃiːɾʋaːt̪amaːka ennaj eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɳʈu
aʋaɾkaɭ ennuʈajjaʋaɾkaɭ alla aːnaːl n̪aːn  n̪aːneː kuːʈa
pala piraʋikaɭin muʈiʋil aʋaɾkaɭ enniʈam ʋaɾukiraːɾkaɭ
aːjinum ɲaːnamuɭɭa makaːt̪maːʋajk kaɳʈupiʈippat̪u kaʈinam
ellaːm ʋaːt͡ʃut̪eːʋ t̪aːn#
jaːɾuʈajja ariʋu purakkaɳikkappaʈʈat̪aோ aʋaɾkaɭum iɾukkiraːɾkaɭ
in̪t̪a aːt͡ʃaj allat̪u at̪anaːl aʋaɾkaɭukku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejja kaொʈukkirat̪u
t͡ʃila t̪aːɻn̪t̪a t̪ejʋaŋkaɭ palʋeːru t͡ʃaʈaŋkukaɭuʈan kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈana
aʋaɾkaɭaj ʋaːɾppat̪an muːlam at̪t̪akajja anajʋaɾukkum 
aʋaɾkaɭ en̪t̪a t͡ʃannat̪ijaj en̪t̪a ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪aj n̪ampikkajjuʈan ʋaɳaŋkuʋaːɾkaɭ 
aʋaɾkaɭukku n̪ampikkaj kaொʈuppaʋan n̪aːneː n̪aːn t̪iɾupt̪ijaːka iɾukkireːn
it̪ajam t̪an kaʈaʋuɭiʈam iʋʋaːru aɾuɭ keːʈkirat̪u
iɾuɳʈa aːnaːl t̪iːʋiɾamaːnat̪u at̪u ʋiɾumpum muʈiʋajk kaொɳʈuɭɭat̪u
kurajn̪t̪a aːt͡ʃiːɾʋaːt̪am  aːnaːl n̪aːnt̪aːn t̪aɾukireːn
innum t͡ʃiːkkiɾameː ʋaːʈippaோj enna t͡ʃirija kanikaɭaj aruʋaʈaj t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
aʋʋaːru ʋaɻipaʈum t͡ʃirija manam kaொɳʈa an̪t̪a manit̪aɾkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ ʋaɻipaʈum iʈat̪t̪irkut͡ʃ t͡ʃelluŋkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭin t̪ejʋaŋkaɭajk kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃelluŋkaɭ
aːnaːl ennuʈajjat̪u enniʈam ʋaː kaɳkaɭ kuɾuʈaɾkaɭ
ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈaːt̪a ʋeɭippaːʈaːkak kaɾut̪uʋat̪u
en uɳmajjaːna t͡ʃujat̪t̪il ennajp puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭaʋillaj
aɻijaːt̪a paːɾʋajjarra ariʋikkappaʈaːt̪a
n̪ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭin en maːja mukkaːʈukku pinnaːl marajn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
n̪aːn ellaோɾaːlum paːɾkkappaʈuʋat̪illaj enakku t̪eɾijaʋillaj 
pirakkaːt̪a marrum maːraːt̪a  t͡ʃejalarra ulakat̪t̪irku
aːnaːl n̪aːn aɾd͡ʒunaː iɾun̪t̪a anajt̪t̪um t̪eɾijum
marrum iɾukkum anajt̪t̪um marrum iɾukka ʋeːɳʈija anajt̪t̪um
aʋaɾkaɭil oɾuʋaɾukkum ennajt̪ t̪eɾijaːt̪u
et̪iɾ d͡ʒaோʈikaɭin miːt̪aːna aːɾʋat̪t̪aːl
lajk ʈislajk enra an̪t̪a iɾu kaɳɳikaɭaːl iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
anajt̪t̪u ujiɾinaŋkaɭum t̪ikajppuʈan ʋaːɻkinrana t͡ʃilaʋarrajk kaːppaːrruŋkaɭ
jaːɾ paːʋaŋkaɭaj ʋiʈʈu punit̪amaːna t͡ʃejal t̪akaʋal
et̪iɾppukaɭil iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈu n̪ampikkajjil urut̪ijaːka
ennajp parrikkaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
jaːɾ piɭaʋupaʈukiraːɾkaɭ jaːɾ ennil t̪eːʈukiraːɾkaɭ
pirappu# marrum irappiliɾun̪t̪u aʈajkkalam aʋaɾkaɭukku uɳmaj iɾukkirat̪u
ennaj arin̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ piɾammaː aːnmaːʋin aːnmaː ennaj arijaʋum
at̪ijaːt̪man kaɾmaːʋaj ariʋeːn en ʋeːlaj
n̪aːn aːt̪ipuːt̪an ʋaːɻʋin irajʋan enpat̪aj arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
meːlum aːt̪it̪ajʋaː anajt̪t̪u kaʈaʋuɭkaɭin irajʋan
marrum aːt̪ijaɲan t̪ijaːkat̪t̪in irajʋan
anpuʈanum n̪ampikkajjuʈanum ennaj n̪anraːka ʋaɳaŋkuŋkaɭ
maɾaɳa n̪eːɾat̪t̪il ennajk kaɳʈupiʈit̪t̪u piʈit̪t̪uk kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
