at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
jaːɾ an̪t̪a piɾammaː enna an̪t̪a aːt̪maːʋin aːt̪maː
at̪ijat̪man enna ellaːʋarrilum t͡ʃiran̪t̪aʋaɾ
uŋkaɭ ʋeːlaj kaɾmaː at̪u ennaʋenru t͡ʃaொlluŋkaɭ
n̪iːŋkaɭ aːt̪ipuːt̪aː enru pejaɾiʈukiriːɾkaɭaː miːɳʈum enna
aːt̪it̪aːʋaː enraːl aːm at̪u eppaʈi ʋaɾukirat̪u
unnuʈajja maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪il aːt̪ijaɲanaːka iɾukka muʈijumaː
mat̪uʋajk kaொnraʋan meːlum enakku t̪eɾijappaʈut̪t̪uŋkaɭ
maɾaɳa n̪eːɾat̪t̪il unnaj eʋʋaɭaʋu n̪alla manit̪aɾkaɭ kaɳʈupiʈippaːɾkaɭ
kiɾuʂɳaː
n̪aːn piɾammaː oɾeː n̪it̪t̪ija kaʈaʋuɭ
meːlum at̪ijaːt̪man enpat̪u en ujiɾin pejaɾ
aːt̪maːkkaɭin aːnmaː enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u enna purappaʈukirat̪u
ellaː ujiɾkaɭajjum ʋaːɻa ʋajppat̪u kaɾmaː enru aɻajkkappaʈukirat̪u
marrum piɾikkappaʈʈa ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈukirat̪u
n̪aːn aːt̪ipuːt̪an ujiɾkaɭin irajʋan
meːlum aːt̪it̪ajʋaː anajt̪t̪u kaʈaʋuɭkaɭin irajʋan
eːnenraːl n̪aːn puɾuʂanajp perraʋan
marrum aːt̪ijaɲan t̪ijaːkat̪t̪in irajʋan
n̪aːn  iŋkeː in̪t̪a uʈalil unnuʈan peːt͡ʃukireːn 
aːm n̪iː oɾu uɾuʋam anajt̪t̪u aːlajaŋkaɭukkum
enakkut͡ʃ t͡ʃuʈaɾ meːlum maɾaɳa n̪eːɾat̪t̪il
ennaj maʈʈum t̪ijaːnit̪t̪aʋan
aʋanuʈajja t͡ʃat̪ajjajk kaɭajn̪t̪u enniʈam ʋeɭijeː ʋaɾukiraːn
en iɾuppukkuɭ n̪uɻajkirat̪u  t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkam illaj
aːnaːl aʋaɾ ʋeːruʋit̪amaːka t̪ijaːnam t͡ʃejt̪aːl
maɾaɳa n̪eːɾat̪t̪il t͡ʃat̪ajjajk kaɭajʋat̪il
kun̪t̪ijin makaneː t̪aːn t̪eːʈija iʈat̪t̪irkut͡ʃ t͡ʃelkiraːn
eːnenil aːnmaː at̪an ʋaʈiʋamaːkaʋeː uɭɭat̪u
appaʈijaːnaːl ennaj eppaோt̪um un it̪ajat̪t̪il iɾu marrum t͡ʃaɳʈaj
it̪ajamum manamum en miːt̪u n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾukkum paோt̪u n̪iːjum
n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka enniʈam ʋaɾuʋeːn piɾin̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ anajʋaɾum ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ
urut̪ijaːna n̪ampikkajjin oɾupaோt̪um at͡ʃajjaːt̪a ʋiɾuppat̪t̪uʈan
ʋeːru kaʈaʋuɭkaɭukkut͡ʃ t͡ʃaொn̪t̪amillaj anajʋaɾum enniʈam ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ
mika ujaɾn̪t̪a puɾuʂan punit̪amaːnaʋaɾ
muniʋaɾum paːʈakaɾumaːna ennaj arin̪t̪aʋaɾ
n̪aːɭ paɻamajjaːnat̪u muːnru ulakaŋkaɭ t̪aŋkum
ellajjarrat̪u aːnaːl oʋʋaொɾu aɳuʋirkum kaொɳʈu ʋaɾupaʋaɾ
at̪aj ʋiɾajʋupaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪u parri jaːɾaj n̪aːn t͡ʃaொlkireːn
maɾaɳa ariʋajk kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃellum en ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪aj arin̪t̪eːn
en piɾakaːt͡ʃat̪t̪ajk kaɳʈeːn  en̪t̪ak kaɳɳum kaːɳaːt̪at̪u 
t͡ʃuːɾijan eɾijum t̪aŋkat̪t̪aj ʋiʈa piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːka oɭiɾkirat̪u
iɾuɭ t͡ʃit̪ariaʋaɾukku ʋan̪t̪iɾukkirat̪u
t͡ʃaɾijaːna ʋaːɻkkaj meːlum ʋaːɻkkaj muʈiʋaʈajjum n̪eːɾat̪t̪il
ʋeːkamaːna marrum n̪ampakamaːna pakt̪ijuʈan
amajt̪ijaːna puɾuʋaŋkaɭukku aʈijil at͡ʃajjaːmal muːt͡ʃt͡ʃaj ʋaɾajt̪al
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna amajt̪ijil uɳmajjuɭɭa oɾuʋaɾ irakkiraːɾ 
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijil puɾuʂanin t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪irku amajt̪i t͡ʃenrat̪u
ʋeːt̪am oːt̪upaʋaɾkaɭ pejaɾ perra iʈam
akʂaɾam alʈimeːʈ eŋkeː paːʈupaʈʈeːn
t̪uraʋikaɭ marrum t̪uraʋikaɭ  aʋaɾkaɭin paːt̪aj onrut̪aːn
an̪t̪a ʋaɻijil  ujaɾn̪t̪a ʋaɻi  muːʈupaʋaɾ t͡ʃelkiraːɾ
aʋanuʈajja anajt̪t̪u pulankaɭin ʋaːjilkaɭum aːt͡ʃajjajp puːʈʈukirat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u it̪ajat̪t̪il paːt̪ukaːppaːnat̪u mukkija kaːrrukaɭaj majjappaʈut̪t̪ukirat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u piɾin̪t̪a t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj miːt̪u urut̪ijaːka amajkka
meːlum oːm muɳumuɳuppat̪u punit̪amaːna eɻut̪t̪u
piɾammaːʋin t͡ʃinnam  ennaj t̪ijaːnam t͡ʃejkiraːɾ
jaːɾukkaːka ʋeːru en̪t̪a kaʈaʋuɭkaɭum paːɾkkaʋillaj
eppaொɻut̪um enakku n̪aːn eɭit̪aːkap perreːn
at̪t̪akajja jaோkijaːl marrum ennaj aʈajt̪al
aʋaɾkaɭ ʋiɻaʋillaj  an̪t̪a makaːt̪maːkkaɭ  miːɳʈum pirappirku
ʋaːɻkkajkku it̪u ʋalijin iʈam it̪u muʈiʋaʈajkirat̪u
aːnaːl mikun̪t̪a aːt͡ʃiːɾʋaːt̪at̪t̪in ʋaɻijaj eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
ulakaŋkaɭ aɾd͡ʒunaːpiɾammaːʋin ulakamum kuːʈa
maɾaɳat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋaːɻkkajjin amajt̪ijinmajkku miːɳʈum t̪iɾumpaʋum
aːnaːl aʋaɾkaɭ kun̪t̪ijin makaneː at̪u ennaj aʈajjum
ini ɾut͡ʃi piraʋi piɾammaːʋin n̪aːɭ t̪eɾin̪t̪aːl
et̪u aːjiɾam jukaŋkaɭ uŋkaɭukku t̪eɾin̪t̪aːl
piɾammaːʋin iɾaʋaj uɾuʋaːkkum aːjiɾam jukaŋkaɭ
pinnaɾ aʋaɾ arin̪t̪at̪u paோl pakalajjum iɾaʋajjum arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
an̪t̪a paɾan̪t̪a ʋiʈijal uʈajkkumpaோt̪u ​​at̪u kaɳɳukku t̪eɾijaːt̪at̪u
kaːɳakkuːʈijat̪aːka put̪it̪aːka kaொɳʈuʋaɾappaʈʈat̪u
an̪t̪a aːɻamaːna iɾaʋu iɾuɭaʈajjum paோt̪u ​​uɭɭa anajt̪t̪um
at̪aj anuppijaʋaɾiʈam miːɳʈum maŋkukirat̪u
aːm ujiɾinaŋkaɭin in̪t̪a paɾan̪t̪a n̪iruʋanam 
miːɳʈum miːɳʈum urpat̪t̪i  kaːlaːʋat̪ijaːkirat̪u
piɾammaːʋin iɾaʋu n̪eːɾat̪t̪il marrum piɾammaːʋin ʋiʈijalil
put̪it̪aːkap piran̪t̪a ʋaːɻkkajkku at̪an ʋiɾuppaminri eɻukirat̪u
aːnaːlujaɾn̪t̪a aːɻamaːna uɭɭukkuuɭɭat̪u
marraொɾu ʋaːɻkkaj uɳaɾʋin ʋaːɻkkajjajp paோla alla
paːɾʋajjiliɾun̪t̪u t̪appit̪t̪al maːraːt̪at̪u it̪u t̪aːŋkum
t͡ʃiɾuʂʈikkappaʈʈa anajt̪t̪um aɻin̪t̪uʋiʈʈaːl
it̪ut̪aːn ʋaːɻkkaj enru pejaɾiʈappaʈʈat̪u
ellajjarrat̪u anajt̪t̪u murrilum
aŋku ʋan̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ jaːɾum t̪iɾumpuʋat̪illaj an̪t̪a ʋaːɻkkaj
ennuʈajjat̪u n̪aːn aŋkeː iɾukkireːn meːlum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː n̪ampikkaj muːlam
et̪u alajjaːt̪u ʋaɾa oɾu ʋaɻi iɾukkirat̪u
aŋku n̪aːn puɾuʂan n̪aːn paɾaʋijaʋan
ennajt͡ʃ t͡ʃurrijuɭɭa piɾapaɲt͡ʃam  jaːɾil ʋaːɻkirat̪u
ellaː ujiɾkaɭumaʋʋaːru t͡ʃenraʈajn̪t̪u kaːɳappaʈalaːm
              #
ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭ ʋaɭaɾum punit̪a kanijaj ʋiʈa ʋaɭamaːnat̪u
paɾit͡ʃukaɭaj ʋiʈa peɾijat̪u piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj allat̪u n̪aோnpaj ʋiʈa t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
at̪t̪akajja ɲaːnam jaோki in̪t̪a ʋaɻijil t̪eɾin̪t̪u
kaʈajt͡ʃijil mikat͡ʃ t͡ʃiran̪t̪a amajt̪ikku ʋaɾukirat̪u
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
akʂaɾapaɾapɾahmajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u oɾeː unnat̪a kaʈaʋuɭukkaːna pakt̪ijin muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
ippaோt̪u n̪aːn unakkut̪ t̪irappeːn  jaːɾuʈajja it̪ajam
n̪iɾaːkaɾikkaʋillaj  an̪t̪a kaʈajt͡ʃik kat̪aj aːɻamaːnamarajkkappaʈʈa
en ʋaːnaŋkaɭ marrum puːmijin an̪t̪a t̪aொlajt̪uːɾa ɾakat͡ʃijam
ariʋajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa et̪u unnaj n̪aோjkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈuʋikkum
oɾu aɾat͡ʃak kat̪aj oɾu aɾat͡ʃa maɾmam
aːm aːnmaːʋaj t̪uːjmajppaʈut̪t̪um oɭi
oʋʋaொɾu paːʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪um punit̪at̪t̪in oɭi
uɭɭam paொliʋuʈan paːɾppat̪arku ʋerru
n̪aʈakka eɭit̪aːnat̪u ʋarraːt̪at̪u
it̪ajp peraːt̪aʋaɾkaɭ ʋit͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃat̪t̪il t̪aʋariʋiʈukiraːɾkaɭ
peɾija ɲaːnat̪t̪ajp puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa ennaj aʈajjaːt̪eː
un et̪iɾikaɭaj aɻippaʋaneː aʋaj put̪it̪aːka muːɻkum
t͡ʃat̪ajjin t͡ʃaːmɾaːd͡ʒjat̪t̪irkuɭ ellaːmeː maːrum
ennaːleːjeː paொɾuɭkaɭin paɾan̪t̪a piɾapaɲt͡ʃam
ʋeɭin̪aːʈʈil paɾaʋijuɭɭat̪uʋeɭippaʈajjaːt̪a ennaːl
ennil anajt̪t̪u iɾuppukaɭum aʈaŋkijuɭɭana
aʋarril n̪aːn illaj
innum aʋaj aʈaŋkaʋillaj
kaɳɳukkut̪ t̪eɾin̪t̪a ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ perru aɾaʋaɳajkka mujaluŋkaɭ
maɾmam kampiːɾamaːnat̪u en iɾuppu
anajt̪t̪ajjum uɾuʋaːkkut̪al anajt̪t̪ajjum n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪ut̪al  innum ʋaːɻkirat̪u
ellaːʋarrirkum ʋeɭijeː
paːɾ kaɾajjillaːt̪a kaːrraːka
aɭaʋarra iʈat̪t̪il n̪akaɾaʋum aːnaːl aʋaj iʈam alla
meːlum ʋiɳʋeɭi enpat̪u n̪akaɾum kaːrrukaɭ illaːt̪a iʈamaːka iɾun̪t̪at̪u
enaʋeː anajt̪t̪um ennuɭ uɭɭana aːnaːl n̪aːn illaj
oʋʋaொɾu kalpat̪t̪in muʈiʋilum in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ
en iɾuppukkut̪ t̪iɾumpum anajt̪t̪um ʋaɾukinrana
oʋʋaொɾu kalpat̪t̪in t̪aொʈakkat̪t̪ilum anajt̪t̪um
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u put̪it̪aːkap piran̪t̪aʋaj
aːrral muːlam
marrum piɾakiɾut̪ijin ut̪aʋi en ʋeɭippura t͡ʃujam
miːɳʈum miːɳʈum n̪aːn ʋeɭijeː t͡ʃelkireːn
kaːɳakkuːʈija ʋiʂajaŋkaɭin pakut̪ikaɭ  aʋaɾkaɭin ʋiɾuppam illaːmal 
aʋaj anajt̪t̪um  piɾakiɾut̪ijin t͡ʃakt̪ijaːl
innum in̪t̪a arput̪amaːna paʈajppukaɭ iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː ennaj iːʈupaʈut̪t̪aʋillaj
ennaj ent͡ʃejn illaj n̪aːn aʋaɾkaɭiʈamiɾun̪t̪u piɾin̪t̪u amaɾn̪t̪iɾukkireːn
marra marrum ujaɾ marrum ilaʋat͡ʃa  iɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
ennaːl uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈa ulakap paொɾuɭkaɭ ippaʈit̪t̪aːn t͡ʃejkinrana
at͡ʃajjum allat̪u at͡ʃajjaːt̪a anajt̪t̪ajjum ʋeɭijeː kaொɳʈu ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ
ʋaːɻum allat̪u ujiɾarra iʋʋaːreː ulakaŋkaɭ t͡ʃelkinrana
ʋaʈiʋil marajkkappaʈʈa ennaj manaŋkaɭ t̪aʋaraːka n̪inajkkinrana
en ɾakat͡ʃija iɾuppaj aʋaɾkaɭ paːɾkkaʋillaj illaj
en marajn̪t̪a ijarkaj ʋaːɻum anajt̪t̪ajjum aːɭukirat̪u
ʋiːɳ n̪ampikkajkaɭ pint̪aொʈaɾt̪al ʋiːɳ t͡ʃejalkaɭ t͡ʃejt̪al uːʈʈi
ʋiːɳaːna ariʋaj aɾt̪t̪amillaːmal t̪eːʈukiraːɾkaɭ
oɾu t̪iːja ʋaɻi miɾukaŋkaɭ marrum pit͡ʃaːt͡ʃukaɭin ʋaɻi
aːnaːl en makaːt̪maːkkaɭ unnat̪a aːt̪maːkkaɭ
paɾalaோkap paːt̪ajjil t͡ʃelpaʋaɾkaɭeː ennaj ʋaɳaŋkuŋkaɭ
alajkkaɻikkaːt̪a it̪ajaŋkaɭuʈanennaj aːt̪aːɾamaːka arin̪t̪u
ʋaːɻkkajjin n̪it̪t̪ija aːt̪aːɾam muʈiʋillaːt̪at̪u
aʋaɾkaɭ ennaj makimajppaʈut̪t̪ukiraːɾkaɭ ennajt̪ t̪eːʈu aʋaɾkaɭin t͡ʃapat̪aŋkaɭajk kaːppaːrruŋkaɭ
maɾijaːt̪aj marrum anpu maːraːt̪a n̪ampikkajjuʈan
ennaj ʋaɳaŋkut̪al aːm aʋaɾkaɭum ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾkaɭ
jaːɾ ʋiɻit̪t̪a it̪ajaŋkaɭaj t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
aːʋijin aɻut̪t̪at̪t̪aj uːʈuɾuʋi uɳaɾuŋkaɭ
panmaʈaŋku iɾun̪t̪aːlum ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum oɾu paʈaj
n̪aːn t̪ijaːkam n̪aːn piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj
iran̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭukkaːna irut̪it͡ʃ t͡ʃaʈaŋkukeːk n̪aːn
n̪aːn kuɳappaʈut̪t̪um muːlikaj n̪aːn n̪ej
man̪t̪iɾam t͡ʃuʈaɾ marrum eɾijum
n̪aːn in̪t̪a ellajjarra piɾapaɲt͡ʃam
t̪an̪t̪aj t̪aːj muːt̪aːt̪ajjaɾ marrum kaːʋalaɾ
karralin muʈiʋu t̪uːjmajppaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪u
paɭapaɭappaːna n̪iːɾil n̪aːn oːm n̪aːn
ɾikʋeːt̪am t͡ʃaːmaʋeːt̪am jad͡ʒuɾʋeːt̪am
ʋaɻi ʋaɭaɾppaʋaɾ irajʋan n̪iːt̪ipat̪i
t͡ʃaːʈt͡ʃi t̪aŋkumiʈam aʈajkkalam
n̪aɳpan n̪iːɾuːrru marrum ʋaːɻkkaj kaʈal
et̪u anuppukirat̪u ʋiɻuŋkukirat̪u ulakaŋkaɭin paொkkiʂam
marrum put̪ajjal araj ʋit̪aj marrum ʋit̪aj ʋit̪ajppaʋaɾ
muʈiʋillaː aruʋaʈajkaɭ eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾukinrana t͡ʃuːɾija ʋeppam ennuʈajjat̪u
t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪in maɻaj ʋaɻaŋkuʋat̪u allat̪u t̪aʈuppat̪u ennuʈajjat̪u
maɾaɳam n̪aːn aɻijaːt̪a ʋaːɻkkaj n̪aːn
aɾd͡ʒunaː  marrum  kaːɳakkuːʈija ʋaːɻkkaj
marrum ʋaːɻkkaj kaɳɳukku t̪eɾijaːt̪at̪u
aːm karraʋaɾkaɭ
t͡ʃaோma mat̪uʋaj aɾun̪t̪ija muppeɾum ʋeːt̪ikaɭ
paːʋaŋkaɭaj n̪iːkkuŋkaɭ pali t͡ʃelut̪t̪uŋkaɭ  aʋaɾkaɭ enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃampaːt̪ikkiraːɾkaɭ
sʋaɾkaː t͡ʃellum paːt̪aj irajt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ t̪ejʋiːkamaːnaʋaj
peɾija t̪eːʋaɾkaɭ ujaɾn̪t̪a in̪t̪iɾanin t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪il aʋaɾkaɭukku uɳaʋaɭikkiraːɾkaɭ
aːjinum aʋaɾkaɭ an̪t̪a aɭappaɾija makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaj ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪um paோt̪u
t͡ʃelaʋaɻit̪t̪a t͡ʃaொɾkkam kaொʈukkappaʈʈa t̪akut̪ikkaːna kuːli
maɾaɳa ulakirku ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ miːɳʈum oɾumuraj maːruŋkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭukkuɾija kuːli kiʈajt̪t̪at̪u aʋaɾkaɭ t̪aŋkaɭ put̪ajjalaj t͡ʃeːmit̪t̪u ʋajt̪t̪anaɾ
mummaʈaŋku ʋeːt̪aːkamat̪t̪ajjum at̪an eɻut̪t̪ajjum pinparrut̪al
appaʈit̪ t̪eːʈukiraʋan ʋiɾajn̪t̪a inpat̪t̪ajp perukiraːn
ʋan̪t̪u paோkum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi n̪aːn aʋaɾkaɭukku ʋaɻaŋkukireːn
aːnaːl ennaj ʋaɻipaʈum paːkkijaʋaːnkaɭukku
ʋeːru eŋkum t̪iɾumpaːmal ʋeːkamaːna manat̪uʈan
appaːl muɻu aːnan̪t̪at̪t̪in urut̪ijaj n̪aːn kaொɳʈu ʋaɾukireːn
illaj marra kaʈaʋuɭkaɭajp pinparrum it̪ajaŋkaɭ
eɭimajjaːna n̪ampikkajjil aʋaɾkaɭin piɾaːɾt̪t̪anajkaɭ enniʈam eɻukinrana
kun̪t̪ijin makaneː aʋaɾkaɭ t̪aʋaraːka d͡ʒepit̪t̪aːlum
eːnenil n̪aːn perupaʋaɾum aːɳʈaʋaɾum
iʋaɾkaɭ arijaːt̪a oʋʋaொɾu t̪ijaːkat̪t̪ilum
t͡ʃaɾijaːka at̪anaːl aʋaj miːɳʈum puːmijil ʋiɻukinrana
kaʈaʋuɭkaɭajp pinparrupaʋaɾkaɭ t̪aŋkaɭ kaʈaʋuɭkaɭiʈam t͡ʃelkinranaɾ jaːɾ t͡ʃapat̪am
pit̪ɾukkaɭukku aʋaɾkaɭin aːnmaː pit̪ɾikaɭukkut͡ʃ t͡ʃelkirat̪u manaŋkaɭ
t̪iːja puːʈʈukaɭukku puːʈʈukaɭukku t͡ʃiŋk kaொʈukkappaʈʈat̪u
ennaj n̪eːt͡ʃikkiraʋan enniʈam ʋaɾukiraːn
ʋit͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃat̪t̪uʈanum anpuʈanum enakku aɾppaɳippaʋaɾ
oɾu ilaj oɾu puː oɾu paɻam t̪aɳɳiːɾ uːrrappaʈʈat̪u
an̪t̪a piɾat͡ʃaːt̪at̪t̪aj n̪aːn eːrrukkaொɭkireːn anpuʈan t͡ʃejt̪eːn
pakt̪i t͡ʃit̪t̪at̪t̪uʈan n̪iː enna t͡ʃejʋaːj iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
uɳɳut̪al allat̪u t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃejt̪al paɾit͡ʃukaɭ ʋaɻaŋkut̪al
t̪aொɻukajjaோ ʋiɾat̪amaோ anajt̪t̪um n̪irajʋeːraʈʈum
enakkaːka ennuʈajjat̪aːka enaʋeː n̪iː unnaj ʋiʈuʋit̪t̪ukkaொɭ
kaɾmapan̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u manit̪aɾkaɭaj ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkum t͡ʃaŋkili
n̪allat̪u marrum t̪iːja piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃinajkku at̪anaːl ʋaɾum
enakkup paːt̪ukaːppu  n̪iː t͡ʃat̪ajjaj ʋiʈʈu ʋeɭijeːrumpaோt̪u 
n̪ampikkajjinaːlum t̪uraʋarat̪t̪inaːlum ennuʈan iɳajn̪t̪at̪u
n̪aːn anajʋaɾukkum t͡ʃamam ʋerukkaʋillaj enru enakkut̪ t̪eɾijum
t͡ʃaːt̪akamaːka illaj enru enakkut̪ t̪eɾijum uɳʈaːnat̪u ennuʈajjat̪u
aːnaːl ennaj anpuʈan ʋaɳaŋkupaʋaɾkaɭaj n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkireːn
aʋaɾkaɭ ennil iɾukkiraːɾkaɭ n̪aːn aʋaɾkaɭil
illaj iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
t̪iːja ʋaːɻʋu onru t̪an t͡ʃin̪t̪anajjil t̪iɾumpinaːl
enakku n̪eːɾaːka n̪allaʋaɾkaɭiʈajjeː aʋaɾaj eɳɳuŋkaɭ
aʋaɾ t̪eːɾn̪t̪eʈukkappaʈʈa ujaɾn̪t̪a ʋaɻi aʋan ʋaɭaɾʋaːn
n̪iːt̪imaːn n̪iːɳʈa aʋaɾ an̪t̪a amajt̪ijaj aʈajʋaːɾ
et̪u maːraːt̪u in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ennaj n̪ampi jaːɾum aɻija muʈijaːt̪u enpat̪il urut̪ijaːka iɾuŋkaɭ
piɾut̪ajjin makaneː jaːɾ enniʈam t̪iɾumpuʋaːɾkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ paːʋat̪t̪in ʋajirril iɾun̪t̪u piran̪t̪aːlum
peɳ allat̪u aːɳ ʋajt͡ʃija t͡ʃaːt̪ijil uɾuʋaːnat̪u
allat̪u t̪aːɻʋaːkap purakkaɳikkappaʈʈa t͡ʃuːt̪t̪iɾananajʋaɾum
mika ujaɾn̪t̪a paːt̪ajjil kaːl n̪aʈa piraku eppaʈi
punit̪a piɾaːmaɳaɾkaɭum en aɾat͡ʃa punit̪aɾkaɭum
aː in̪t̪a maோt͡ʃamaːna ulakat̪t̪irku ʋan̪t̪uɭɭiːɾkaɭ 
ʋiɾajʋaːna marrum paொjjaːna  uŋkaɭ n̪ampikkajjaj en miːt̪u ʋeːkamaːka ʋajkkaʋum
it̪ajat̪t̪aj n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪i ennajp parri t͡ʃin̪t̪ijuŋkaɭ ennaj ʋaɳaŋku kaொɳʈu ʋaː
enakku piɾat͡ʃaːt̪am enakku sad͡ʒt̪aːt͡ʃ t͡ʃej t͡ʃejja
uŋkaɭ ujaɾn̪t̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi enakku marrum piɾikkappaʈaːt̪a
en iɭajppaːrut̪alukku uŋkaɭ aːʋikaɭ ʋaɻin̪aʈat̪t̪appaʈum
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  muʈikirat̪u pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
ɾaːd͡ʒaʋit̪jaɾaːd͡ʒakuhjajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u aɾat͡ʃa ariʋu marrum aɾat͡ʃaɾkaɭin mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam
maɾmam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː#
innum kaொɲt͡ʃam t̪uːɾam keːɭ n̪iːɳʈa aːjut̪am kaொɳʈa aːɳʈaʋaɾeː n̪aːn t͡ʃaொllum in̪t̪a t͡ʃamiːpat̪t̪ija ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ
eppaொɻut̪um ennaj n̪eːt͡ʃikkum unakku peːɾinpat̪t̪ajjum amajt̪ijajjum t̪aɾuʋat̪aːka kuːrappaʈʈat̪u
peɾija t̪eːʋaɾkaɭaோ allat̪u aɾat͡ʃa ɾiʂikaɭaோ t̪eɾijaːt̪u
en ijalpu t̪eːʋaɾkaɭajjum ɾiʂikaɭajjum ʋeku kaːlat̪t̪irku munpeː uɳʈaːkkijaʋaɾ
aʋaɾ maʈʈumeː ariʋaːɾ  aʋaɾ paːʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈaʋaɾ ɲaːnamuɭɭaʋaɾ
ulakaŋkaɭin irajʋanaːkija ennaj n̪ampikkaj oɭimajamaːna kaɳkaɭaːl paːɾppaʋaɾ
pirakkaːt̪a irakkaːt̪a t̪aொʈaŋkaːt̪a ijarkajkaɭ et̪uʋaːka iɾun̪t̪aːlum t͡ʃaɾi
ʋin̪ijaோkikkappaʈʈa manit̪aɾkaɭukku an̪t̪a ijalpukaɭ enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u pirakkinrana
put̪t̪i t̪iramaj ɲaːnam t͡ʃakipput̪t̪anmaj t͡ʃujakkaʈʈuppaːʈu
uɳmajt̪t̪anmaj t͡ʃamat̪t̪uʋam marrum aːnmaːʋin t̪ujaɾam allat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
pirappum irappum at͡ʃt͡ʃamum at͡ʃt͡ʃaminmajjum aʋamaːnamum
marrum maɾijaːt̪aj marrum inimajjaːna t̪iːŋkarra t̪anmaj# marrum amajt̪i it̪u
at̪eː
enna n̪eːɾn̪t̪aːlum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijum kaɳɳiːɾum pakt̪ijum t͡ʃikkanamum
meːlum kaொʈukka ʋiɾumpuʋat̪um ut̪aʋi t͡ʃejja ʋiɾumpuʋat̪um anajt̪t̪um enat̪u paɾit͡ʃil iɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u
eːɻu mukkija t̪uraʋikaɭ peɾijaʋaɾkaɭ n̪aːlʋaɾ irajjaɾuɭaːna manus amajppu
en ʋeːlajjajp pakiɾn̪t̪ukaொɭʋat̪u  ulakaŋkaɭaj aːɭa iʋajjum enakkup piran̪t̪ana
marrum ɾiʂikaɭ pit̪ɾukkaɭ manukkaɭ anajʋaɾum en manat̪in oɾu eɳɳat̪t̪aːl
in̪t̪a ulakat̪t̪aj n̪iɾappa manit̪a inaŋkaɭ t̪aோnrina
maːja maːʈt͡ʃimajjin enat̪u aːʈt͡ʃijaj jaːɾ puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭkiraːɾkaɭ 
an̪t̪a uɳmaj uɳmaj  inimeːl ennuʈan paɻut̪arra n̪ampikkajjuʈan iɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
aːm ellaːʋarrin muːlamum ennaj arin̪t̪u ellaː ujiɾinaŋkaɭum ennaːl uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈana
aːʋijil uɭɭa ɲaːnikaɭ ennajp parrikkaொɭkiraːɾkaɭ en aːɭt̪at̪t̪uʋat̪t̪irkuɭ kaொɳʈuʋaɾappaʈukiraːɾkaɭ
it̪ajaŋkaɭ en miːt̪u n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾukkinrana muːt͡ʃt͡ʃu ennaj t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃit̪t̪at̪u ennajp pukaɻn̪t̪u oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾukkum
at̪anaːl aʋaɾkaɭukku makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijum amajt̪ijum uɳʈu pakt̪ijaːna t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj marrum peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu
meːlum iʋaɾkaɭukku  iʋʋaːru n̪anraːka t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejt̪u iʈajjaraːt̪u anpu t͡ʃelut̪t̪ut̪al 
n̪aːn oɾu muɻumajjaːna manan̪ilajjaj kaொʈukkireːn at̪an muːlam aʋaɾkaɭ enniʈam iːɾkkiraːɾkaɭ
meːlum aʋaɾkaɭ miːt̪uɭɭa anpirkaːka aʋaɾkaɭin iɾuɳʈa aːnmaːkkaɭukkuɭ n̪aːn ʋaːɻkireːn
meːlum ɲaːna ʋiɭakkin piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːna kat̪iɾkaɭaːl aʋaɾkaɭin arijaːmaj akarrappaʈukirat̪u
aɾd͡ʒunaː
aːm n̪iːjeː paɾapiɾammam ujaɾn̪t̪a urajʋiʈam
maːpeɾum t͡ʃut̪t̪ikaɾippu n̪iːjeː kaʈaʋuɭ
n̪it̪t̪ija anajt̪t̪ajjum paʈajt̪t̪a punit̪amaːna mut̪al
aːɾampam illaːmal irajʋan marrum kaʈaʋuɭkaɭin irajʋan
anajt̪t̪u makaːnkaɭaːlum ariʋikkappaʈʈat̪u  n̪aːɾat̪aɾ
ʋijaːt͡ʃa at͡ʃit̪aː marrum t̪eːʋaːlajaŋkaɭ
iŋkeː n̪iːjeː enakku ariʋikkiraːj
n̪iː t͡ʃaொnnat̪u ippaோt̪u enakku uɳmaj enru t̪eɾijum
keːt͡ʃaʋaː kaʈaʋuɭkaɭaோ manit̪aɾkaɭaோ alla
umat̪u maɾmat̪t̪aj peːjkaɭ puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭaʋillaj
ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u t̪ejʋiːkamaːnat̪u n̪iːjeː
unnukkeː t̪eɾijum meːkkaɾ t͡ʃupɾiːm
ujiɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪irkum t̪alajʋaɾeː t̪eːʋaɾkaɭin irajʋaː
piɾapaɲt͡ʃat̪t̪in ɾaːd͡ʒaː unakku maʈʈum
t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪in t͡ʃirappajt͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlʋat̪arku uɾijat̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ n̪iɾappum an̪t̪a paɾipuːɾaɳaŋkaɭil
unnuʈajja in̪t̪a ulakaŋkaɭ ʋijaːpit̪t̪uɭɭa immaneːʈ
n̪aːn eppaʈi karrukkaொɭʋeːn mika ujaɾn̪t̪a maɾmam
n̪aːn t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u jaோt͡ʃit̪t̪aːlum unnaj arijaʋaː
uŋkaɭ eɳɳarra ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭin en̪t̪a ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪in kiːɻ
n̪iːŋkaɭ puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa muʈijumaː aː miːɳʈum miːɳʈum kuːraʋum
t̪eɭiʋaːna marrum muɻumajjaːna uŋkaɭ t͡ʃiran̪t̪a t̪aோrraŋkaɭ
umat̪u maːʈt͡ʃimaj marrum ʋallamajjin iɾakat͡ʃijaŋkaɭ
manit̪aɾkaɭin ujaɾ makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi oɾupaோt̪um paோt̪aːt̪u
en kaːt̪ukaɭ at̪t̪akajja ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭin amɾit̪t̪aj# kuʈikkumaː
kiɾuʂɳaː
hanʈaː appaʈijeː aːkaʈʈum kuɾu iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː n̪aːn uŋkaɭukku ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪uʋeːn
en maːʈt͡ʃimajjin t͡ʃila pakut̪ikaɭ at̪an aːrralkaɭ panmaʈaŋku
oʋʋaொɾu ujiɾinat̪t̪in it̪ajat̪t̪ilum aːɻamaːka ʋiːrriɾukkum aːʋi n̪aːn
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u aʋaɾkaɭ ʋaɾukiraːɾkaɭ ennaːleːjeː aʋaɾkaɭ ʋaːɻkiraːɾkaɭ en ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjil aʋaɾkaɭ purappaʈuʋaːɾkaɭ
aːt̪it̪jaɾkaɭin ʋiʂɳu n̪aːn an̪t̪a oɭijin at̪ipat̪ikaɭ
maːɾuʈkaɭin maɾit͡ʃt͡ʃi pujal marrum pɭajʈʈin mannaɾkaɭ
pakalil n̪aːn piɾakaːt͡ʃikkireːn eɾijum meːkamarra n̪aɳpakal paொn t͡ʃuːɾijan
iɾaʋil n̪aʈt͡ʃat̪t̪iɾaŋkaɭin n̪aʈuʋeː n̪aːn t͡ʃarukkukireːn paɭapaɭappaːna t͡ʃan̪t̪iɾan
ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭil n̪aːn t͡ʃaːmaʋeːt̪ in̪t̪iɾanin t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪il uɭɭa kaʈaʋuɭkaɭin
ʋaːt͡ʃaʋaː ujiɾkaɭukku kaொʈukkappaʈʈa t̪irankaɭ
uɳaɾn̪t̪u t͡ʃin̪t̪ikkum manam ɾut̪ɾaːs t͡ʃaŋkaɾaɾin
jakʂaɾkaɭ marrum ɾaːʈt͡ʃat͡ʃaɾkaɭ ʋiʈʈeːʂ marrum paːʋakaː
ʋat͡ʃukkaɭ marrum meːɾu malajt͡ʃ t͡ʃikaɾaŋkaɭin ʋiɾuhaspat̪i
ennaj arika mat̪t̪ija kiɾaka t͡ʃakt̪ikaɭ miʈ ʋaːɾijaɾs paɾalaோka
skan̪t̪aː ellaː n̪iːɾʋeɭɭaŋkaɭilum oʋʋaொnrajjum kuʈikkum kaʈal
marrum punit̪a t̪uraʋikaɭin piɾuku marrum punit̪amaːna peːt͡ʃt͡ʃin oːm
piɾaːɾt̪t̪anajkaɭil n̪iːŋkaɭ kit͡ʃukit͡ʃukkum piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj# malajkaɭ himaːlaːʋin pani
meːlum asʋat̪t̪aː at̪t̪i maɾam ʋaɭaɾum anajt̪t̪u maɾaŋkaɭ
t̪eːʋaɾʂikaɭil n̪aːɾat̪aɾ aʋaɾkaɭin t͡ʃit̪ɾaɾat̪
enru t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪il paːʈa marrum munis kapila marrum maːɳikkam
parakkum kut̪iɾajkaɭ ut͡ʃt͡ʃajsɾaʋas ʋeʈit̪t̪a amiɾt̪a alajjiliɾun̪t̪u
jaːnajkaɭ ajɾaːʋat̪am aːɳkaɭil t͡ʃiran̪t̪a marrum mut̪al
aːjut̪aŋkaɭ  in t͡ʃuːʈaːna iʈi ʋeɭɭaj kamat̪uk pat͡ʃukkaɭ
jaːɾuʈajja peɾija paːl maʈimulajkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u anajt̪t̪u it̪ajaŋkaɭin aːt͡ʃajkaɭum aʈipaʈukinrana
paːmpup paɻaŋkuʈijinaɾin ʋaːt͡ʃuki t͡ʃurrija man̪t̪aːɾajp piɳajn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
marrum paɾan̪t̪a t͡ʃuɾuɭkaɭ t͡ʃaːjn̪t̪iɾukkum aːjiɾam kaோɾaj anan̪t̪aː
t͡ʃaːjn̪t̪a ʋiʂɳu marrum n̪iːɾ paொɾuɭkaɭ ʋaɾuɳan aːɾjam
pit̪ɾukkaɭ marrum t̪iːɾppaɭippaʋaɾkaɭil jama n̪iːt̪ipat̪i n̪aːn
t̪ajt̪t̪ijaɾkaɭ piɾahalaːt̪anukku pajappaʈukiraːɾkaɭ n̪aːʈkaɭajjum ʋaɾuʈaŋkaɭajjum t͡ʃan̪t̪ippat̪u et̪u
kaːlat̪t̪in t͡ʃujam n̪aːn ʋanaʋilaŋkukaɭeɾumajkaɭ maːnkaɭ marrum kaɾaʈikaɭ
irajʋanʋaɾɳam puːt͡ʃappaʈʈa puli paraʋajkaɭin paɾan̪t̪a kaɾuʈan
t͡ʃuːraːʋaɭi kaːrrin n̪aʈuʋil iɾat̪t̪am t̪aோjn̪t̪a mat̪t̪ija t̪alajʋaɾ ɾaːmaɾ
makaɾ kaʈalin n̪aʈu miːnkaɭ marrum kaŋkaj oːʈajkaɭ mat̪t̪ijil
aːm mut̪al marrum kaʈajt͡ʃi marrum iɾukkum allat̪u t̪aோnrum anajt̪t̪in majjam
n̪aːn aɾd͡ʒunaː ɲaːnam et̪uʋaோ at̪ajʋiʈa ujaɾn̪t̪a ɲaːnam
ut̪aʈukaɭil ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ n̪aːn marrum kaɳkaɭin paːɾʋaj
marrum eɻut̪appaʈʈa eɻut̪t̪ukkaɭin  pinnappaʈʈa peːt͡ʃt͡ʃin t̪ʋan̪t̪ʋaː#
marrum muʈiʋillaː ʋaːɻkkaj marrum ellajjarra anpu at̪an t͡ʃakt̪i oʋʋaொnrajjum n̪ilajn̪irut̪t̪ukirat̪u
marrum kat͡ʃappaːna maɾaɳam anajʋaɾajjum aːʈkaொɭkirat̪u marrum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna t̪iʈiːɾ pirappu
it̪u puːmijil iɾukkum anajt̪t̪u ujiɾinaŋkaɭajjum ʋeɭit͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪irkuk kaொɳʈuʋaɾukirat̪u
marrum paːɾʋajjarra n̪arpaɳpukaɭil pukaɻ at̪iɾʂʈam paːʈal n̪aːn
marrum n̪inajʋakam marrum paொrumaj marrum kajʋinaj marrum n̪ilajt̪t̪anmaj
ʋeːt̪a t̪ut̪ikaɭil ʋɾihaʈt͡ʃam miːʈʈaɾ kaːjat̪ɾi
maːt̪aŋkaɭil maːɾkat͡ʃiɾʂaː anajt̪t̪u paɾuʋaŋkaɭin muːnru
malaɾ maːlajjiʈappaʈʈa ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪am   
iɾaʈʈajeʈʈu
makat̪t̪uʋat̪t̪in t͡ʃirappajjum peɾijaʋaɾin peɾumajjajjum
ʋerri n̪aːn marrum at̪iɾaʈi marrum n̪allaʋaɾkaɭin n̪anmaj
marrum ʋiɾuʂɳijin inat̪t̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃeːɾn̪t̪a ʋaːt͡ʃut̪eːʋ in̪t̪a paːɳʈu kuʈʈi
n̪iːjeːaːm en aɾd͡ʒunaː n̪iːjeː eːnenil n̪iː ennuʈajjaʋan
kaʋiɲaɾkaɭ ut͡ʃaːnaː t̪uraʋikaɭ ʋijaːt͡ʃaɾ muniʋaɾ t̪ejʋiːka
ʋerrijaːɭaɾkaɭin kaொɭkaj aɾat͡ʃaɾkaɭin aːrral
karkum iɾakat͡ʃija ʋiʂajaŋkaɭaj peɾum uʈajkkaːt̪a maௌnam
karrarin̪t̪a anajʋaɾin kalaːt͡ʃaːɾam ʋiɭajjum anajt̪t̪in ʋit̪aj
ʋaːɻum allat̪u ujiɾarra amajt̪ijaːna allat̪u kiɭaɾn̪t̪eɻun̪t̪a en̪t̪a ujiɾinamaːka iɾun̪t̪aːlum
aʋaj et̪uʋum ellaː ulakaŋkaɭilum illaj aːnaːl at̪u ennaːleːjeː uɭɭat̪u
n̪aːʋaːl t͡ʃaொlla muʈijaːt̪u aɾd͡ʒunaː ʋaː enru t͡ʃaொlli muʈiʋat̪illaj
iʋarril enat̪u ellajjarra makimajkaɭil t͡ʃilaʋarraj n̪aːn unakkuk karpikkireːn
eːnenraːl aʋaɾ arput̪amaːna ʋeːlajjum kampiːɾamum ʋallamajjum
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪eː anajt̪t̪um n̪aʈan̪t̪ana it̪aj n̪iː eːrrukkaொɭ
aːjinum iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː n̪iː eppaʈip pera ʋeːɳʈum in̪t̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjin paɾan̪t̪a t̪anmaj
anajt̪t̪ajjum aːkki anajt̪t̪ajjum paʈajt̪t̪a n̪aːneː at̪an t̪ani irajʋanaj n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾuppeːn
pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin  at̪t̪ijaːjam iŋkeː
ʋipuːt̪i jaோkam enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u paɾalaோka paɾipuːɾaɳaŋkaɭaːl mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
en aːnmaː t͡ʃaːn̪t̪ijaʈajja it̪aj n̪aːn unniʈam keːʈʈeːn
maɾma ut͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪in ʋiɾiʋaʈajt̪al
at̪jaːt̪man enru pejaɾ et̪ajp puɾin̪t̪ukaொɭʋat̪u
en iɾuɭ n̪iːŋkijat̪u ippaோt̪ajkku enakku t̪eɾijum
oː t̪aːmaɾajk kaɳɳeː#aːɳkaɭin pirappu eŋkiɾun̪t̪u
aʋaɾkaɭin maɾaɳam eŋkiɾun̪t̪u marrum enna makimajkaɭ
uŋkaɭ aɻijaːt̪a aːʈt͡ʃi n̪anraːka n̪aːn paːɾkkireːn
n̪iːjeː ariʋit̪t̪apaʈi irajjaːɳmaj aːɳʈaʋaɾeː
umat̪u ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪in an̪t̪a makimajjin t͡ʃaːjal
muɻuʋat̪umaːka ʋeɭippaʈʈat̪u oː t̪ejʋiːkamaːnaʋaneː
it̪u muʈin̪t̪aːl n̪aːn paːɾʋajjajt̪ t̪aːŋkinaːl
ellaː piɾaːɾt̪t̪anajkaɭukkum irajʋaneː unnajk kaːɳumpaʈi t͡ʃejʋaːjaːka
n̪it̪t̪ija kaʈaʋuɭaːna ummajjeː enakkuk kaːʈʈuŋkaɭ
kiɾuʂɳaː
appaʈijaːnaːl piɾut̪ajjin makaneː n̪aːn unakkaːka ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪ukireːn
en maɾmat̪t̪aj alaŋkaɾikkum an̪t̪a ilaʈt͡ʃam aːjiɾam ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭ
ellajjarra ajt͡ʃuʋaɾijamaːna t̪ejʋiːkamaːna ennuʈajja ellaː t͡ʃaːjalkaɭajjum unakkuk kaːʈʈukireːn
en maːriʋaɾum t͡ʃaːjalkaɭ en eɳɳarra ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭ paːɾ ennuʈajja in̪t̪a mukat̪t̪il
aːt̪it̪jaɾkaɭ ʋat͡ʃukkaɭ ɾut̪t̪iɾaɾkaɭ asʋinkaɭ marrum maɾut̪ukaɭ paːɾkka
eɳɳarra at̪it͡ʃajaŋkaɭ in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː unnajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa jaːɾukkum ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈaʋillaj
it̪oː it̪ut̪aːn piɾapaɲt͡ʃampaːɾuŋkaɭ ujiɾ marrum irappu enraːl enna
n̪aːn anajt̪t̪ajjum onru t̪iɾaʈʈukireːn  ennil un ut̪aʈukaɭ kuːrijat̪u paோl paːɾ
n̪it̪t̪ijamaːna kaʈaʋuɭ miːt̪u mikaʋum kaʈaʋuɭ ennaj paːɾ n̪iːŋkaɭ enna piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj t͡ʃejkiriːɾkaɭ enru paːɾuŋkaɭ
unnaːl muʈijaːt̪uallat̪u manit̪ak kaɳkaɭaːl aɾd͡ʒunaː eppaோt̪um iɾukkalaːm
aːkajjaːl n̪aːn unakku t̪ejʋiːka uɳaɾʋajt̪ t̪aɾukireːn ʋeːru kaɳkaɭ ʋeːɳʈum put̪ija oɭi
marrum paːɾ it̪u en makimaj maɾaɳa paːɾʋajkku ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
piraku aɾat͡ʃeː kaʈaʋuɭ iʋʋaːru kuːrukiraːɾ
pɾit̪aːʋin makan kaːʈt͡ʃikku n̪inraːn
ellaː t͡ʃirappum aːt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾijamum at͡ʃt͡ʃamum
aʋaɾat̪u paɾan̪t̪a t͡ʃaɾʋaʋallamajjuɭɭa t̪alaj
eɳɳarra kaɳkaɭaːl
eɳɳarra ʋaːjkaɭaːl kaʈʈaɭajjiʈukirat̪u
eɳɳarra maːja ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭ t͡ʃuːɻn̪t̪uɭɭana
oɾu ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪il mika ujaɾn̪t̪a n̪ilaj
eɳɳarra oɭiʋiːt͡ʃum makimajkaɭ aɳin̪t̪u
eɳɳarra paɾalaோka aːjut̪aŋkaɭ t̪aːŋki
n̪aʈt͡ʃat̪t̪iɾak kuːʈʈaŋkaɭin maːlajkaɭaːl muʈit͡ʃuːʈʈappaʈʈa
n̪ejjappaʈʈa paɭapaɭappaːna uʈajjil
aʋaɾat̪u paɾipuːɾaɳa iɾuppiliɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃam
oʋʋaொɾu n̪uʈpamaːna t͡ʃaːɾat̪t̪in t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃam
anajt̪t̪u paɾalaோka ʋaːt͡ʃanajkaɭilum ut̪iɾt̪al
kaɳmuːʈit̪t̪anamaːna put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anam at̪ikamaːka paɾaʋukirat̪u
ellajjarra aɻakaːna  anajt̪t̪u iʈaŋkaɭum
aʋanuʈajja ellaː mukaŋkaɭaோʈum
enaʋeː aʋaɾ kaːʈʈinaːɾ iɾun̪t̪aːl ujaɾa ʋeːɳʈum
t̪iʈiːɾenru ʋaːnat̪t̪il
aːjiɾam t͡ʃuːɾijankaɭin ʋejil
n̪ilam ʋeɭɭat̪t̪il muːɻkum oɭikkarrajkaɭ
appaோt̪u an̪t̪a paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪amaːnaʋaɾuʈajjat̪aːka iɾukkalaːm
kampiːɾamum piɾakaːt͡ʃamum kanaʋu kaɳʈat̪u
paːɳʈuʋin makan paːɾt̪t̪aːn
in̪t̪a piɾapaɲt͡ʃam muɻuʋat̪um t͡ʃuːɻn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
at̪an anajt̪t̪u peɾija panmukat̪t̪anmaj
oɾu paɾan̪t̪a ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪il marrum iɾukkum
kaːɳakkuːʈijat̪u paːɾkkappaʈʈat̪u marrum kalan̪t̪at̪u
oɾu uʈalil  n̪uʈpamaːna arput̪amaːna
pejaɾarraʋat̪u anajt̪t̪umpuɾit̪al

t̪ejʋam
aːnaːl mikaʋum aːt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾijamaːka
t͡ʃiliɾt̪t̪u t̪ikajt̪t̪u t̪ikajt̪t̪u t̪ikajt̪t̪u
aɾd͡ʒunan maɳʈijiʈʈaːn marrum t̪alaj kunin̪t̪u

piɾammaː t̪anijaːka amaɾn̪t̪iɾukkiraːɾ
aʋaɾat̪u t̪aːmaɾaj t͡ʃimmaːt͡ʃanat̪t̪in miːt̪u
t̪uraʋikaɭ marrum muniʋaɾkaɭ marrum paːmpu inaŋkaɭ
anan̪t̪aː ʋaːt͡ʃuki
aːm ʋalimajmikka irajʋan n̪aːn paːɾkkireːn
unat̪u aːjiɾam kaɾaŋkaɭum maːɾpakaŋkaɭum mukaŋkaɭum
marrum kaɳkaɭ  oʋʋaொɾu pakkat̪t̪ilum
t͡ʃaɾijaːna palʋakajppaʈʈa
meːlum unnuʈajja muʈiʋu eŋkum illaj eŋkum aːɾampamum illaj
eŋkum oɾu majjam ʂipʈukaɭil

unat̪u majja t͡ʃujam anajt̪t̪ajjum kajjaːɭʋat̪u marrum anajt̪t̪ajjum ʋenrat̪u

un miːt̪aːna anaːʈem

paொkkiʂamaɾaɳmanaj t͡ʃejjappaʈʈat̪u

arat̪t̪in t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭaj aʈajkkalam

t͡ʃan̪t̪iɾan marrum t̪aŋkat̪t̪in ʋeɭɭi
t͡ʃuːɾijanin makimajkaɭ uɾuɭappaʈukinrana

ʋaːɻkkaj aːt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾijat̪t̪aj t͡ʃuːʈeːrra ʈaோt̪
uŋkaɭ piɾapaɲt͡ʃam ulakaŋkaɭ aːt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾijat̪t̪aːl n̪iɾampijuɭɭana
umat̪u paɾipuːɾaɳaŋkaɭil ʋiɳʋeɭi

aʋaɾkaɭ t̪aŋkaɭ uɭɭaŋkajkaɭaj maʈit̪t̪u kumpiʈukiraːɾkaɭ

ʋat͡ʃus marrum t͡ʃat̪jaːs ʋisʋaːs uʂmapaːs
maːɾuʈs marrum an̪t̪a peɾija iɾaʈʈajjaɾkaɭ
paɾalaோka t͡ʃikappu asʋin
kan̪t̪aɾʋaɾkaɭ ɾaːʈt͡ʃat͡ʃaɾkaɭ t͡ʃit̪t̪aɾkaɭ marrum at͡ʃuɾaɾkaɭ#
iʋaj unnajk kaɳʈu ʋaɳaŋkukinrana
t̪iʈiːɾ pajat̪t̪il
aːm ulakaŋkaɭ  unnat̪amaːna ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪uʈan unnajk kaːɳpat̪u
panmaʈaŋku mukaŋkaɭuʈan
anajʋaɾum paːɾkkum kaɳkaɭaːl
eɳɳarra kaɳkaɭ paɾan̪t̪a kaɾaŋkaɭ piɾamaːɳʈamaːna uruppinaɾkaɭ
t͡ʃuːɾijan marrum n̪aʈt͡ʃat̪t̪iɾat̪t̪aːl oɭiɾum pakkaʋaːʈʈukaɭ
aɾukil marrum t̪aொlajʋil n̪aʈappaʈʈa paːt̪aŋkaɭ
pajat̪t̪in kaொn̪t̪aɭippukaɭ kaோpamaːna marrum menmajjaːna ʋaːjkaɭ
unakku mun muːnru paɾan̪t̪a ulakaŋkaɭ
ʋaɳaŋku n̪aːn unnaj ʋaɳaŋkuʋat̪u paோla
n̪ilan̪aʈukkam n̪aːn n̪ilan̪aʈukkam iʋʋaɭaʋu t͡ʃirappajk kaːɳa
n̪aːn unnaj ʋaːnat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪aːkkuʋat̪ajk kurikkireːn
munpakkat̪t̪uʈan arput̪am ʋaːɾijaːka
peɾija ʋaːnaʋil ʋaɾɳam puːt͡ʃappaʈʈa minnum marrum uŋkaɭ ʋaːj
t̪irakkappaʈʈat̪u marrum paːɾps
ellaːm et̪uʋaːka iɾun̪t̪aːlum
unat̪u anajt̪t̪u ulakaŋkaɭilum kiɻakku meːrku ʋaʈakku marrum t̪erku
kaʈaʋuɭin kaɳkaɭeː t̪alajʋaɾeː
en aːnmaːʋin ʋalimaj oːʈippaோjirru
it̪ajat̪t̪in ʋalimaj paோjʋiʈʈat̪u kaɳʈit̪t̪at̪u manat̪in aːt͡ʃaj
n̪aːn unnaj appaʈi paːɾkkumpaோt̪u
pajaŋkaɾamaːna puɾuʋaŋkaɭuʈan oɭiɾum
eɾijum paːɾʋajjuʈanum n̪eɾuppaːl oɭiɾum ut̪aʈukaɭuʈanum
t̪iːppiɻampukaɭ paோnra kaʈumajjaːna
aɾukileːjeː n̪ukaɾn̪t̪u
puːmi t͡ʃaொɾkkam aʈa n̪aːn n̪aːn puːmijajjum t͡ʃaொɾkkat̪t̪ajjum paːɾkkaʋillaj
aːɳʈaʋaɾeː n̪aːn paːɾkkireːn
n̪iː maʈʈumn̪iː maʈʈum
ippaோt̪u umat̪u kaɾuɳaj enakku ʋaɻaŋkappaʈaʈʈum
ulakat̪t̪in pukaliʈameː
it̪aோ kukajkku ʋiːt͡ʃappaʈʈat̪u
unat̪u akanra t̪aொɳʈaj marrum ʋeɳmajjaːna ut̪aʈukaɭ
eŋkaɭ unnat̪amaːnaʋaɾkaɭaj n̪aːn kaːɳkireːn
peɾija t̪iɾut̪aɾaːʂʈiɾanin makankaɭ
piːʂmaɾ t̪uɾaோɳaɾ kaɾɳan piʈit̪t̪u n̪at͡ʃukkappaʈʈanaɾ
aɾat͡ʃaɾkaɭum t̪alajʋaɾkaɭum uɭɭeː iɻukkappaʈʈanaɾ
uɭɭeː an̪t̪a iʈajʋeɭi paɭɭam
in̪t̪a iɾu paʈajkaɭilum t͡ʃiran̪t̪aʋaj kiɻin̪t̪u kiɻin̪t̪ana
unat̪u t̪aːʈajkaɭukku iʈajjil aʋaj kiʈakkinrana
muɻu iɾat̪t̪am t̪aோjn̪t̪a n̪ilajjil
maɳɳaːkaʋum maɾaɳamaːkaʋum t̪aɾajjiraŋkukirat̪u n̪iːɾaோʈajkaɭ paோla
ut̪aʋijarra aʋat͡ʃaɾat̪t̪uʈan it̪u t͡ʃelkirat̪u
t̪alajkiːɻaːna aːʋeːt͡ʃa oːʈʈat̪t̪il
n̪iɾappappaʈaːt̪a kaʈalin aːɻamaːna pakut̪ikku n̪eːɾaːka
enaʋeː an̪t̪a eɾijum kukajkku
an̪t̪a hiːɾaோkkaɭ peɾijaʋaɾkaɭ marrum t̪ajɾijamaːnaʋaɾkaɭ
muʈiʋarra n̪iːɾaோʈajkaɭil ut̪aʋijarra ijakkat̪t̪uʈan uːrraʋum
iɾaʋil an̪t̪uppuːt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭajp paோla
oɭijaj n̪aோkki paʈapaʈakka
aʋaɾkaɭin umiɻum aɻiʋukku iːɾkkappaʈʈu paran̪t̪u iran̪t̪u
enaʋeː aʋaɾkaɭin maɾaɳam innum t̪uʈikkirat̪u
kuɾuʈaɾ t̪ikajppu uʈan t̪aːŋki
oːjaːmal an̪t̪ak kuːʈʈaŋkaɭ anajt̪t̪um kaːʈʈup parakkinrana
n̪iː at̪u manit̪aɾkaɭaj uɾuʋaːkkijat̪u
aʋarraj miːɳʈum t̪inru
onru marraொnru peɾija marrum t͡ʃirija oɾeː maːt̪iɾijaːka
n̪iː uɾuʋaːkkija ujiɾinaŋkaɭ
eɾijum t̪aːʈajkaɭuʈan n̪iː eʈukka ʋeːɳʈum
aʋaɾkaɭaj maʈit̪t̪al irajʋaː uŋkaɭ pajaŋkaɾaŋkaɭ t̪aːkkukinrana
puːmijin muʈiʋu mut̪al irut̪i ʋaɾaj
pirappiliɾun̪t̪eː ʋaːɻkkajjaj muɻumajjaːka n̪iɾapput̪al
maɾaɳat̪t̪irku kaொʈija eɾijum man̪t̪amaːna at͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪uʈan
aː ʋiʂɳu enakku t̪eɾijappaʈut̪t̪u
unat̪u t̪aோrram eːn ippaʈi iɾukkirat̪u
iran̪t̪aʋaɾaj iʋʋaːru ʋiɾun̪t̪u ʋajkkum n̪iː jaːɾ
 pajaŋkaɾamaːna t̪ejʋam
n̪aːn unnaj ʋaɳaŋkukireːn
n̪amaோst̪u t̪eː t̪eːʋaʋaɾaː piɾat͡ʃit̪#
oː ʋalla irajʋaneː ot̪t̪ikaj
n̪iːŋkaɭ eːn iʋʋaɭaʋu kaொʈuːɾamaːka et̪iɾkaொɳʈiːɾkaɭ
in̪t̪a pajaŋkaɾamaːna amt͡ʃam eŋkiɾun̪t̪u t̪aொʈaɾkirat̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
n̪iː ennajk kaொllum n̪eːɾamaːkap paːɾkkiraːj
anajt̪t̪ajjum aɻiʋukkuk kaொɳʈuʋaɾum n̪eːɾam
t̪i sleːjaɾ ʈajm paɳʈajja kaːlaŋkaɭ iŋku ʋan̪t̪u n̪ukaɾkinrana
unnajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa ʋaɾit͡ʃajppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈa in̪t̪a ʋiɾaோt̪ikaɭin t̪alajʋaɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪ilum
paோɾkkaɭat̪t̪aj jaːɾum ujiɾuʈan ʋiʈamaːʈʈaːɾkaɭ t̪ikajt̪t̪eːn
ini iɾukkaːt̪eː eɻun̪t̪iɾu pukaɻ pera un et̪iɾikaɭaj aɻit̪t̪uʋiʈu
n̪iːŋkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭaj ʋenraʋuʈan uŋkaɭukkaːka kaːt̪t̪iɾukkum ɾaːd͡ʒjat̪t̪irkaːka paோɾaːʈuŋkaɭ
ennaːleːjeː aʋaj ʋiɻukinrana  unnaːl alla maɾaɳat̪t̪in pakkaʋaːt̪am aʋaɾkaɭukku ippaோt̪u t̪iːɾkkappaʈʈat̪u
aʋaɾkaɭ iʋʋaːru kalaːʈʈaː kaːʈʈinaːlum en kaɾuʋi n̪iːjeː
palamaːna aːjut̪am kaொɳʈa iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾeː t̪uɾaோɳaɾajt̪ t̪aːkkuŋkaɭ piːʂmaɾ t̪aːkkut̪alil maɾaɳat̪t̪aj t͡ʃamaːɭikka
kaɾɳan miːt̪u d͡ʒajat̪ɾat̪an aʋaɾkaɭin paோɾ muːt͡ʃt͡ʃaːka iɾuŋkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭaj aɻijat͡ʃ t͡ʃaொnnaʋan n̪aːneː kaொllappaʈʈaʋaɾkaɭajk kaொlʋiːɾkaɭ
t͡ʃaɳʈaj aʋaɾkaɭ ʋiɻa ʋeːɳʈum n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋaːɻa ʋeːɳʈum in̪t̪a t͡ʃamaʋeɭijil ʋerri
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
ʋalimajmikka keːt͡ʃaʋaɾin ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjajk keːʈʈu
n̪aʈukkat̪t̪uʈan enru t̪alajjat͡ʃajt̪t̪aːɾ irajʋan
t̪uːkkija uɭɭaŋkajkaɭajp parrikkaொɳʈu piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj t͡ʃejt̪aːn
kiɾuʂɳaɾin aɾuɭ  aŋkeː n̪inru
kunin̪t̪a puɾuʋam marrum ut͡ʃt͡ʃaɾippukaɭ uʈajn̪t̪a n̪ilajjil
in̪t̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ t̪ajakkat̪t̪uʈan peːt͡ʃappaʈukinrana
aɾd͡ʒunaː
t̪akut̪ijaːnaʋan ʋallamajjin irajʋaneː
ulakam muɻuʋat̪um makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
umat̪u at̪iːt̪a t͡ʃakt̪ijil umakkuk kiːɻppaʈit̪al
ɾaːʈt͡ʃat͡ʃaɾkaɭ at͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪il
unnajp paːɾt̪t̪at̪um ʋeːkamaːj oːʈukirat̪u
n̪aːnku pakut̪ikaɭukkum marrum n̪iruʋanam
t͡ʃit̪t̪aɾkaɭ umat̪u pejaɾaj olikkiraːɾkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ eppaʈi ariʋikkakkuːʈaːt̪u
uŋkaɭ maːɳpukaɭ t̪ejʋiːkamaːna ʋalimajmikkat̪aː
n̪iː piɾammaː piɾammat̪t̪aj ʋiʈa peɾijaʋan
ellajjarra paʈajppaːɭijeː
t̪ejʋaŋkaɭin kaʈaʋuɭeː ʋaːɻʋin iɾuppiʈam marrum oːjʋu
n̪iːjeː anajt̪t̪u aːnmaːkkaɭin aːnmaː
puɾin̪t̪ukaொɭɭum muɻumaj
uɾuʋaːnaʋaɾ marrum uɾuʋamarraʋaɾaːka iɾuppat̪u kaʈʈamajppaːɭaɾ
oː unnat̪amaːnaʋaɾeː aːɳʈaʋaɾeː
paɻajja ʋiʈa paɻajja jaːɾ t͡ʃeːmit̪t̪u
ʋaːɻʋu ʋaɭam kaொɳʈa ulakaŋkaɭeː put̪ajjal uɾimajjaːɭaɾeː
jaːɾ anajt̪t̪u marrum kalaj 
ɲaːnam n̪iːjeː  pakut̪i
anajt̪t̪u marrum anajt̪t̪u eːnenil unniʈamiɾun̪t̪u anajʋaɾum ujiɾt̪t̪eɻun̪t̪anaɾ
eɳɳarrat̪u ippaோt̪u paːɾkkireːn
amt͡ʃaŋkaɭ unnuʈajjat̪u
ʋaːju# n̪iːjeː t͡ʃirajjaj ʋajt̪t̪iɾuppaʋan
n̪aɾakkin jama iɾuɳʈa
meːlum aknijin oɭiɾum t̪iːppaொri
ʋaɾuɳanin alajkaɭ unat̪u alajkaɭ t͡ʃan̪t̪iɾanum n̪aʈt͡ʃat̪t̪iɾa oɭijum
unnuʈajjaʋaj piɾad͡ʒaːpat̪i
n̪iːjaː at̪u unakku
aʋaɾkaɭ paɻajja ulakin t̪uːɾa oɭijaj ʋaɳaŋki maɳʈijiʈʈanaɾ
maɾaɳa manit̪aɾkaɭil mut̪anmajjaːnaʋaɾ
miːɳʈum kaʈaʋuɭeː miːɳʈum
aːjiɾam aːjiɾam maʈaŋku peɾit̪aːkkappaʈum
maɾijaːt̪aj marrum ʋaɻipaːʈu 
makimajjum pukaɻum unakkeː
n̪amaோ n̪amast̪eː enru oʋʋaொɾu pakkamum aɻut̪aːɾkaɭ
iŋkeː meːleː kiːɻeː aɻut̪eːn
n̪iː paோkum paோt̪u t͡ʃaொnnat̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ eŋku ʋaɾuʋiːɾkaɭ enru kuːrinaːɾ n̪amaோ n̪aːŋkaɭ aɻajkkiroːm
n̪amaோst̪u kaʈaʋuɭ paோrrinaːɾ
n̪amaோst̪u pejaɾ t̪eɾijaːt̪a irajʋaneː
unakku ʋaɳakkam umakkeː paோrri ellaːʋarrilum n̪iː oɾuʋan
eːnenraːl n̪iːŋkaɭ ellaːm aːm n̪iː
aː ippaோt̪u kaோpat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪aːl
n̪aːn unnaj n̪aɳpan enru n̪inajt̪t̪eːn enpat̪aj n̪iː n̪inajʋil ʋajt̪t̪iɾukka ʋeːɳʈum
eɭimajjaːna peːt͡ʃt͡ʃil peːt͡ʃuʋat̪u
aːɳkaɭ oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾukkum oʋʋaொnrajjum pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪u paோla
unnaj kiɾuʂɳaː iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃan enru aɻajt̪t̪aːnaː allat̪u puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭaʋillaj
unnuʈajja marajʋaːna makimaj
ʋallamaj unnuʈajja piɾamippu
t͡ʃejt̪eːn en alaʈt͡ʃijat̪t̪il allat̪u en kaːt̪alil
pajaɳat̪t̪il allat̪u keːli
allat̪u n̪aːm oːjʋil iɾukkumpaோt̪u
t͡ʃapajjil amaɾn̪t̪u t̪aோppil ʋaɻit̪aʋari
t̪anijaːkaʋaோ kuːʈʈamaːkaʋaோ
n̪iː t͡ʃej mika paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪am t̪aʋaru
an̪t̪a ajaோkkija paːʋat̪t̪irku umat̪u aɾuɭ kiʈajkkaʈʈum
n̪iːŋkaɭ ippaோt̪u enakku t̪eɾijum
kiːɻeː uɭɭa anajʋaɾukkum t̪an̪t̪aj
meːleː uɭɭa ellaːʋarrilum uɭɭeː iɾukkum anajt̪t̪u ulakaŋkaɭilum
kuɾukkaɭin kuɾu meːlum
ʋaɳaŋkuʋat̪arkum ʋaɳaŋkuʋat̪arkum
apimaːnam marrum ujaɾn̪t̪a anajt̪t̪ajjum ʋiʈa
eppaʈi paɾan̪t̪a ulakaŋkaɭ muːnru
t͡ʃamamaːka iɾukka ʋeːɳʈumaː
uŋkaɭ maːʈt͡ʃimajjaj ʋeːru jaːɾaːʋat̪u pakiɾn̪t̪u kaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈumaː
enaʋeː uʈal ʋaɭajn̪t̪a n̪ilajjil
marrum maɾijaːt̪ajkkuɾija n̪aோkkam
n̪aːn t̪ut̪ikkireːn t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejkireːn unnajt̪ t̪eːʈukireːn aɾuɭajk keːʈkireːn
oɾu makanukku t̪an̪t̪ajjaːka
n̪aɳpaɾukku n̪aɳpaɾaːka oɾuʋaɾaːka
t̪an kaːt̪alaniʈam anpu kaːʈʈukiraʋan un mukat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾuppikkaொɭ
en miːt̪u menmajjil
n̪allat̪u n̪aːn paːɾt̪t̪eːn
un ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪in in̪t̪a arijappaʈaːt̪a arput̪am aːnaːl pajam
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijil kalakkirat̪u miːɳʈum eʈut̪t̪u
anpeː irajʋaː paɾit̪aːpat̪t̪irkaːka
puːmikkuɾija kaɳkaɭ t̪aːŋkakkuːʈija uŋkaɭ puːmikkuɾija ʋaʈiʋam
iɾakkamaːjiɾuŋkaɭ kaːʈʈuŋkaɭ
n̪aːn arin̪t̪a kaːʈt͡ʃi
n̪aːn unnaj munpu paோl ʋaɾit͡ʃajjaːka kaɾut̪ukireːn
ʋaʈʈu marrum n̪erri ɾat̪t̪inat̪t̪uʈan
t͡ʃuːlaːjut̪am marrum anaːʈem uʈan
anajt̪t̪ajjum t̪aːŋkupaʋaneː t̪ikajkkaʋillaj
miːɳʈum oɾumuraj paːɾkkireːn
paɻaŋkaːlat̪t̪il n̪aːn ʋiɾumpija ʋaʈiʋam
aːjiɾam kaɾaŋkaɭilum eɳɳarra kaɳkaɭilum n̪iːjeː
in̪t̪a pajan̪t̪a it̪ajam palaʋiːnamaːnat̪u
miːʈʈeʈut̪t̪at̪aj miːɳʈum paːɾkka
en t̪eːɾaோʈʈi kiɾuʂɳaɾin ʋakajjaːna maːruʋeːʈat̪t̪il
kiɾuʂɳaː
aːm n̪iː paːɾt̪t̪aːj aɾd͡ʒunaː n̪aːn unnaj n̪anraːka n̪eːt͡ʃit̪t̪at̪aːl
maːja man̪t̪iɾat̪t̪aːl ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈa en ɾakat͡ʃija mukam
piɾakaːt͡ʃamaːna marrum arput̪amaːna marrum paɾan̪t̪a kampiːɾamaːna panmaʈaŋku
ellaː ʋaɾuʂaŋkaɭilum unnajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa ʋeːru jaːɾukkumeː paːɾkka t̪ajaʋu illaj
eːnenil it̪u ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭaːl ʋaɾaʋillaj jaːkamaோ t̪aːnamaோ ʋaɾaːt̪u
n̪anraːkat͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪illaj n̪iːɳʈa n̪eːɾam t̪aʋam t͡ʃejʋat̪illaj d͡ʒepaŋkaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪illaj eːɭanam t͡ʃejʋat̪illaj
t͡ʃaŋkiːt̪am
aɻijaːt̪a aːt̪maːʋaj aːʈajjinrip paːɾkka an̪t̪a maɾaɳak kaɳkaɭ t̪aːŋka ʋeːɳʈum
kuɾukkaɭin iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː it̪u unakkaːka maʈʈumeː ʋajkkappaʈʈat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːka iɾu
un kaɳkaɭ paːɾt̪t̪apaʈijaːl ini un iɾut̪ajat̪t̪aj at͡ʃajkka ʋeːɳʈaːm
en makimajjuʈan en pajaŋkaɾam n̪aːn munpu iɾun̪t̪at̪ajp paோlaʋeː
appaʈijeː n̪aːn miːɳʈum unakkaːka iɾuppeːn iɭakija it̪ajat̪t̪uʈan paːɾ
miːɳʈum oɾumuraj n̪aːn unat̪u kiɾuʂɳan unakkut̪ t̪eɾin̪t̪a ʋaʈiʋam
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
in̪t̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ aɾd͡ʒunaniʈam peːt͡ʃappaʈʈat̪u
ʋaːt͡ʃut̪eːʋ n̪eːɾaːka eʈut̪t̪aːɾ
miːɳʈum miːɳʈum t͡ʃaːjal anpeː
n̪anku ʋiɾumpappaʈʈa t̪eːɾaோʈʈijin
amajt̪ijajjum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajjum at̪u miːʈʈeʈut̪t̪at̪u
iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ miːɳʈum oɾumuraj paːɾt̪t̪apaோt̪u
ʋalimajmikka piɾammaːʋin ʋaʈiʋamum mukamum
kiɾuʂɳaɾin menmajjaːna kaɾuɳajjil aːʈaj aɳin̪t̪aʋaɾ
aɾd͡ʒunaː
ippaோt̪u t̪iɾumpi ʋaɾuʋat̪ajp paːɾkkireːn d͡ʒanaːɾt̪anaː
in̪t̪a n̪aʈpu manit̪a t͡ʃaʈʈat̪t̪aj en manam t͡ʃin̪t̪ikka muʈijum
miːɳʈum oɾumuraj amajt̪ijaːna eɳɳaŋkaɭ en it̪ajam miːɳʈum t̪uʈikkirat̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
aːm at̪u arput̪amaːkaʋum pajaŋkaɾamaːkaʋum iɾun̪t̪at̪u
n̪iː paːɾt̪t̪at̪ajp paோlaʋeː ennajp paːɾkka anpaːna iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː kaʈaʋuɭkaɭ
t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u paːɾkka at͡ʃt͡ʃamum aːt͡ʃajjum
aːjinum ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭaːl alla jaːkat̪t̪aːl alla
t̪aʋamaோ anpaɭippukaɭaோ piɾaːɾt̪t̪anajjaோ alla
n̪iː paːɾt̪t̪apaʈi jaːɾaːʋat̪u paːɾkkalaːmaː
muɻumajjaːna t͡ʃeːʋaj paɾipuːɾaɳa n̪ampikkajjaːl maʈʈumeː
meːlum murrilum t͡ʃaɾaɳaːkat̪i n̪aːn arijappaʈʈaʋan
in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ paːɾt̪t̪aːɾ uɭɭeː n̪uɻajn̪t̪aːɾ
enakkaːka anajt̪t̪ajjum t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ jaːɾ ennajk kaɳʈupiʈippaːɾkaɭ
aːkamot̪t̪am eppaோt̪um ʋaɳaŋkukirat̪u anajt̪t̪ajjum n̪eːt͡ʃikkiraːɾ
anpin oɾeː muʈiʋirkaːka n̪aːn uɾuʋaːkkijat̪u marrum n̪aːn
an̪t̪a manit̪an aɾd͡ʒunaː ennaj n̪aோkki t͡ʃelkirat̪u
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
ʋisʋaɾuːpat̪aɾt͡ʃanam enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u onrajjum panmukat̪t̪anmajjajjum ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪um put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
irajʋaː umakku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjum manit̪aɾkaɭinuɳmajjaːna uɭɭat̪t̪il
kaʈaʋuɭ ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪ijapaʈi marrum t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejjum aːɳkaɭin
ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈaːt̪a uʈalarra t̪uːɾamaːna unnaj ʋaɳaŋkut̪al
n̪ampikkaj marrum ʋaːɻkkajjin t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ʋaɻi et̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
enakku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ  n̪aːn kaːʈʈuʋat̪u paோl 
t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u uɳmaj muɻu pakt̪ijil n̪ilajjaːnat̪u
aʋaɾkaɭ ennaj mikaʋum punit̪amaːka kaɾut̪ukinranaɾ aːnaːl jaːɾ t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ 
kaɳɳukku t̪eɾijaːt̪a oɾuʋaneː ennaj ʋaɳaŋkukireːn
ʋeɭippaʈut̪t̪appaʈaːt̪a pejaɾiʈappaʈaːt̪a t͡ʃin̪t̪ikka muʈijaːt̪a
murrum muɻut̪um n̪irajn̪t̪at̪u ujaɾn̪t̪at̪u urut̪ijaːnat̪u
iʋʋaːru ennaj ʋaɳaŋkupaʋaɾkaɭ t̪aŋkaɭ uɳaɾʋil t̪eːɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi perukiraːɾkaɭ
anajʋaɾukkum oɾeː manat̪aːka ellaː n̪anmajkaɭilum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
in̪t̪a aːt͡ʃiːɾʋat̪ikkappaʈʈa aːt̪maːkkaɭ enniʈam ʋaɾukiraːɾkaɭ
aːnaːlum kaʈinamaːnat̪u
manat̪aj ʋaɭajppaʋaɾkaɭukkeː t̪unpam
  enru paːɾʋajjarra paːt̪ajjaj aʈajja
t͡ʃat̪ajjajt͡ʃ t͡ʃumakkum manit̪anaːl mit̪ikkappaʈuʋat̪u kurajʋu
aːnaːl eʋanum t̪an t͡ʃejalkaɭajjellaːm t͡ʃejkiraːn
enakkaːka t̪annajt̪ t̪urappat̪u ennil n̪irajn̪t̪at̪u n̪ilajjaːnat̪u
iɾaʋum pakalum ujaɾn̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭukku maʈʈumeː t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum
ennajp parri jaோt͡ʃit̪t̪u  n̪aːn aʋaɾaj ʋiɾajʋaːka ujaɾt̪t̪uʋeːn
t̪unpam marrum maɾaɳam enra ʋaːɻkkajjin kaʈalil iɾun̪t̪u
jaːɾuʈajja aːnmaː ennaோʈu oʈʈikkaொɳʈiɾukkirat̪u ennajp parrikkaொɭ
it̪ajat̪t̪aːlum manat̪aːlum ennajk kajppiʈi at̪anaːl n̪iː kuʈijiɾuppaːj
n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka ennuʈan ujaɾat̪t̪il aːnaːl uŋkaɭ eɳɳam enraːl
at̪t̪akajja ujaɾat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u t̪uɭikaɭ n̪iːŋkaɭ amajkka palaʋiːnamaːka iɾun̪t̪aːl
uʈalum aːnmaːʋum t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u en miːt̪u
ʋiɾakt̪ijaʈajja ʋeːɳʈaːm enakku kurajn̪t̪a t͡ʃeːʋaj kaொʈu t̪eːʈuŋkaɭ
ennaj aʈajja urut̪ijaːna ʋiɾuppat̪t̪uʈan ʋaɳaŋkut̪al
meːlum n̪iːŋkaɭ urut̪ijaːka ʋaɳaŋka muʈijaːʋiʈʈaːl
enakkaːka ʋeːlaj t͡ʃej enakku ʋiɾuppamaːna t͡ʃejalkaɭil uɻaj
eːnenraːl enmiːt̪u anpu t͡ʃelut̪t̪uʋat̪arkaːka uɻajkkiraʋan
irut̪ijaːka aʈajjum aːnaːl it̪il iɾun̪t̪aːl
uŋkaɭ it̪ajam t͡ʃejaliɻakkirat̪u uŋkaɭ t̪aோlʋijaj enniʈam kaொɳʈu ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ kaɳʈupiʈikka
ennil aʈajkkalam uɻajppin palankaɭ paோkaʈʈum
enakkaːna n̪ampikkajjajt̪ t̪uran̪t̪u t̪aːɻmajjaːna it̪ajat̪t̪uʈan
enaʋeː n̪iː ʋaː eːnenil t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭʋat̪u innum at̪ikam
ʋiʈaːmujart͡ʃijaj ʋiʈa ʋaɻipaːʈu t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
t̪eɾin̪t̪ukaொɭʋat̪aj ʋiʈa t̪urappat̪u innum t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
t̪urappat̪arku aɾukil  mika aɾukil 
n̪it̪t̪ija amajt̪i ʋaːɻka
et̪ajjum ʋerukkaːt̪aʋaɾ
ujiɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪ilum t̪annajt̪ t̪aːneː n̪allaʋanaːka ʋaːɻka
iɾakkamuɭɭaʋaɾ aːɳaʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋilakku
t͡ʃuja anpiliɾun̪t̪u ʋilakku maːraːt̪at̪u
n̪allat̪u allat̪u keʈʈat̪u paொrumaj t̪iɾupt̪i urut̪ijaːna
ʋit͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃat̪t̪il t̪annajt̪ t̪aːneː t̪eːɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi perru t̪an ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkku uɳmajjaːka
ennaj n̪aːʈuʋat̪u it̪ajam marrum aːnmaː enakku t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejt̪eːn
n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkum an̪t̪a manit̪an t̪an inat̪t̪aj t̪aொn̪t̪aɾaʋu t͡ʃejjaːt̪aʋaɾ
meːlum aʋaɾkaɭaːl t̪aொn̪t̪aɾaʋu t͡ʃejjappaʈaʋillaj kaோpat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u t̪eɭiʋaːka
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi t̪ukkam allat̪u pajam aːkijaʋarrirku mika at̪ikamaːka ʋaːɻʋat̪u
n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkum an̪t̪a manit̪an jaːɾ amajt̪ijaːna kaɳkaɭuʈan ʋat͡ʃikkiraːɾ#
t̪uɾuppiʈikkaːt̪a amajt̪ijaːna n̪anku t͡ʃaman̪ilajjaːna kuɻappamillaːt̪a
ennuʈan ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejt̪aːlum ellaː ʋeːlajkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um piɾin̪t̪u
n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkum an̪t̪a manit̪an en miːt̪u n̪ampikkaj ʋajt̪t̪aʋaɾ
jaːɾajjum ʋiɾumpuʋat̪illaj jaːɾajjum t̪uːrruʋat̪illaj makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi illaj
meːlum t̪ukkappaʈuʋat̪illaj n̪allat̪u allat̪u t̪iːmajjaj ʋiʈaːmal
at̪u iɾukkum paோt̪u ʋeɭit͡ʃt͡ʃam at̪u eppaோt̪u purappaʈum
n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkum an̪t̪a manit̪an jaːɾ n̪aɳpaɾ marrum et̪iɾikku
t͡ʃamamaːna manat̪uʈan t͡ʃamamaːna it̪ajat̪t̪aj ʋajt̪t̪iɾut̪t̪al
aʋamaːnat̪t̪ajjum peɾumajjajjum t̪aːŋkukirat̪u t͡ʃama amajt̪ijuʈan
ʋeppam marrum kuɭiɾ inpam marrum t̪unpat̪t̪aj eʈukkum n̪ilajt̪t̪u n̪irkirat̪u
aːt͡ʃajkaɭaj ʋiʈʈu ʋiʈuŋkaɭ pukaɻ allat̪u aʋat̪uːrukaɭajk keːʈkalaːm
uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijarra kaʈʈuppaːʈʈil oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾaːlum at͡ʃajjaːt̪u
puːmijuʈan en̪t̪a pan̪t̪amum illaːmal iɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u ennil urut̪ijaːka
n̪aːn n̪eːt͡ʃikkum an̪t̪a manit̪an aːnaːl ellaːʋarrirkum meːlaːka n̪aːn ʋiɾumpukireːn
jaːɾukku ʋaːɻʋat̪u enpat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːnaʋaɾkaɭ
oɾeː t̪iːʋiɾamaːna n̪ampikkajjilum kaːɳaːt̪a anpilum
ennuʈajja aːt͡ʃiːɾʋat̪ikkappaʈʈa amiɾt̪at̪t̪ajp paɾukukireːn
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
pakt̪ijaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u n̪ampikkajjin mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
ippaோt̪u n̪aːn keːʈkireːn kaɾuɳajjuɭɭa keːt͡ʃaʋaː#
t̪aோrramaɭikkum ʋaːɻkkaj marrum at̪arku appaːl uɭɭa aːt̪maː
at̪u n̪amakku enna t̪eɾijum  allat̪u t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa n̪inajkkiraோm
kiɾuʂɳaː
aːm kun̪t̪ijin makaneː in̪t̪a maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪irkaːka n̪iːŋkaɭ paːɾkkiriːɾkaɭ
kʂeːt̪ɾaː enpat̪u d͡ʒiːʋan paɾaʋum kaɭam
meːlum et̪ajp paːɾkkirat̪aோ at̪uʋeː aːt̪maːʋaːkum
kʂeːt̪ɾad͡ʒɲaː ellaː t̪urajkaɭilum in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
n̪aːn kʂeːt̪ɾad͡ʒɲan n̪aːn enna aːjʋukaɭ
et̪u t̪eɾin̪t̪at̪u enpat̪aj an̪t̪a ariʋu maʈʈumeː arijum
arin̪t̪aʋaɾ muːlam# at̪u enna ʋaːɻʋin an̪t̪a pulam
it̪u enna kuɳaŋkaɭajk kaொɳʈuɭɭat̪u at̪u eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u
at̪u eːn maːrukirat̪u marrum aːt͡ʃiɾijaɾ
it̪u it̪an ʋalimajjaj uɳaɾt̪t̪ukirat̪u
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u in̪t̪a ʋiʂajaŋkaɭajk keːʈpat̪u eppaʈi
           #
kuːrukaɭ uɳaɾʋu ʋaːɻkkaj manam
kaɳɳukku t̪eɾijaːt̪a mukkija t͡ʃakt̪i onpat̪u ʋit͡ʃit̪t̪iɾamaːna ʋaːjilkaɭ
uʈal marrum uɳaɾʋin ajn̪t̪u kaɭaŋkaɭ
aːt͡ʃaj ʋeruppu inpam marrum t̪unpam marrum t͡ʃin̪t̪anaj
aːɻamaːka n̪ejjappaʈʈa marrum iɾuppat̪il n̪ilajt̪t̪anmaj
iʋaj anajt̪t̪um aːnmaːʋaːl paொɾuɭin aʈippaʈajjil uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈaʋaj
paɳiʋu uɳmaj marrum t̪iːŋkarra t̪anmaj
paொrumaj marrum maɾijaːt̪aj ɲaːnikaɭukku maɾijaːt̪aj
t̪uːjmaj n̪ilajt̪t̪anmaj t͡ʃuja kaʈʈuppaːʈu
uɳaɾʋuinpaŋkaɭaj aʋamat̪it̪t̪al t͡ʃuja t̪ijaːkam
n̪aோjʋaːjppaʈʈat̪arkaːna t͡ʃaːnrit̪aɻin kaɾut̪t̪u
pirappu irappu ʋajat̪u n̪aோj t̪unpam marrum paːʋat̪t̪il
parrinmaj ʋiːʈʈaj leːt͡ʃaːkap piʈit̪t̪uk kaொɳʈu
kuɻan̪t̪ajkaɭ marrum manajʋi marrum aːɳkaɭaj piɳajkkum anajt̪t̪um
n̪alla at̪iɾʂʈat̪t̪il eppaோt̪um amajt̪ijaːna it̪ajam
marrum at̪iɾʂʈam t̪iːmaj urut̪ijaːna oɾu ʋiɾuppat̪t̪uʈan
ennaj ʋaɳaŋkuʋat̪arku  ennaj maʈʈumeː n̪irut̪t̪aʋillaj
ellaː t̪animajkaɭajjum n̪eːt͡ʃippat̪u t͡ʃat̪t̪at̪t̪aj t̪aʋiɾppat̪u
muʈʈaːɭ kuːʈʈam urut̪ijaːna mujart͡ʃikaɭ
unnat̪a aːt̪maːʋin uɳaɾʋaj aʈajja
at̪u enna aːt̪aːjam enpat̪aj puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa aɾuɭ
enaʋeː aʈajja  it̪u uɳmajjaːna ɲaːnam iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
marrapaʈi arijaːmajjeː
ippaோt̪u n̪aːn ariʋat̪arku t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ariʋajp parri peːt͡ʃuʋeːn
an̪t̪a uɳmaj manit̪anukku amiɾt̪at̪t̪ajk kuʈikkak kaொʈut̪t̪at̪u
aʋanuʈajja uɳmaj paɾapiɾammam anajt̪t̪um
uɾuʋaːkkappaʈaːt̪at̪u at͡ʃat̪ alla t͡ʃat̪ alla
ʋaʈiʋam alla allat̪u uɾuʋaːkkappaʈaːt̪at̪u innum iɾaɳʈum meːlum
jaːɾuʈajja kajkaɭ ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum uɭɭana
aʋaɾ kaːlkaɭaj n̪aʈʈaːɾ aʋaɾuʈajja kaɳkaɭ eŋkum
paːɾkkiraːɾ ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum aʋaɾuʈajja kaːt̪ukaɭ
keːʈpat̪u marrum ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum aʋaɾat̪u mukaŋkaɭ
aʋanat̪u ulakaŋkaɭaj ariʋuːʈʈuʋat̪um t͡ʃuːɻʋat̪um
aʋaɾ kaொʈut̪t̪a pulankaɭaːl makimajppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈaːɾ
innum uɳaɾʋukku appaːrpaʈʈaʋaɾ aʋaɾ anajt̪t̪ajjum t̪aːŋki
innum aʋaɾ iɳajkkappaʈaːmal ʋaːɻkiraːɾ ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭ marrum murajkaɭ
ed͡ʒamaːnaɾeː innum aʋaɾukku ʋaʈiʋamaோ murajjaோ illaj
aʋaɾ ellaː ujiɾkaɭukkuɭɭum  marrum illaːmal  iɾukkiraːɾ
at͡ʃajjaːt̪u innum n̪akaɾkirat̪u kaɳʈukaொɭɭaʋillaj
uʈanaʈi iɾuppin n̪uɳukkat̪t̪irkaːka n̪eɾukkamaːna
anajʋaɾukkum oʋʋaொɾuʋaɾukkum innum aɭaʋarra t̪uːɾam
panmaʈaŋku illaj innum ʋaːɻkirat̪u
ʋaːɻum anajt̪t̪ilum enrenrum arijappaʈum
n̪ilajt̪t̪iɾuppaʋaɾaːka innum kaːlat̪t̪in irut̪ijil
aʋaɾ anajt̪t̪ajjum muʈikkiraːɾ  miːɳʈum uɾuʋaːkkukiraːɾ
oɭijin oɭi aʋaɾ iɾuɭin it̪ajat̪t̪il iɾukkiraːɾ
n̪it̪t̪ijamaːka oɭiɾkirat̪u ɲaːnam aʋaɾ
ɲaːnat̪t̪in ʋaɻijum ɲaːnikaɭukkellaːm ʋaɻikaːʈʈijum
oʋʋaொɾu it̪ajat̪t̪ilum ʋit̪ajkkappaʈukirat̪u
at̪anaːl n̪aːn t͡ʃaொllijiɾukkireːn
ʋaːɻkkajjin paொɾuɭ marrum ʋaːɾppu marrum puɾaːɳam
puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa jaːɾ ennaj ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾkaɭ
it̪aj uɳaɾn̪t̪aːl n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka enniʈam ʋaɾum
ijarkaj marrum aːʋi iɾaɳʈum enpat̪aj n̪iː ariʋaːj
aːɾampam illaj an̪t̪a kuɳaŋkaɭaj arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
meːlum aʋarrin maːrraŋkaɭ ijarkajjaːl uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈaʋaj
ijarkajjaːnat̪u n̪aʈippu t͡ʃaʈʈat̪t̪aj ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejja ʋajkkirat̪u
aːnaːl aːʋijaːnaʋaɾ at̪aj ariʋikkiraːɾ at̪anaːl eːrpaʈut̪t̪ukiraːɾ
ʋali marrum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijin uɳaɾʋu aːʋi iɳajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
ʋaːɾkkappaʈʈa paொɾuɭukku piɳajppil n̪uɻajkirat̪u
ijarkajjaːl kaʈʈamajkkappaʈʈa kuɳaŋkaɭuʈan marrum iʋʋaːru
ʋiʂajam t̪iɾumaɳam miːɳʈum pirappu inappeɾukkam
n̪alla allat̪u t̪iːja jaோnisil#
aːnaːlum it̪ut̪aːn
aːm at̪an uʈal t͡ʃirajjilaːnmaː t̪uːja
aːnmaː ut͡ʃt͡ʃam aːjʋu aːʈt͡ʃi
kaːʋal uʈajmaj irajʋan marrum kuɾu innum
puɾuʂaː alʈimeːʈ ennuʈan oɾu aːt̪maː
iʋʋaːru t̪annaj aripaʋan t̪an aːnmaːʋaj ariʋaːn
puɾuʂaː kuɳaŋkaɭin muːlam t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːɾ
ijarkajjin murajkaɭaːl aʋaɾukku ʋeɭit͡ʃt͡ʃam ʋan̪t̪uʋiʈʈat̪u
aʋaɾ en̪t̪a t͡ʃat̪ajjaj t͡ʃuman̪t̪aːlum ini oɾupaோt̪um
aʋaɾ at̪an t͡ʃumajjaj eːrrukkaொɭʋaːɾaː t͡ʃila t͡ʃila uɭɭana
t̪ijaːnat̪t̪in muːlam aːnmaːʋaj t͡ʃujamaːka kaɳʈarijaʋum
t͡ʃuja kalʋi marrum t͡ʃila n̪iːɳʈa t̪at̪t̪uʋat̪t̪aːl
meːlum punit̪a ʋaːɻʋu aŋku t͡ʃenraʈajjum t͡ʃila paʈajppukaɭ muːlam
t͡ʃilaɾ oɾupaோt̪um aʋʋaːru aʈajja maːʈʈaːɾkaɭ oɭijajk keːʈkiraːɾkaɭ
marra ut̪aʈukaɭil iɾun̪t̪u marrum kajpparri at̪aj oʈʈikkaொɭɭaʋum
ʋaɻipaʈut̪al aːm marrum an̪t̪uɳmajjaːna paோt̪anajkku
oːʋaɾ paːs maɾaɳam
eŋkiɾun̪t̪aːlum in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
ʋaːɻkkaj enpat̪u n̪akaɾum paொɾuɭkaɭ allat̪u at͡ʃajjaːt̪a ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ
aːlaj allat̪u innum ʋit̪aj  t̪eɾijum aŋku enna ʋaɭaɾn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
paொɾuɭ marrum aːʋijin piɳajppinaːl t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
anajʋaɾajjum oɾeː maːt̪iɾijaːkap paːɾppaʋaɾ uɳmajjil paːɾkkiraːɾ
ʋaːɻum iraj aːt̪maː aːnmaː ut͡ʃt͡ʃam
aɻin̪t̪u paோʋat̪arku mat̪t̪ijil aɻijaːt̪at̪u
eːnenil oʋʋaொɾu iʈat̪t̪ilum iʋʋaːru paːɾkkiraʋaɾ
oʋʋaொɾu ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪ilum oɾeː onru ʋaːɻum ʋaːɻkkaj
ini t̪anakkut̪t̪aːneː an̪ijaːjam t͡ʃejt̪u kaொɭɭaːt̪eː
aːnaːl mika ujaɾn̪t̪a paːt̪ajjil t͡ʃelkirat̪u at̪u peːɾinpat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪aɾukirat̪u
paːɾt̪t̪al aʋaɾ paːɾkkiraːɾ uɳmajjil jaːɾ ʋeːlaj paːɾkkiraːɾkaɭ enru
aːnmaː pajirt͡ʃi t͡ʃejja ijarkajjin ʋaɻakkam
n̪aʈippu innum mukaʋaɾaːka illaj n̪iraj paːɾkkirat̪u
t̪anit̪t̪ani ujiɾinaŋkaɭ  oʋʋaொnrum at̪an ʋakaj 
onriliɾun̪t̪u ʋeɭiʋan̪t̪u miːɳʈum onril kalakkaʋum
pinnaɾ aʋaɾ piɾammat̪t̪aj aʈajn̪t̪aːɾ aʋaɾ aʈajkiraːɾ
iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
an̪t̪a irut̪i ujaɾ aːʋi uɾuʋaːkkaːt̪a
at̪u maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪il n̪uɻajn̪t̪aːlum t̪akut̪ijarrat̪u
t͡ʃejalkaɭin karajjaj eʈukkaːt̪u ʋiːɳaːka ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejjaːt̪u
anajt̪t̪ilum ʋijaːpit̪t̪iɾukkum at̪iːt̪ak kaːrrajp paோla
it̪u t͡ʃut̪t̪a n̪uɳukkat̪t̪irkaːka kaɭaŋkat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪aʋiɾkkirat̪u
n̪uʈpamaːna aːnmaː karaj paʈijaːmal ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum amaɾn̪t̪iɾukkirat̪u
anajt̪t̪ajjum t̪uɭajkkum t͡ʃuːɾijanin oɭijajp paோla
et̪uʋum maːraːt̪at̪u at̪an miːt̪u piɾakaːt͡ʃikkirat̪u
aːnmaːʋin oɭi ellaː iʈaŋkaɭilum t̪uːjmajjaːka piɾakaːt͡ʃikkirat̪u
at̪t̪akajja ɲaːnak kaɳɳaːl paːɾkkiraʋaɾkaɭ
eppaʈi meːʈʈaɾ marrum enna kajjaːɭkirat̪u piɾikka
aːʋikkum maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪ukkum eppaʈi t͡ʃaɳʈaj uɳʈaːkirat̪u
an̪t̪a ɲaːnikaɭ ʋaːɻkkajkku ʋaɻiʋakukkum ʋaɻijil t͡ʃelkiraːɾkaɭ
iŋkeː  at̪t̪ijaːjam muʈikirat̪u pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
kʂeːt̪ɾakʂeːt̪ɾad͡ʒɲaʋipaːkajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u paொɾuɭ marrum aːnmaːʋajp piɾippat̪an muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
innum t̪aொlajʋil n̪aːn unakku t̪irappeːn
anajt̪t̪u ɲaːnaŋkaɭin in̪t̪a ɲaːnam murrum
en punit̪aɾkaɭ anajʋaɾum kaʈan̪t̪uʋiʈʈanaɾ
muɻumajkku at̪t̪akajja ujaɾ uɳmajkaɭil
t͡ʃaːɾn̪t̪u kuːʈʈaːka ujaɾkirat̪u
ennuʈan aʋaɾkaɭ pirakkumpaோt̪u miːɳʈum pirappat̪illaj
kalpaŋkaɭilaோ piɾaɭajaŋkaɭilaோ maːrram eːrpaʈaːt̪u
in̪t̪a piɾapaɲt͡ʃam t̪aːn n̪aːn n̪aʈum iʈam
ellaː ujiɾkaɭukkum ʋit̪aj aŋkiɾun̪t̪u in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ ʋaɾukiraːɾ
ellaː ujiɾkaɭukkum pirappu jaːɾaோ kun̪t̪ijin makaneː
t̪aːjmaːɾkaɭ oʋʋaொɾu maɾaɳa ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪ilum piɾammaː kaɾuʋurraːɾ
meːlum n̪aːn t̪aːn ʋit̪ajkaɭaj anuppum t̪an̪t̪aj

ijarkajjin kuɳaŋkaɭ n̪it̪aːnam
aːɾʋam marrum arijaːmaj iʋaj muːnrum piɳajkkappaʈukinrana
maːraːt̪a maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪il maːraːt̪a aːʋi
t̪uːjmajjin muːlam inimajjaːna inimaj
karajpaʈaːt̪a marrum ariʋaொɭijuʈan ʋaːɻʋat̪u piɳajkkirat̪u
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikkum uɳmajkkum paːʋamillaːt̪a aːt̪maː
marrum peːɾaːɾʋam pat͡ʃijuʈan t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajjat̪u
marrum inappeɾukkam t̪uːɳʈut̪al marrum n̪aːʈʈam
uɾuʋaːna aːnmaːʋaj piɳajkkirat̪u kun̪t̪ijin makaneː
ʋeːlajkaɭin iɳajppu muːlam aːnaːl arijaːmaj piran̪t̪at̪u
iɾuɭ manit̪aɾkaɭajk kuɾuʈaːkki piɳajkkirat̪u
aʋaɾkaɭin aːnmaː majakkam t͡ʃaோmpal marrum t̪uːkkam
aːm in̪t̪ijaːʋin iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ n̪it̪aːnam aːnmaːkkaɭaj piɳajkkirat̪u
t͡ʃat̪ajkku inimajjaːna ɲaːnat̪t̪il marrum peːɾaːɾʋam piɳajkkirat̪u
uɻajkkum ʋikaːɾat̪t̪aːl aːnaːl arijaːmaj it̪u karajpaʈukirat̪u
ɲaːnak karrajkaɭ aːnmaːʋaj t͡ʃaோmpalil piɳajkkirat̪u
peːɾaːɾʋam marrum arijaːmaj oɾumuraj ʋenru
n̪it̪aːnat̪t̪aj ʋiʈuŋkaɭ oː paːɾat̪aː it̪u eŋkeː
arijaːmaj illaːt̪at̪aːl peːɾaːɾʋam ʋit̪ikaɭ
meːlum it̪ajaŋkaɭil arijaːmaj n̪allat̪alla allat̪u ʋiɾajʋaːnat̪u alla

an̪t̪a n̪akaɾat̪t̪il amajt̪i n̪ilajt̪t̪u aːʈt͡ʃi t͡ʃejkirat̪u
eːkkamum t̪iːʋiɾamum amajt̪ijinmajjum iɾukkum iʈat̪t̪il

at̪u paɻakka ʋaɻakkat̪t̪il purappaʈʈaːl
t̪uːɳʈut̪alin peːɾil at̪u ulakirkut͡ʃ t͡ʃellum
ʋeːlajkaɭuʈan piɳajkkappaʈʈa aːʋikaɭ marrum at̪u iran̪t̪aːl
kaʈinamaːna arijaːmajjil an̪t̪a kuɾuʈʈu aːnmaː

oɾeː ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjaːka oli jaːɾuʈajja aːɻamaːna kaɳkaɭukku
kaʈʈijum paɭiŋkum paொnnum onru
jaːɾuʈajja t͡ʃamamaːna it̪ajam at̪eː menmajjajk kaொɳʈuɭɭat̪u
aɻakaːna marrum ʋiɾumpat̪t̪akaːt̪a ʋiʂajaŋkaɭukku urut̪ijaːka amajkka
pukaɻilum ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijilum makiɻn̪t̪aʋaɾ t̪iɾupt̪i
maɾijaːt̪aj allat̪u maɾijaːt̪ajjuʈan n̪aɳpaɾkaɭukku
marrum t͡ʃakipput̪t̪anmajjil et̪iɾikaɭukku
mujart͡ʃikaɭil iɾun̪t̪u piɾin̪t̪aʋaɾ  aʋaɾ pejaɾiʈappaʈʈaːɾ
kuɳaŋkaɭaj miɲt͡ʃupaʋaɾ
marrum at̪t̪akajja 
ennaj ʋaɳaŋkum orraj t̪iːʋiɾa n̪ampikkajjuʈan
kuɳaŋkaɭukku appaːrpaʈʈat̪u ot̪t̪uppaோkirat̪u
piɾammaːʋiʈam ennaj aʈajkiraːn
n̪aːn t̪aːn
at̪uʋeː piɾammaːʋin uɾuʋam ennuʈajjat̪u
amiɾt̪am enpat̪u marrum aɻijaːmaj
ennuʈajjat̪u marrum ennuʈajja t͡ʃaɾijaːna ஃpelit͡ʃiʈʈi
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  muʈikirat̪u pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
kuɳat̪ɾajaʋipaːkajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u kuɳaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u piɾippat̪an muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
aːɳkaɭ asʋat̪t̪ajaːlamaɾam
at̪an kiːɻ kiɭajkaɭ uɭɭana at̪an ʋeːɾkaɭ meːleː 
eppaோt̪um punit̪amaːna maɾam aːm at̪an ilajkaɭukku
pat͡ʃt͡ʃaj marrum at͡ʃajjum paːʈalkaɭ uɳmajjaj kit͡ʃukit͡ʃukkinrana
asʋat̪t̪aj arin̪t̪aʋan ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭ marrum anajt̪t̪ajjum arin̪t̪aʋan
at̪an kiɭajkaɭ ʋaːnat̪t̪aj n̪aோkkit͡ʃ t͡ʃenru puːmijil muːɻkum#
aʋaɾkaɭin pirappaj eʈukkum manit̪aɾkaɭin t͡ʃejalkaɭum kuːʈa
kuɳaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u at̪an ʋeɭɭi spɾeːkkaɭ marrum puːkkaɭ
marrum at̪an t͡ʃurraɭaʋu anajt̪t̪u aːɾʋamuɭɭa pat͡ʃumajjaːna
t͡ʃuːɾijan marrum kaːrrin mut̪t̪at̪t̪il ʋiɾajʋaːna ʋaːɻkkajkku paːjt͡ʃt͡ʃal
aːɳkaɭin ʋaːɻkkaj t͡ʃalanaŋkaɭ n̪ijaːjamaːna ʋiɾajʋu
kaʋaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi uɳaɾʋu at̪an t̪aொŋkum ʋeːɾkaɭ t̪eːʈukinrana
kiːɻeː uɭɭa maɳ at̪aj aŋkeːjeː ʋajt̪t̪iɾukka ut̪aʋukirat̪u
manit̪aɾkaɭin in̪t̪a ulakat̪t̪in mat̪t̪ijil t͡ʃejalkaɭ t͡ʃejjappaʈʈana
eppaோt̪um irukkamaːna piɳajppukaɭaːl aʋarraj piɳajkkaʋum
n̪iːŋkaɭ maɾat̪t̪in paோt̪anajjaj n̪anku arin̪t̪iɾun̪t̪aːl
at̪an ʋaʈiʋam enna t͡ʃaொlkirat̪u at̪u eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋiɭajkirat̪u marrum pinnaɾ
at̪u eppaʈi muʈiʋukku ʋaɾa ʋeːɳʈum at̪an anajt̪t̪u t̪iːmajkaɭum
kuːɾmajjaːna parrinmajjin kaோʈaːɾijaj n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪uːɳʈuʋiːɾkaɭ
marrum oʈʈijiɾukkum paːmpu ʋeːɾkaɭaj piɭaʋupaʈut̪t̪i iʈuŋkaɭ
in̪t̪a asʋat̪t̪aj uɳaɾʋuʋaːɻkkaj kurajn̪t̪amajkka
an̪t̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna ʋaːnat̪t̪il put̪ija ʋaɭaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ eɻukinrana
et̪aj aʈajkiraːɾaோ aʋaɾkaɭ irakkum n̪aːɭ illaj
marajn̪t̪u paோkaʋum illaj ʋiɻaʋum aʋaɾiʈam at̪aːʋat̪u
t̪an̪t̪aj marrum mut̪al maɾmat̪t̪aj uɾuʋaːkkijat̪u jaːɾ
paɻajja paʈajppu eːnenraːl aʋaɾkaɭ aʋaɾiʈameː ʋaɾukiraːɾkaɭ
aːɾʋat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪um uʈajn̪t̪u paோkum kanaʋukaɭiliɾun̪t̪um
jaːɾ piɳajppukaɭajp piɾikkiraːɾkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭaj uʈaluʈan kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪ukiraːɾkaɭ
meːlumujaɾn̪t̪aʋaneː eppaொɻut̪um ʋaɻipaʈukiraːn
ini enna t̪enral kaɾuɳajjil ʋaɭaɾa
kaோʈaj inpam t̪uːŋkum maɾaŋkaɭajt̪ t̪uːɳʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃuːraːʋaɭijin ʋeʈippu aʋaɾkaɭaj kaொmpu marrum t̪aɳʈukaɭaj kiɻit̪t̪erikirat̪u
it̪u paோnra n̪it̪t̪ija ulakat̪t̪irku t͡ʃelluŋkaɭ
marraொɾu t͡ʃuːɾijan aŋkeː piɾakaːt͡ʃikkirat̪u marraொɾu t͡ʃan̪t̪iɾan
marraொɾu oɭi  an̪t̪i alla ʋiʈijalla n̪aɳpakal alla 
oɾumuraj paːɾt̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ ini t̪iɾumpuʋat̪illaj
aʋaɾkaɭ en oːjʋaj aʈajn̪t̪uʋiʈʈaːɾkaɭ ʋaːɻkkajjin ut͡ʃt͡ʃa ʋaɾam
eppaோt̪u ​​in̪t̪a ʋeɭippaʈʈa ʋaːɻkkaj ulakil
aɻijaːt̪a aːʋi enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u purappaʈukirat̪u
ʋaʈiʋam perukirat̪u at̪u t̪anakkut̪t̪aːneː iːɾkkirat̪u
piːjiŋkin kaɭaɲt͡ʃijat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪uanajt̪t̪ajjum uɭɭaʈakkijat̪u
pulankaɭ marrum ariʋu irajjaːɳmaj aːnmaː
iʋʋaːru t͡ʃat̪ajkkuɭ n̪uɻajʋat̪u allat̪u at̪aj ʋiʈʈu ʋeɭijeːruʋat̪u
kaːrru ʋaːt͡ʃanajkaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃeːkaɾippat̪u paோla iʋarrajt͡ʃ t͡ʃeːkaɾikkirat̪u
malaɾ paʈukkajkaɭukku meːleː ʋiːt͡ʃukirat̪u kaːt̪u marrum kaɳ
marrum t̪aொʈut̪al marrum t͡ʃuʋajt̪t̪al marrum maɳam iʋaj t̪eːʋaj 
aːm marrum oɾu uɳaɾʋuɭɭa manamt̪annaj iɳajt̪t̪uk kaொɭʋat̪u
ʋiʂajaŋkaɭaj uɳaɾa
ariʋillaːt̪aʋaɾkaɭ
an̪t̪a aːʋi paோkumpaோt̪um ʋaɾumpaோt̪um aʋaɾajk kurikka ʋeːɳʈaːm
allat̪u aʋaɾ ʋaʈiʋil t̪anat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajp perumpaோt̪u
kuɳaŋkaɭuʈan iɳajn̪t̪at̪u aːnaːl aʋaj t̪eɭiʋaːkak kaːɳappaʈukinrana
paːɾkka kaɳkaɭ jaːɾukku uɳʈu paɾit͡ʃut̪t̪a aːt̪maːkkaɭ paːɾkkiraːɾkaɭ
et̪u at̪arkaːka paːʈupaʈukirat̪u ariʋaːɭi aʋaɾkaɭ uɳaɾkiraːɾkaɭ
t̪aŋkaɭukkuɭ an̪t̪a aːʋi aːnaːl muʈʈaːɭkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ paːʈupaʈʈaːlum pakut̪t̪ariʋat̪illaj it̪ajaŋkaɭ uɭɭana
iɾakkamarra t̪aʋaraːna t̪akaʋal
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪um t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
t͡ʃuːɾijankaɭin t̪iɾaɳʈa makimajjaj piɾakaːt͡ʃikkirat̪u
it̪u ulakam muɻuʋat̪ajjum oɭiɾat͡ʃ t͡ʃejkirat̪u enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u n̪ilaʋukaɭ
ʋeɭɭik karrajkaɭaj ʋaɾajjaʋum kaʈumajjaːna aɻakajk kaொɭut̪t̪aʋum
n̪aːn kaɭimaɳɳaj uːʈuɾuʋi ellaː ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭajjum kaொʈukkireːn
aʋaɾkaɭin ujiɾ t͡ʃakt̪i n̪aːn aːlajkkuɭ t͡ʃarukkukireːn 
ʋeːɾ ilaj marrum puːkkaɭ  kaːʈukaɭaj pat͡ʃumajjaːkka
iɭan̪iːɾuʈan mukkija ʋeppamaːka maːrum
n̪aːn makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃikkum t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭil piɾakaːt͡ʃikkireːn kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃelkireːn
ʋeɭippura marrum uɭ t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃat̪t̪uʈan uɳaʋaɭikka
anajt̪t̪u irajt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭaːlum uʈal#
in̪t̪a ulakil
iɾut̪t̪al iɾuʋakaj piɭaʋupaʈʈat̪u onru
piɾikkappaʈaːt̪a onru ʋaːɻum anajt̪t̪um
piɾikkappaʈʈaʋaɾkaɭ piɾin̪t̪u amaɾn̪t̪iɾuppat̪u
piɾikkappaʈaːt̪a
aʋaɾ innum ujaɾn̪t̪aʋaɾ
unnat̪amaːna anajt̪t̪ajjum t̪aːŋki jaːɾuʈajja pejaɾ kaɾt̪t̪aɾ
n̪it̪t̪ija irajjaːɳmaj mut̪al ellaː ulakaŋkaɭajjum n̪iɾappupaʋaɾ
aʋaɾkaɭajt̪ t̪akkaʋajt̪t̪al meːlum  iʋʋaːru appaːl ʋat͡ʃippat̪u
piɾikkappaʈʈa marrum piɾikkappaʈaːt̪a  n̪aːn
n̪aːn manit̪aɾkaɭaːlum ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭaːlum aɻajkkappaʈʈeːn ujiɾ ut͡ʃt͡ʃam
puɾuʂaோt̪t̪aman
jaːɾ ennaj appaʈi ariʋaːɾ
manam meːkamuːʈʈamillaːmal anajt̪t̪ajjum arin̪t̪aʋaɾeː anpeː iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
meːlum aʋaɾat̪u muɻu aːnmaːʋaோʈu ennaj eppaோt̪um ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾ
ippaோt̪u punit̪amaːna iɾakat͡ʃija maɾmam
umakku ariʋikkappaʈʈat̪u it̪aj jaːɾ puɾin̪t̪ukaொɭʋat̪u
hat̪ ɲaːnam aʋaɾ makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijil ʋeːlajkaɭaj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈʈaːɾ
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  muʈikirat̪u pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
puɾuʂaோt̪t̪amapɾaːpt̪ijaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u ujaɾn̪ilajjaj aʈajʋat̪an muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
kiɾuʂɳaː
at͡ʃt͡ʃaminmaj aːnmaːʋin t̪animaj ʋiɾuppam
ɲaːnat̪t̪irkaːka eppaோt̪um paːʈupaʈuŋkaɭ t̪iran̪t̪a kaj
marrum aːɭappaʈum pat͡ʃijinmaj marrum pakt̪i
marrum t̪animajjil paʈikkum kaːt̪al paɳiʋu
n̪eːɾmaj ujiɾkaɭ et̪ajjum kaːjappaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪il kaʋanam
t͡ʃat̪t̪ijam kaோpat̪t̪irku t̪aːmat̪am oɾu manam
marraʋaɾkaɭ et̪ajp paɾit͡ʃiːlikkiraːɾkaɭaோ at̪aj leːt͡ʃaːka ʋiʈʈuʋiʈukiraːɾ
marrum t͡ʃaman̪ilaj marrum t̪aொɳʈu
en̪t̪a manit̪anin t̪aʋarukaɭajjum uɭaʋu paːɾppat̪illaj marrum menmaj
t̪unpappaʈum anajʋaɾajjum n̪aோkki t̪iɾupt̪ijaːna it̪ajam
aːt͡ʃajkaɭ illaːmal paʈapaʈakkirat̪u oɾu t̪aːŋkum leːt͡ʃaːna
aʈakkamaːna marrum kaʈumajjaːna aːɳmaj unnat̪amaːka kalan̪t̪a
paொrumaj t̪ajɾijam marrum t̪uːjmajjuʈan
oɾu paɻiʋaːŋkaːt̪a aːʋi oɾupaோt̪um kaொʈukkappaʈaʋillaj
t̪annaj mika at̪ikamaːka mat̪ippiʈuʋat̪uat̪t̪akajja arikurikaɭ
in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː jaːɾuʈajja paːt̪aŋkaɭ amajkkappaʈʈat̪aோ aʋanuʈajja
t͡ʃaொɾkkap pirappukku ʋaɻiʋakukkum an̪t̪a n̪ijaːjamaːna paːt̪ajjil
ʋaɲt͡ʃakamum aːɳaʋamum peɾumajjum
t͡ʃiːkkiɾam kaோpam kaʈumajjaːna marrum t̪iːja peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu
marrum arijaːmaj at̪an t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a iɾuɭukku kuɾuʈʈu
iʋaj aʈajjaːɭaŋkaɭ en iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː jaːɾuʈajja pirappu
iɻin̪t̪a pakut̪ikaɭukku ʋit̪ikkappaʈʈat̪u#
paɾalaோkap pirappu ʋiʈut̪alajjajk kaொɳʈuʋaɾukirat̪u
enaʋeː n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈum at͡ʃuɾaɾkaɭuʈan pirappu
aʈimajt̪t̪anat̪t̪irku kaொɳʈu ʋaɾukirat̪u iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːka iɾu
paɾalaோkap pirappukkaːka jaːɾuʈajja paŋku ot̪ukkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
ʋaːɻum manit̪aɾkaɭ miːt̪u iɾaɳʈu mut̪t̪iɾajkaɭ kurikkappaʈʈuɭɭana
t̪ejʋiːka marrum t̪ejʋiːkamarra n̪aːn unniʈam peːt͡ʃineːn
paɾalaோka manit̪anaj n̪iːŋkaɭ enna kurikaɭaːl arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭa ʋeːɳʈum
t͡ʃaொɾkkamarrat̪ajp parri ippaோt̪u enniʈam keːɭuŋkaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭ puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭaʋillaj paɾalaோkat̪t̪irku illaj
enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u aːt̪maːkkaɭ eʋʋaːru purappaʈukinrana eppaʈi ʋaɾukiraːɾkaɭ
enniʈam t̪iɾumpaʋum iʋarril uɳmajjum illaj
t̪uːjmajjum illaj ʋaːɻkkajjin ʋit̪ijum illaj in̪t̪a ulakam
t͡ʃaʈʈamaோ oɻuŋkaோ irajʋanaோ illaj
enaʋeː aʋaɾkaɭ kuːrukiraːɾkaɭ kaːɾaɳat̪t̪aːl eɻun̪t̪iɾukkaʋillaj
kaːɾaɳat̪t̪aj pinparri t͡ʃaɾijaːna n̪aோkkat̪t̪il
aːnaːl at̪u kaːma ʋiːʈu t̪aʋiɾa ʋeːrillaj
meːlum in̪t̪a ʋiʂajat̪t̪aj n̪inajt̪t̪u an̪t̪a paːɻaʈajn̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ anajʋaɾum 
kurajn̪t̪a put̪t̪i iɾuɳʈa manam  t̪aŋkaɭajk kaொʈuŋkaɭ
t̪iːja t͡ʃejalkaɭukku aʋaɾkaɭin ʋakajjaːna t͡ʃaːpaŋkaɭ
t̪iːɾaːt̪a aːt͡ʃajkaɭukku t͡ʃaɾaɳaʈajn̪t̪u
ʋaɲt͡ʃakam muʈʈaːɭt̪anam marrum peɾumaj n̪irajn̪t̪a
kuɾuʈʈut̪t̪anmajjil aʋaɾkaɭin piɻajkaɭ parri piʈit̪t̪u
paːʋamaːna paோkkil aʋaɾkaɭ in̪t̪ap paொjjaj n̪ampukiraːɾkaɭ
at̪u uɳmajjaːka iɾun̪t̪apaோt̪ilum  in̪t̪a paொj maɾaɳat̪t̪irku ʋaɻiʋakukkum 
makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijil ellaː n̪anmajkaɭajjum kaɳʈarit̪al
meːlum it̪aோ muʈin̪t̪at̪u
t͡ʃikkijat̪u
n̪uːru ʋiːɳ n̪ampikkajkaɭin kajirukaɭil
aʋaɾkaɭin aːɾʋat̪t̪irkum kaோpat̪t̪irkum aʈimajkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭ ʋaːŋkukiraːɾkaɭ
aʈippaʈajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejalkaɭajk kaொɳʈa t͡ʃelʋam t͡ʃuːʈaːna pat͡ʃijajp paோkka
iʋʋaɭaʋu inru aʋaɾkaɭ kuːrukiraːɾkaɭ at̪an muːlam n̪aːŋkaɭ perraோm
it̪ajat̪t̪in at̪t̪akajja marrum at̪t̪akajja ʋiɾuppam at̪an n̪irajʋaːka iɾukkum
meːlum it̪u n̪ammuʈajjat̪u marraொnru n̪ammuʈajjat̪aːka iɾukkum
inru n̪aːm oɾu et̪iɾijajk kaொnraோm n̪aːŋkaɭ kaொlʋaோm
n̪aːɭaj n̪amat̪u innaொɾu et̪iɾi paːɾ
n̪aːm aːɳʈaʋaɾkaɭ illajjaː eŋkaɭaj n̪anraːka urt͡ʃaːkappaʈut̪t̪aʋillajjaː
n̪amat̪u at̪iɾʂʈam piɾapalamaːnat̪u t̪ajɾijamaːnat̪u peɾijat̪u allaʋaː
n̪aːm paɳakkaːɾaɾkaɭ peɾumajjuʈan piran̪t̪aோm ʋeːru enna aːɳkaɭ
n̪ammajp paோl ʋaːɻaʋaː palikkaːka kaொlluŋkaɭ
peɾija aɭaʋil n̪aʈikkaʋum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːkaʋum iɾuŋkaɭ enaʋeː aʋaɾkaɭ peːt͡ʃukiraːɾkaɭ
arijaːmajjaːl iɾuɭ t͡ʃuːɻn̪t̪at̪u at̪anaːl aʋaj ʋiɻukinrana 
t̪iʈʈaŋkaɭuʈan aŋkum iŋkum t̪uːkki erijappaʈʈu eːmaːrrappaʈʈu piɳajkkappaʈʈat̪u
karuppu maːjajjin ʋalajjil kaːmaŋkaɭil t̪aொlajn̪t̪u
ʈaʋun ʈu ஃpaʋul n̪aɾakaː kaɾʋamuɭɭa anpaːna
piʈiʋaːt̪amum peɾumajjum kaொɳʈaʋaɾ mat̪uʋajk kuʈit̪t̪u iran̪t̪aʋaɾ
t͡ʃelʋam marrum paொrupparra aʋaɾkaɭin anajt̪t̪u piɾat͡ʃaːt̪am
pajapakt̪ijin oɾu n̪ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijajk kaொɳʈiɾuŋkaɭ t͡ʃejjappaʈaʋillaj
paɳʈajja n̪ampikkajjin pakt̪ijil iʋʋaːru t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejt̪aːɾ
t̪annampikkaj palam aʈaːʋaʈit̪t̪anam ʋiɾun̪t̪u kaோpam
in̪t̪a en n̪in̪t̪anaj t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭ aɳijum ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil
aʋaɾkaɭ inappeɾukkam t͡ʃejjum ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil en et̪iɾikaɭ
ʋeruppu marrum ʋeruppu kaொʈuːɾamaːna t̪iːja iɻiʋaːna
n̪aːn t̪aːɻt̪t̪appaʈʈa manit̪aɾkaɭil mikak kurajn̪t̪a marrum kurajn̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ
miːɳʈum miːɳʈum ʋaːɻʋin muʈiʋil
eːt̪aோ pit͡ʃaːt͡ʃu ʋajirril eŋkiɾun̪t̪u  pirappaːl piran̪t̪at̪u 
pit͡ʃaːt͡ʃu kaɾuppajkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭaj miːɳʈum spaːn anajt̪t̪u eːmaːrru
meːlum aʋaɾkaɭ ennajk kaɳʈupiʈit̪t̪u ʋaɳaŋkum ʋaɾaj anpaːna iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
aʋaɾkaɭ an̪t̪a n̪et̪aɾ ɾaோʈʈaj mit̪ijuŋkaɭ
n̪aɾakat̪t̪in kat̪aʋukaɭ
mummaʈaŋku it̪an muːlam manit̪aɾkaɭ kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃella 
kaːmat̪t̪in kat̪aʋu kaோpat̪t̪in kat̪aʋu kat̪aʋu
peːɾaːt͡ʃaj kaொɳʈaʋaɾ oɾu manit̪an an̪t̪a muːnrajjum t̪aʋiɾkkaʈʈum
uɭɭeː n̪uɻajjaːmal ot̪uŋki iɾuppaʋaɾ
n̪aɾakkin an̪t̪a muːnru ʋaːjilkaɭum n̪eːɾaːka t͡ʃelkirat̪u
aʋanuʈajja amajt̪ijajk kaːɳa sʋaɾkaːʋin ʋaːjilukku ʋan̪t̪aːn
