iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
t̪ajʋat͡ʃaɾasaௌpat̪ʋipaːkajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u t̪ejʋiːka marrum t̪ejʋiːkat̪t̪anmajjin t̪anit̪t̪anmajjin put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
manit̪aɾkaɭ punit̪a n̪ijamat̪t̪aj kajʋiʈʈaːl
t͡ʃaːst̪iɾaŋkaɭajk kaʋanikkaːmal n̪ampikkajjaj it̪ajat̪t̪il ʋajt̪t̪iɾuŋkaɭ
meːlum ʋaɳaŋkuŋkaɭ aʋaɾkaɭin n̪ilaj ennaʋaːka iɾukkum
peɾija kiɾuʂɳaː t͡ʃat̪ʋaːn ɾad͡ʒas t̪amas t͡ʃol
kiɾuʂɳaː
mummaʈaŋku n̪ampikkaj manit̪akulam marrum n̪iːɾuːrrukaɭ
an̪t̪a muːnru kuɳaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪u  uɳmajjaːka
allat̪u uɳaɾʋu paʈin̪t̪a allat̪u iɾuɳʈa n̪iːŋkaɭ keːʈpat̪u paோl
oʋʋaொɾu ʋit͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃijin n̪ampikkaj in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃaɾ
aʋan uɳmajjil ennaʋaːka iɾukkiraːnaோ at̪u t̪annajt̪t̪aːneː ot̪t̪ukkaொɭɭum
eŋkeː oɾu ʋaɻipaːʈʈaːɭanajk kaːɳpaːj at̪u
aʋan et̪aj ʋaɳaŋkukiraːnaோ at̪ajjeː ujiɾkaɭ oɾuŋkiɳajkkinrana
t͡ʃan̪n̪it̪i paோnraʋaj ʋaːkkaːɭanum
amajt̪ijaːna aːnmaːkkaɭ uɳmajjaːna kaʈaʋuɭkaɭaj ʋaɳaŋkukinrana aːt̪maːkkaɭ
kiːɻppaʈin̪t̪a ɾaːd͡ʒaːkkaɭ ɾaːʈt͡ʃat͡ʃaɾkaɭaj ʋaɳaŋkukiraːɾkaɭ#
allat̪u jakʂaɾkaɭ marrum iɾuɭ manit̪aɾkaɭ piɾaːɾt̪t̪anaj
pɾiːt̪aːs marrum puːʈʈaːs# aːm marrum an̪t̪a
kat͡ʃappaːna t̪aʋam t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭ ʋit̪ikkappaʈaʋillaj
t͡ʃaɾijaːna ʋit̪ijaːl  t̪aʋam at̪an ʋeːɾajk kaொɳʈat̪u
t̪annirajʋu peɾumajmikka paːt͡ʃaːŋkukaɭil
an̪t̪a manit̪aɾkaɭ uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃiʋat͡ʃappaʈʈa ʋanmuraj kaːʈʈu
t͡ʃit̪t̪iɾaʋat̪aj  ariʋarraʋaɾkaɭ  en kuːrukaɭ
aʋaɾkaɭin maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪irkuɭ n̪ijaːjamaːna n̪iruʋanat̪t̪il muːʈuŋkaɭ
illaj n̪aːneː t͡ʃat̪ajkkuɭ iɾukkireːn
paɾalaோkat̪t̪irku alla aɾppaɳikkappaʈʈa pit͡ʃaːt͡ʃukaɭukku aʋarraj arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
eːnenil uɳaʋukaɭ manit̪a kulat̪t̪irku mummaʈaŋkaːnat̪u
uːʈʈamaɭippat̪il mummaʈaŋku ʋaɻi uɭɭat̪u
ʋaɻipaːʈu mat̪uʋilakku annat̪aːnam
it̪aj n̪aːn keːɭ kaொɳʈu ʋaɾum uɳaʋu iɾukkirat̪u
t͡ʃakt̪i paொɾuɭ ʋalimaj marrum aːɾaோkkijam marrum ʋaːɻʋat̪arkaːna makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi
n̪anku paɾuʋamaʈajn̪t̪u anpaːna aːrut̪alaːka
t͡ʃuːt̪ஃpaːsʈ irajt͡ʃt͡ʃi marrum kaொɳʈu ʋaɾum uɳaʋukaɭ uɭɭana
ʋalikaɭ marrum amajt̪ijinmaj marrum eɾijum iɾat̪t̪am marrum t̪ukkam
mikaʋum kaʈit̪t̪al t͡ʃuːʈu uppu marrum kuːɾmajjaːka iɾuppat̪u
enaʋeː mikaʋum ʋaluʋaːna pat͡ʃijaːl eːŋkijat̪u
meːlum maோt͡ʃamaːna uɳaʋu uɭɭat̪u  iɾaʋu muɻuʋat̪um ʋajkkappaʈukirat̪u#
ɾut͡ʃijarra aɻukku keʈʈat̪u t͡ʃaːppiʈum
aɻukum ʋiɾun̪t̪u ut̪aʈukaɭukku t͡ʃan̪t̪ippu
kaːt̪al paோnraʋarril iɾuɭ
iʋʋaːru t͡ʃaʈaŋkukaɭuʈan
ʋekumat̪ikkaːka t͡ʃejjappaʈaːt̪a t̪ijaːkam
t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejjum paோt̪u ​​n̪ijaːjamaːna murajjil ʋaɻaŋkappaʈukirat̪u
it̪aj n̪aːn t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum
t͡ʃuːt̪ஃpaːsʈ t͡ʃaʈaŋku aːnaːl aːt̪aːjat̪t̪irkaːka t̪ijaːkam
n̪alla n̪arpejaɾukkaːka ʋaɻaŋkappaʈukirat̪u it̪aj urut̪ippaʈut̪t̪ik kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
oː paːɾat̪aŋkaɭil t͡ʃiran̪t̪aʋaɾeː it̪u ɾaːd͡ʒasja t͡ʃaʈaŋku
aːɾʋam enra mut̪t̪iɾajjuʈan marrum oɾu t̪ijaːkam
t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭukku et̪iɾaːka ʋaɻaŋkappaʈum uɾija t̪aொkaj illaːmal
uɳaʋu kaொʈuppat̪u t̪uɳajjillaːmal
punit̪amaːna paːʈal allat̪u paːt̪iɾijaːɾkaɭukku peɾijat̪u
n̪ampikkajjarra kaொɳʈaːʈʈat̪t̪il at̪aj keːʋalam enru aɻajkkaʋum
iɾuɭiɻan̪t̪at̪u
t̪ejʋa ʋaɻipaːʈu
t͡ʃirappu ʋaɻipaːʈu t̪aːɻʋaːna maɾijaːt̪aj
iɾaɳʈu muraj piran̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ aːt͡ʃiɾijaɾkaɭ peɾijaʋaɾkaɭ t̪uːjmaj
n̪eːɾmaj marrum piɾammat͡ʃt͡ʃaɾija ʋaːkku
en̪t̪a ut̪aʋijarra ʋiʂajat̪t̪ajjum kaːjappaʈut̪t̪akkuːʈaːt̪u 
iʋaj t͡ʃaʈʈat̪t̪in uɳmajjaːna mat̪at̪t̪anmajjaj uɾuʋaːkkukinrana
jaːɾukkum t̪unpam t̪aɾaːt̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ eppaோt̪um uɳmaj
menmajjaːna marrum inimajjaːna ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭ marrum n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃaொlʋat̪u
oɾu punit̪a n̪uːlin muɳumuɳuppu ʋaːt͡ʃippil
iʋaj peːt͡ʃt͡ʃin uɳmajjaːna mat̪at̪t̪anmajjaj uɾuʋaːkkukinrana
aːnmaːʋin amajt̪i kaɾuɳaj
amajt̪ijaːna aːʋijin at͡ʃajʋu n̪ilajjaːna mana aɻut̪t̪am
ijarkajjaj punit̪appaʈut̪t̪iʋajkaɭaj uɾuʋaːkkukinrana
n̪alla t͡ʃaʈaŋku marrum manat̪in uɳmajjaːna mat̪am
it̪t̪akajja muppeɾum n̪ampikkaj ujaɾn̪t̪a irajjat͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪il
aːt̪aːja n̪ampikkajjinri aɾppaɳit̪t̪a it̪ajaŋkaɭaːl ʋajt̪t̪iɾun̪t̪aːɾ
t͡ʃat̪ʋaːnin t͡ʃaɾijaːna ʋeːlaj uɳmajjaːna n̪ampikkaj
mat̪am peɾumajjuʈan kaːʈt͡ʃijaɭikkirat̪u
n̪alla paொɻut̪upaோkku ʋaɻipaːʈu pukaɻ pera
appaʈit͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlluŋkaɭ  n̪aːn ɾaːd͡ʒas t͡ʃaொri marrum ʋiːɳ
mat̪am oɾu ariʋarra ʋiɾuppat̪t̪aj pinparrukirat̪u
t̪annajt̪ t̪aːneː t͡ʃit̪t̪iɾaʋat̪aj t͡ʃejja allat̪u kaːjappaʈut̪t̪a at̪ikaːɾat̪t̪irku ʋaɾa
marraொnrut̪amas iɾuɳʈa marrum n̪aோjʋaːjppaʈʈa
anpuʈan kaொʈukkappaʈum paɾit͡ʃu
ippaோt̪u n̪aːn makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijuʈan kaொʈukka ʋeːɳʈum eʈukkum paோt̪u
et̪ajjum t̪iɾuppi kaொʈukka muʈijaːt̪u uɾija iʈat̪t̪il t͡ʃejjappaʈʈat̪u
uɾija n̪eːɾam marrum t͡ʃan̪t̪ippajp perupaʋaɾukku
it̪u t͡ʃat̪ʋaːnin paɾit͡ʃu n̪ijaːjamaːnat̪u marrum laːpakaɾamaːnat̪u
t͡ʃujan̪alat̪t̪uʈan kaொʈukkappaʈʈa paɾit͡ʃu eŋkeː peruʋat̪u
miːɳʈum n̪ampikkaj uɭɭat̪u allat̪u t͡ʃila muʈiʋu t̪eːʈappaʈum paோt̪u
allat̪u oɾu ʋeruppuʈan paɾit͡ʃu ʋaɻaŋkappaʈum iʈat̪t̪il
it̪u ɾaːd͡ʒaːsin un̪t̪ut̪alaːl karaj paʈin̪t̪a n̪aோjʋaːjppaʈʈat̪u
t̪iːja n̪eːɾat̪t̪il paɾit͡ʃu kaொn̪t̪aɭippuʈan ʋiːt͡ʃappaʈʈat̪u
t̪aʋaraːna iʈat̪t̪il aʈippaʈaj perun̪aɾukku
alaʈt͡ʃijam allat̪u kaʈumajjaːna iɾakkaminmajjaːl t͡ʃejjappaʈʈat̪u
t̪amas paɾit͡ʃu iɾuɳʈa at̪u aːt͡ʃiːɾʋat̪ikkaːt̪u#
iŋkeː at̪t̪ijaːjam  pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin
sɾat̪t̪aːt̪ɾajaʋipaːkajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u muːnruʋit̪amaːna n̪ampikkajjaːl mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam




at̪t̪ijaːjam 
aɾd͡ʒunaː
makimajjuɭɭaʋaɾeː
mikaʋum uɳmaj  it̪ajat̪t̪in irajʋant͡ʃannijaːs
mat̪uʋilakku marrum ut͡ʃt͡ʃaɾippu aːɳʈaʋaɾeː
t̪ijaːkaː in̪t̪a iɾuʋaɾajjum piɾippat̪u et̪u
kiɾuʂɳaː
t͡ʃan̪n̪ijaːt͡ʃam enru pulaʋaɾkaɭ t͡ʃaɾijaːkap paோt̪ikkiraːɾkaɭ
it̪u ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪a kaːlat̪t̪in anajt̪t̪u t͡ʃejalkaɭukkum mun̪t̪ajjat̪u
aːt͡ʃajjaːl marrum aʋaɾkaɭin put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anamaːna t͡ʃaொl
t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃejalkaɭin palanajt̪ t̪urakkiraːɾ
t̪uraʋikaɭukkuɭɭum t͡ʃilaɾ kaʈajppiʈit̪t̪uɭɭanaɾ
anajt̪t̪u t͡ʃejalkaɭum paːʋam marrum kajʋiʈappaʈa ʋeːɳʈum
meːlum t͡ʃilaɾ illaj n̪alla t͡ʃejalkaɭ 
ʋaɻipaːʈu t̪aʋam t̪aːnam ena  t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum
ippaோt̪u en ʋaːkkijat̪t̪ajk keːɭ paːɾat̪aŋkaɭil t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
un et̪iɾikaɭajt̪ t̪uɾat̪t̪ukiraʋaɾeː
t̪urat̪t̪al enpat̪u mummaʈaŋku ʋaʈiʋamaːkum
marrum ʋaɻipaːʈu t̪aʋam t̪aːnam t̪aŋkakkuːʈaːt̪u
illaj makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijuʈan t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum an̪t̪a muːnrukkum
uɳmajjaːna aːnmaːkkaɭukku t͡ʃut̪t̪ikaɾikkum n̪iːɾ
innum an̪t̪a ujaɾn̪t̪a t͡ʃejalkaɭaj kuːʈa n̪aʈajmurajppaʈut̪t̪a ʋeːɳʈum
parrut̪alajjum ellaːp palanajjum ʋiʈʈuk kaொʈuppat̪il
paʈajppukaɭaːl t̪ajaːɾikkappaʈʈat̪u it̪u en t̪iːɾppu iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
it̪u enat̪u t̪aʋiɾkkamuʈijaːt̪a marrum n̪ilajjaːna aːɳaj
t͡ʃaɾijaːna murajjil paɾin̪t̪uɾajkkappaʈʈa ʋeːlajjajt̪ t̪aʋiɾppat̪u
t͡ʃan̪t̪ippat̪illaj enaʋeː ʋat͡ʃan̪t̪at̪t̪aj t̪aʋiɾkka ʋeːɳʈum
iɾuɭ marrum maːjajjiliɾun̪t̪u at̪ajk karpikkirat̪u
maːmt͡ʃat̪t̪irku iɻiʋaːna ʋeːlajjiliɾun̪t̪u ʋilaki iɾut̪t̪al
it̪u ʋiɾumpat̪t̪akaːt̪at̪u enru oɾuʋaɾ kuːrumpaோt̪u it̪u puːd͡ʒjamaːnat̪u
at̪t̪akajjaʋaɾ aːʋeːt͡ʃat̪t̪il iɾun̪t̪u t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːɾ aːt̪aːjam et̪uʋum illaj
aʋaɾat̪u t̪uraʋu ʋerri aːnaːl aɾd͡ʒun
ʋeːlajjin miːt̪aːna parrut̪alajt̪ t̪aʋiɾppat̪u
ʋeːlajjil ʋekumat̪ijajt̪ t̪aʋiɾppat̪u
oɾuʋan at̪aj muɻumajjaːka uɳmajjaːkat͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪aːlum
t͡ʃejʋat̪u t͡ʃaɾit̪aːn at̪u uɳmajjaːna t͡ʃejal
marrum mat̪uʋilakku jaːɾ kaʈamajkaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
aʋaɾat̪u ʋeːlaj t̪aோlʋijaʈajn̪t̪aːl ʋerrijaʈajn̪t̪aːl aʋiɻt̪t̪uʋiʈaːt̪iːɾkaɭ
mukast̪ut̪ijinri t̪an it̪ajat̪t̪il n̪ijaːjappaʈut̪t̪inaːɾ
ʋiʋaːt̪aŋkaɭ marrum t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkaŋkaɭaj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈuŋkaɭ aʋaɾuʈajja uɳmajjaːna t͡ʃejal
eːnenil uʈalil iɾuppat̪aːl jaːɾum n̪irka muʈijaːt̪u
t͡ʃejalil iɾun̪t̪u murrilum ʋilaki innum jaːɾ ʋaːkkaɭikkaʋillaj
aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃejalkaɭin laːpat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u ʋilakijiɾukkirat̪u
uɻajppin palan ʋaɾum ʋaːɻʋil
ellaː manit̪aɾkaɭukkum muːnru maʈaŋku  ʋiɾumpat̪t̪akkat̪u
marrum ʋiɾumpat̪t̪akaːt̪a marrum iɾaɳʈum kalan̪t̪a
aːnaːl en̪t̪a ʋeːlajjum illaːt̪a iʈat̪t̪il paɻam illaj
en peːt͡ʃt͡ʃajk keːɭ n̪iːɳʈa kaɾaŋkaɭaj uʈajja irajʋaneː uɾuʋaːkkam ajn̪t̪u
oʋʋaொɾu t͡ʃejalukkum t͡ʃellum t͡ʃaːŋkijat̪t̪il karpikkappaʈukirat̪u
t̪eːʋajjaːna aɭaʋu mut̪alil paʈaj pinnaɾ
mukaʋaɾ aʈut̪t̪u palʋeːru kaɾuʋikaɭ
n̪aːnkaːʋat̪u t͡ʃirappu mujart͡ʃi ajn̪t̪aːʋat̪u kaʈaʋuɭ
en̪t̪a maɾaɳam enna ʋeːlaj
uʈal manam allat̪u peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu t̪iːmaj allat̪u n̪anmaj
in̪t̪a ajn̪t̪in muːlam aʋaɾ at̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejkiraːɾ iʋʋaːru iɾuppat̪u
ariʋinmajjaːl eʋan t̪annajp paːɾkkiraːn
oɾeː n̪aʈikaɾaːka et̪uʋum t̪eɾijaːt̪u
marrum et̪ajjum paːɾkkaʋillaj enaʋeː n̪aːn t͡ʃaொlkireːn onru enraːl 
karaj paʈijaːt̪a manat̪uʈan  t̪anniʈamiɾun̪t̪u ot̪uŋki iɾuppat̪u
kaொlla eːlam ʋiʈappaʈʈa anajt̪t̪u puɾaʋalaɾkaɭajjum kaொlla ʋeːɳʈum
aʋaɾ kaொlʋat̪illaj aʋaɾ at̪arkuk kaʈʈuppaʈaʋillaj
ariʋu t̪eɾin̪t̪a ʋiʂajam arin̪t̪a manam
iʋaj t͡ʃejalpaːʈʈin mummaʈaŋku t̪aொʈakkan̪ilajjaj uɾuʋaːkkukinrana
t͡ʃejal n̪aʈikaɾ marrum kaɾuʋi
iʋaj pat̪t̪iɾat̪t̪in muːnru maʈaŋku maொt̪t̪at̪t̪aj uɾuʋaːkkukinrana
aːnaːl ariʋu mukaʋaɾ t͡ʃejal ʋeːru
muːnru piɾikkum kuɳaŋkaɭaːl ippaோt̪u keːɭ
aʋajkaɭaj piɾikkum kuɳaŋkaɭ
uɳmajjaːna ariʋu iɾukkirat̪u it̪u it̪ut̪aːn enpat̪aj n̪iːŋkaɭ arin̪t̪u kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ
ellaː ujiɾkaɭilum oɾu maːraːt̪a ʋaːɻkkajjajp paːɾkka
marrum t̪anit̪t̪anijaːka piɾikka muʈijaːt̪a onru
n̪irajʋarra ariʋu uɭɭat̪u paːɾppat̪u
t̪anit̪t̪ani iɾuppukkaɭ t̪aʋiɾa
meːlum piɾikkappaʈʈiɾuppat̪u aʋarraj uɳmajjaːka ʋajt̪t̪iɾukkirat̪u
t̪aʋaraːna ariʋu uɭɭat̪u kaɳmuːʈit̪t̪anamaːka oʈʈikkaொɳʈat̪u
oɾuʋaɾukku ellaːmeː kaːɾaɳam t̪eːʈaːmal
oɭi kurukalaːna marrum man̪t̪amaːna marrum iɾuɳʈa illaːt̪at̪u
t͡ʃaɾijaːna t͡ʃejal uɭɭat̪u at̪u kaʈʈaɭajjiʈappaʈʈat̪u
parrut̪al illaːmal uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijarra murajjil
kaʈamajkkaːka anpirkaːkaʋaோ ʋeruppirkaːkaʋaோ aːt̪aːjat̪t̪irkaːkaʋaோ alla
ʋiːɳ t͡ʃejal uɭɭat̪u manit̪aɾkaɭ pint̪aொʈaɾʋat̪u
aːt͡ʃajkaɭaj puːɾt̪t̪i t͡ʃejja ʋalikkirat̪u t̪uːɳʈappaʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃuja uɳaɾʋu muːlam anajt̪t̪ajjum uriɲt͡ʃum mana aɻut̪t̪at̪t̪uʈan
it̪u ɾaːd͡ʒaːsuʈajjat̪u  uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi marrum ʋiːɳ
iɾuɳʈa t͡ʃejal uɭɭat̪u oɾuʋaɾ oɾu kaːɾijat̪t̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejjumpaோt̪u
piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃinajkaɭaj alaʈt͡ʃijam kaːjam parri alaʈt͡ʃijam
allat̪u marraʋaɾkaɭukku t̪aʋaru aʋaɾ t̪iːŋku t͡ʃejt̪aːl alaʈt͡ʃijam
aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a aːnmaːt̪amas kaɾuppu marrum keʈʈat̪u
t͡ʃaɾijaːna t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ iɾukkiraːɾ t͡ʃejalpaʈupaʋaɾ
t͡ʃujat̪eːʈalil iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈa aʈakkamaːna urut̪ijaːna
urut̪ijaːnaʋaɾ n̪allat̪u allat̪u t̪iːmaj onrut̪aːn
t͡ʃaɾijaːkat͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪arkaːna uɭɭaʈakkamaʋaɾ uɳmajjil t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːɾ
uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijuʈan t͡ʃejpaʋaɾ iɾukkiraːɾ ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejpaʋan
t̪uːɳʈut̪aliliɾun̪t̪u laːpam t̪eːʈuʋat̪u muɾaʈʈut̪t̪anamaːka marrum t̪ajɾijamaːka
   maːri maːri aʈimaj
t̪ukkam marrum makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi ɾaːd͡ʒas aʋaɾ
t̪iːmaj t͡ʃejpaʋaɾkaɭum uɳʈu manam t̪aɭaɾn̪t̪a
t̪aːɻʋu manappaːnmaj piʈiʋaːt̪am eːmaːrru t̪ajakkam
man̪t̪amaːna met̪uʋaːna n̪ampikkajjarra  iɾuɳʈa kuɻan̪t̪ajkaɭ
ariʋaːrral marrum urut̪ijajjum keːɭuŋkaɭ
muppeɾum piɾiʋu ʋerrijaːɭaɾiɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
iʋaj eʋʋaːru kuɳaŋkaɭaːl ʋeːrupaʈukinrana
puɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭum put̪t̪i n̪allat̪u
ʋaːɻkkajjin munnum pinnum
enna t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum enna t͡ʃejjakkuːʈaːt̪u
et̪arku aɲt͡ʃa ʋeːɳʈum et̪arku aɲt͡ʃakkuːʈaːt̪u
et̪u aːnmaːʋaj piɳajkkirat̪u marrum et̪u ʋiʈuʋikkirat̪u
at̪u t͡ʃat̪ʋaːnuʈajjat̪u iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː amajt̪i
maːɾaʈ enpat̪u t͡ʃaɾijaːkat̪ t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭum put̪t̪i
marrum t̪aʋaraːka arin̪t̪u enna t͡ʃejʋat̪u n̪allat̪u
enna t͡ʃejjakkuːʈaːt̪u innum puɾikirat̪u
urut̪ijaːna manat̪uʈan illaj allat̪u amajt̪ijaːna uɳmaj
it̪u ɾaːd͡ʒaːsuʈajjat̪u iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː marrum uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃimikka
t̪iːmaj enpat̪u iɾuɭil muːʈappaʈʈiɾukkum put̪t̪i
t̪aʋaraj t͡ʃaɾijenru paːɾkkirat̪u ellaːʋarrajjum paːɾkkirat̪u
uɳmajkku maːraːka piɾut̪ajjin makaneː
at̪u t̪amas iɾuɳʈa marrum aʋan̪ampikkaj
oɾu manit̪an urut̪ijuʈan iɾuppat̪u n̪allat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u it̪ajat̪ t̪uʈippukaɭaj aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃuʋaːt͡ʃat̪t̪aj maːsʈaɾ
ʋaːɻkkaj aʋaɾat̪u pulankaɭin t͡ʃejal t͡ʃaɾi t͡ʃejjappaʈʈat̪u
oɾupaோt̪um at͡ʃajkkappaʈaːt̪a n̪ampikkajjilum irajjat͡ʃt͡ʃat̪t̪ilum
at̪u t͡ʃat̪ʋaːnuʈajjat̪u iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː mikaʋum marrum n̪ijaːjamaːna
karaj paʈin̪t̪a oɾu manit̪an urut̪ijaːna t̪anmaj
t̪an kaʈamaj n̪aோkkam mujart͡ʃi muʈiʋu
ʋaːɻkkajkkaːkaʋum paொɾuʈkaɭin miːt̪aːna anpajp peruʋat̪arkaːkaʋum
aɾd͡ʒunaː ɾaːd͡ʒaːs peːɾaːɾʋam mut̪t̪iɾaj
muʈʈaːɭiʈam iɾukkum urut̪ijeː t͡ʃaோkam
aʋaɾat̪u t͡ʃaோmpal t̪ukkam marrum pajam aːkijaʋarruʈan oʈʈikkaொɳʈat̪u
aʋaɾat̪u muʈʈaːɭt̪anam marrum aʋan̪ampikkaj it̪upiɾit̪aːʋin makan
t̪amasiliɾun̪t̪u piran̪t̪at̪u iɾuɳʈa marrum t̪unpakaɾamaːnat̪u
meːlum keːɭ paɾat̪at̪ t̪alajʋaneː enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u
muːnruʋit̪amaːna inpaŋkaɭ uɭɭana
n̪alla inpam n̪ilajt̪t̪u n̪irkum inpam
eːjkku ʋalijaj ʋiɾaʈʈukirat̪u mut̪alil kat͡ʃappu
aːnmaːʋirku ʋiʂam aːnaːl pinnaɾ
amiɾt̪at̪t̪in t͡ʃuʋaj paோla inimaj at̪ajk kuʈijuŋkaɭ
at̪u aːʋijin aːɻamaːna uɭɭaʈakkat̪t̪il muɭajkkirat̪u
marrum ʋalimikun̪t̪a inpam piɳajppiliɾun̪t̪u pirakkirat̪u
pulankaɭukkum pulan ulakat̪t̪irkum iʈajjil inippu
amiɾt̪am at̪an mut̪al t͡ʃuʋaj aːnaːl kaʈajt͡ʃi t͡ʃuʋaj
ʋiʂam paோnra kat͡ʃappu ɾaːd͡ʒaːs iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
marrum t̪aʋaraːna marrum iɾuɳʈa inpam spiɾiŋs it̪u
t͡ʃaோmpal marrum paːʋam marrum muʈʈaːɭt̪anat̪t̪iliɾun̪t̪u mut̪alil
marrum kaʈajt͡ʃijil marrum anajt̪t̪u ʋaːɻkkaj muraj
aːnmaː t̪ikajkkirat̪u t̪aːmas iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
eːnenraːl puːmijilum t̪ejʋaŋkaɭukku n̪aʈuʋilum et̪uʋum ʋaːɻʋat̪illaj
ut͡ʃt͡ʃa ʋaːnat̪t̪il aːnaːl at̪an piɳajppu uɭɭat̪u
in̪t̪a muːnru kuɳaŋkaɭuʈan ijarkajjaːl ʋaʈiʋamajkkappaʈʈat̪u
piɾaːmaɳaɾ kʂat̪t̪iɾijaɾkaɭ ʋajt͡ʃijaɾkaɭin ʋeːlaj
meːlum t͡ʃuːt̪t̪iɾaɾkaɭeː oː un et̪iɾikaɭajk kaொnraʋaneː
t̪aɾaŋkaɭin kaːɾaɳat̪t̪aːl t͡ʃaɾi t͡ʃejjappaʈʈat̪u
oʋʋaொnrilum n̪aʈappaʈukirat̪u
oɾu piɾaːmaɳanin n̪arkuɳaŋkaɭ iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
aʋaɾat̪u ijalpil piran̪t̪aʋaɾkaɭ amajt̪ijaːnaʋaɾkaɭ
t̪annampikkaj mat̪am t̪uːjmaj
paொrumaj n̪eːɾmaj karral marrum t̪eɾin̪t̪u kaொɭɭut̪al
iɾukkum ʋiʂajaŋkaɭin uɳmaj oɾu kʂat̪t̪iɾijaɾin peɾumaj
t̪an ijalpil piran̪t̪u ʋiːɾam n̪eɾuppu
n̪ilajt̪t̪anmaj t̪iramaj t͡ʃaɳʈajjil aːʋi
marrum t̪iran̪t̪a kaj marrum unnat̪a mijan
manit̪aɾkaɭin aːɳʈaʋaɾaːka oɾu ʋajt͡ʃijaɾin paɳi
aʋanat̪u ijalpil piran̪t̪aʋan n̪ilat̪t̪aj uɻuʋat̪u
kaːln̪aʈaj ʋaɭaɾppu t̪uɳikaɾa ʋijaːpaːɾam oɾu t͡ʃuːt̪t̪iɾa aɾat͡ʃu
aʋaɾat̪u ijalpukku eːrrat̪u amajt͡ʃt͡ʃaɾaːkkuʋat̪u
jaːɾ t͡ʃejalpaʈukiraːɾkaɭaோ  ʋiʈaːmujart͡ʃijuʈan uɭɭaʈakkam 
ʋeːlaj aʋaɾukku ot̪ukkappaʈʈat̪u at̪u ennaʋaːka iɾukkum
paɾipuːɾaɳat̪t̪ajp piʈikkirat̪u eppaʈi oɾu manit̪an enru keːɭuŋkaɭ
mikaʋum t̪iɾupt̪ijaːka iɾuppat̪aːl muɻumajjajk kaɳʈarikirat̪u
aʋaɾ at̪aj ʋaɻipaːʈʈin muːlam kaɳʈupiʈikkiraːɾ  ʋeːlajjaːl t͡ʃejjappaʈʈaːɾ 
ujiɾkaɭ anajt̪t̪irkum aʋaneː aːt̪aːɾam
jaːɾaːl piɾapaɲt͡ʃam n̪iːʈʈikkappaʈʈat̪aோ aʋaɾaːl
uŋkaɭ t͡ʃaொn̪t̪a ʋeːlaj t̪aʋaru t͡ʃejt̪aːlum t͡ʃiran̪t̪at̪u
marraʋaɾkaɭin ʋeːlajjajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejʋat̪aj ʋiʈa t͡ʃirappaːkat͡ʃ t͡ʃejkireːn
paɳijaj munnirut̪t̪upaʋaɾ paːʋat̪t̪il ʋiɻamaːʈʈaːɾ
ijarkajjin kajjaːl aʋaɾaj amajkkaʋum jaːɾum paோka ʋeːɳʈaːm
aʋanat̪u ijalpaːna kaʈamaj iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː at̪u kurram t͡ʃumat̪t̪inaːlum
oʋʋaொɾu t͡ʃejalukkum oʋʋaொɾu t̪iːppiɻampu paோla paɻi uɳʈu
pukajjaːl muːʈappaʈʈiɾukkum an̪t̪a manit̪an maʈʈumeː aʈajkiraːn
ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejt̪a ʋeːlajjin t͡ʃaɾijaːna ʋaɭaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃi
manat̪aɭaʋil kaʈʈuppaːʈarra aːnmaː muɻuʋat̪umaːka aʈaŋki
eppaோt̪um iran̪t̪a aːt͡ʃajkaɭ muʈiʋukaɭ kajʋiʈappaʈʈana
kun̪t̪ijin makaneː enniʈamiɾun̪t̪u karrukkaொɭ it̪uʋum
eppaʈi oɾuʋaɾ puːɾaɳa amajt̪ijaj aʈajkiraːɾ
piɾammam ellaːʋarrilum ujaɾn̪t̪a ujaɾn̪t̪a ujaɾam
pakt̪i  t̪uːjmajjaːna kaʈʈuppaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈa it̪ajat̪t̪uʈan
iraj t͡ʃujakkaʈʈuppaːʈʈuʈan t̪an̪t̪iɾaŋkaɭaj ʋiʈʈuʋiʈut̪al
kaːt̪al marrum ʋeruppiliɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈa paːʈal marrum uɳaɾʋukaɭ
t̪animajjin n̪aʈuʋil ʋat͡ʃippat̪u uɳaʋu ut̪iɾippil
uʈal peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu marrum kiːɻppaʈiʋat̪arku aʈakkamaːna
eppaொɻut̪um punit̪a t̪ijaːnam t͡ʃejʋat̪aːka t͡ʃapat̪am t͡ʃejt̪eːn
uɳaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭil iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈuŋkaɭ t͡ʃujat̪t̪aj ʋiʈʈu ʋiʈuŋkaɭ
aːɳaʋam paொrumajjinmaj kaோpam peɾumaj
t͡ʃurruppuraŋkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u ʋiʈupaʈʈu amajt̪ijaːna onrum illaːt̪at̪u
appaʈippaʈʈaʋaɾ  uʈan orrumajjaːka ʋaɭaɾkiraːɾ
appaʈippaʈʈaʋaɾ piɾammat̪t̪uʈan ʋaɭaɾum amajt̪ijaːna
ini t̪ukkaŋkaɭ illaj aːt͡ʃajkaɭ illaj aʋaɾat̪u aːnmaː
ʋaːɻum anajt̪t̪ajjum t͡ʃamamaːka n̪eːt͡ʃippat̪u n̪anraːka n̪eːt͡ʃikkirat̪u
n̪aːn aʋarraj uɳʈaːkki ennaj aʈajkireːn
it̪eː anpinaːlum ʋaɻipaːʈʈinaːlum aʋan ariʋaːn
n̪aːn eʋʋaɭaʋu ujaɾn̪t̪a marrum arput̪amaːnaʋan
arin̪t̪u uʈaneː ennuɭ n̪uɻajkirat̪u
meːlum aʋaɾ t͡ʃejjum en̪t̪at͡ʃ t͡ʃejalkaɭum t͡ʃaɾi
ennil aʋaɾ aʈajkkalam paோl  aʋaɾ ʋenraːɾ
en aɾuɭaːl enrenrum enrum
n̪it̪t̪ija oːjʋu enaʋeː n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋerri peruŋkaɭ un eɳɳaŋkaɭil
enakkaːka n̪iː t͡ʃejʋat̪aj ellaːm t͡ʃej enakkaːka t̪ura
it̪ajat̪t̪ajjum manat̪ajjum ʋiɾuppat̪t̪ajjum enakkaːka t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃej
ennaj n̪ampi ʋaːɻka en miːt̪aːna n̪ampikkajjil
ellaː iʈaɾkaɭajjum en aɾuɭaːl ʋelʋaːj
aːnaːl uŋkaɭaj n̪ampi kaʋanikkaːmal
unnaːl aɻija muʈijaːt̪u in̪t̪a n̪aːɭil n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃaொnnaːl
uŋkaɭaj n̪ampi n̪aːn t͡ʃaɳʈajjiʈa maːʈʈeːn
ʋiːɳ n̪aோkkam n̪iɾuːpikkum uŋkaɭ kuɳaŋkaɭ
unnaj paோɾukkut̪ t̪uːɳʈum n̪iːŋkaɭ et̪ajt̪ t̪aʋiɾkkiriːɾkaɭ
n̪ijaːjamaːna maːjajkaɭaːl t̪aʋaraːka ʋaɻin̪aʈat̪t̪appaʈʈu n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪eːʈuʋiːɾkaɭ
uŋkaɭ ʋiɾuppat̪t̪irku maːraːka paɳi uŋkaɭukku ʋaɾumpaோt̪u
uŋkaɭ ijalpu amajppil t̪uːɳʈut̪alkaɭaj eɻupput̪al
manit̪aɾkaɭin it̪ajat̪t̪il oɾu maːsʈaɾ ʋaːɻkiraːɾ
aʋaɾkaɭin t͡ʃejalkaɭaj n̪uʈpamaːka iɻut̪t̪u  t͡ʃaɾaŋkaɭ
aʋaɾ en̪t̪a it͡ʃajkku n̪aʈanamaːʈuʋaːɾ uŋkaɭ muɻu aːnmaːʋuʈan
aʋaɾaj n̪ampuŋkaɭ aʋaɾaj uŋkaɭ t̪uɳajkku eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː
at̪anaːlappaʈijeː aɾd͡ʒunaːn̪iː aːt̪aːjam peruʋaːj
aʋaɾ aɾuɭaːl  murrum n̪immat̪i
n̪it̪t̪ija iʈam
iʋʋaːru n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪irakkappaʈʈiːɾkaɭ
in̪t̪a uɳmajjin uɳmaj maɾmam innum marajkkappaʈʈat̪u
en̪t̪a ɾakat͡ʃija maɾmat̪t̪ajjum ʋiʈa t̪ijaːnam t͡ʃej
marrum  n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋiɾumpijapaʈi  pinnaɾ t͡ʃejalpaʈuŋkaɭ
illaj aːnaːl miːɳʈum oɾumuraj
enat̪u kaʈajt͡ʃi ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjaj eʈut̪t̪uk kaொɭɭuŋkaɭ en ut͡ʃt͡ʃa aɾt̪t̪am uɭɭat̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ enakku ʋilajmat̪ipparraʋaɾ t͡ʃaɾi anpeː
keːɭ unat̪u aːrut̪alukkaːka it̪ajt͡ʃ t͡ʃaொlkireːn
un it̪ajat̪t̪aj enakkuk kaொʈu ennaj ʋaɳaŋku enakku t͡ʃeːʋaj t͡ʃej oʈʈikkaொɭkinrana
en miːt̪u n̪ampikkajjilum anpilum pajapakt̪ijilum
enaʋeː n̪iːŋkaɭ enniʈam ʋaːɾuŋkaɭ n̪aːn t͡ʃat̪t̪ijam t͡ʃejkireːn
eːnenraːl n̪iːŋkaɭ enakku inimajjaːnaʋaɾ
marrum aʋaɾkaɭaj ʋiʈuŋkaɭ 
t͡ʃaʈaŋkukaɭ marrum eɻut̪t̪u kaʈamajkaɭ enniʈam t̪anijaːka parakka
ennaj unat̪u oɾeː aʈajkkalamaːka aːkkuʋaːjaːka n̪aːn ʋiʈuʋippeːn
uŋkaɭ aːnmaː at̪an anajt̪t̪u paːʋaŋkaɭiliɾun̪t̪um makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːka iɾuŋkaɭ
maraj punit̪a kiɾuʂɳaɾ kuːrukiraːɾ
n̪ampikkaj illaːt̪aʋaniʈamiɾun̪t̪u it̪u
ʋaɳaŋkaːt̪aʋaɾ t̪eːʈaːt̪aʋaɾ
aʋaɭ peːt͡ʃumpaோt̪u ɲaːnat̪t̪in paோt̪anaj
keːli t͡ʃejjum ellaː manit̪aɾkaɭiʈamiɾun̪t̪um at̪aj maraj
aːnaːl eŋkiɾun̪t̪aːlum man̪t̪aj n̪aʈuʋeː
en kaːt̪alaɾkaɭil oɾuʋaɾ karpippaːɾ
in̪t̪a t̪ejʋiːkamaːna put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anamaːna peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu 
kaொɳʈu ʋaɾa n̪ampikkajjil karpit̪t̪al
aʋaɾkaɭukku uɳmaj marrum piɾat͡ʃaːt̪am
enakku maɾijaːt̪ajjuʈan
piɾammaːʋiʈam aʋaɾ ʋaɾukiraːɾ
illaj n̪iːŋkaɭ eŋkum kaːɳa muʈijaːt̪u
anajt̪t̪u manit̪akulat̪t̪in en̪t̪a manit̪anum
enakkaːka anpaːna t͡ʃejalajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪al
anpaːnaʋaɾkaɭum iɾukka maːʈʈaːɾkaɭ
en puːmijil aːm meːlum
in̪t̪a uɾajjaːʈalajp paʈippaʋaɾ
t͡ʃamaʋeɭijil eŋkaɭaːl n̪aʈat̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u
pakt̪ijuʈanum man̪t̪amaːkaʋum t͡ʃin̪t̪it̪t̪u
aʋaɾ enakku t̪ijaːkam t͡ʃejt̪aːɾ
kiɾuʂɳan ippaʈit̪t̪aːn peːt͡ʃukiraːn
aːm marrum jaːɾ muɻu n̪ampikkaj
at̪u t͡ʃaொlʋat̪aj put̪t̪it͡ʃaːlit̪t̪anamaːka keːɭuŋkaɭ
t͡ʃaːn̪t̪amaːka keːʈkiraːɾ  aʋaɾ irakkum paோt̪u
n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka aʋaɾuʈajja aːʋi eɻumpum
piɭesʈ iɾukkum an̪t̪a pakut̪ikaɭukku
t͡ʃat̪aj illaːt̪a makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna oːjʋil
in̪t̪ija iɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː it̪aj n̪iːŋkaɭ keːʈʈiːɾkaɭaː
mana n̪aோkkat̪t̪uʈan ellaː arijaːmajjum uɳʈu
et̪u un piɾat͡ʃt͡ʃanajjaj uɳʈaːkkijat̪u  marajn̪t̪u paோnat̪u en aɾd͡ʒun
aɾd͡ʒunaː
t̪unpamum arijaːmajjum n̪iːŋkina oɭi
umat̪u aɾuɭaːl enniʈam ʋan̪t̪eːn aːɳʈaʋaɾeː
ippaோt̪u n̪aːn t͡ʃaɾijaːkiʋiʈʈeːn en t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkam n̪iːŋkiʋiʈʈat̪u
umat̪u ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajjinpaʈi n̪aːnum t͡ʃejʋeːn
t͡ʃaɲt͡ʃajaː
iʋʋaːru n̪aːn kiɾuʂɳaɾin kaɾuɳaj uɾajjaj t͡ʃeːkaɾit̪t̪eːn en aɾat͡ʃeː
in̪t̪a ɲaːnamaːna marrum at̪it͡ʃajamaːna ʋiʂajat̪t̪aj n̪aːn manat̪uʈan t͡ʃiliɾppuʈan t͡ʃaொnneːn
t͡ʃiran̪t̪a ʋijaːt͡ʃaɾin karral eɻut̪t̪in muːlam kiɾuʂɳaɾin t͡ʃujaɾuːpam eppaʈi arijappaʈʈat̪u
jaோkaː jaோkaːʋin irajʋan kaːʈʈappaʈum ujaɾn̪t̪a uɳmajjum appaʈit̪t̪aːn
aːm en ɾaːd͡ʒaːʋaːkija aːɳʈaʋaɾeː n̪aːn miːɳʈum n̪inajʋukuːɾumpaோt̪u
aɾd͡ʒunanum kaʈaʋuɭum peːt͡ʃukiraːɾkaɭ in̪t̪a punit̪a ʋikaːɾam
en makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi peɾit̪u an̪t̪a aɻakaj n̪aːn uɳaɾumpaோt̪u ​​kaʈan̪t̪u t͡ʃellum peːt͡ʃt͡ʃu
kaɳɳukkut̪ t̪eɾijum marrum ʋerumajjaːka iɾukkum haɾikku aʈajja n̪aːkku illaj
en arput̪am marrum en anpu marrum peːɾinpam oː ʋillaːɭaniɭaʋaɾat͡ʃeː ʋaːɻka
oː kiɾuʂɳaː jaோkak kaʈaʋuɭeː n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka t̪aோlʋi aʈajjaːt̪u
aːt͡ʃiːɾʋaːt̪amum ʋerrijum t͡ʃakt̪ijum umat̪u ʋallamajkkaːka
in̪t̪a paːʈal aɾd͡ʒuniʈam eŋkiɾun̪t̪u ʋaɾukirat̪u kaʈaʋuɭuʈan eppaʈi peːt͡ʃinaːɾ
iŋkeː muʈikirat̪u at̪t̪ijaːjam 
maோkʂat͡ʃanjaːt͡ʃajaோk enra t̪alajppil
allat̪u ʋiʈut̪alaj marrum t̪urappat̪an muːlam mat̪at̪t̪in put̪t̪akam
pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪aj




# miːɳʈum miːɳʈum ʋaɾum t͡ʃila ʋaɾikaɭ iŋkeː t̪aʋiɾkkappaʈʈuɭɭana

# ʋeːt̪a mat̪at̪t̪in t̪aொɻiln̪uʈpa t͡ʃaொrraொʈaɾkaɭ

# in̪t̪a pat̪t̪i muɻuʋat̪um mikaʋum iːʈupaːʈu kaொɳʈat̪u marrum ʋaɻaŋkuʋat̪u kaʈinam

# t͡ʃaːŋkjaːnanum jaோkinanum iŋkeː aɾt̪t̪at̪t̪il iʈamaːrram t͡ʃejjappaʈa ʋeːɳʈum enru n̪aːn urut̪ijaːka uɳaɾkireːn

# n̪aːn iŋkeː t̪ullijamaːka t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkikkireːn

# t͡ʃuːɾijanin pejaɾ

# paɻat̪t̪in miːt̪u aːt͡ʃaj illaːmal

# at̪aːʋat̪u makiɻt͡ʃt͡ʃi marrum t̪ukkam ʋerri marrum t̪aோlʋi ʋeppam marrum kuɭiɾ&

# at̪aːʋat̪u uʈal

# t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪at̪t̪il aːt̪maːʋin iɾaʈʈaj aɾt̪t̪at̪t̪il in̪t̪a n̪aːʈakam uɭɭat̪u

# enaʋeː at͡ʃal

# t̪aːɻn̪t̪a marrum pit͡ʃaːt͡ʃu t̪anmaj kaொɳʈaʋaɾkaɭ

# kiɾuʂɳaː

# n̪aːn iŋkeː d͡ʒanmaː pirappu paʈit̪t̪eːn d͡ʒaːɾaː alla ʋajat̪u

# t͡ʃila ʋeːt̪aːn̪t̪ikaɭin t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkat̪t̪irku iʈamillaːt̪a iʈajt͡ʃt͡ʃeɾukalaːka t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a uɾajjin pat̪t̪u ʋaɾikaɭaj iŋku n̪iɾaːkaɾit̪t̪uɭɭeːn

# iŋkuɭɭa t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪ak kaʋit̪aj n̪aʈaj marrum n̪aʈajjin ujaɾat̪t̪irku ujaɾkirat̪u miːʈʈaɾaj maːrruʋat̪an muːlam n̪aːn kurikka mujart͡ʃit̪t̪eːn

# ahint͡ʃaː

# aɻijaːmajjin t̪eːn

# t̪i d͡ʒaːp enru aɻajkkappaʈukirat̪u

# t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a ʋaːɾt̪t̪ajkaɭin kuːʈʈu ʋaʈiʋam

# kamalaːpat̪ɾaːkʂaː

# iʋaj anajt̪t̪um hin̪t̪u paːn̪t̪ijanin t̪ejʋiːka allat̪u t̪ejʋiːka kaʈʈaɭajkaɭ

# kaʈaʋuɭin kaʈaʋuɭeː unakku n̪amaskaːɾam t͡ʃaːt̪akamaːka iɾu

# kaːrru

# anaːpeːkʂaːʋajp parri paːɾkkaʋillaj

# makaːpaːɾat̪at̪t̪in kalkat̪t̪aː pat̪ippil in̪t̪a muːnru t̪aொʈakka ʋaɾikaɭ uɭɭana

# it̪u kʂeːt̪ɾakʂeːt̪ɾad͡ʒɲajaோd͡ʒɲaːnan jat̪ t̪ad͡ʒɲan mat̪an mama enpat̪an aɾukiluɭɭa t͡ʃaːt̪t̪ijamaːna pat̪ippaːkum

# t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪at̪t̪in iɾaɳʈu ʋaɾikaɭaj n̪aːn iŋkeː t̪aʋiɾkkireːn ʋeɭippaʈajjaːka t͡ʃila ʋeːt̪aːn̪t̪ikaɭaːl iʈajkkaɳikkappaʈʈat̪u

# kaɾuppajkaɭ

# n̪aːn iŋkeː t͡ʃamaskiɾut̪a ʋat͡ʃanaŋkaɭaj kaɾut̪t̪il kaொɭɭaʋillaj  aʋaj oːɾaɭaʋu t͡ʃut̪an̪t̪iɾamaːka ʋaɻaŋkappaʈʈuɭɭana  t̪iɾu ʈeːʋisin ʋeːt̪aŋkaɭin at̪ikaːɾat̪t̪in miːt̪aːna t̪aːkkut̪al aːnaːl oɾu aɻakaːna paːʈal at̪t̪ijaːjam oɾu put̪ija at̪t̪ijin uʋamaj maɾam

# n̪aːn iŋkeː oɾu ʋat͡ʃanat̪t̪aj t̪aʋiɾkkireːn ʋeɭippaʈajjaːka iʈajt͡ʃt͡ʃeɾukal

# at͡ʃuɾaɾkaɭin lajʈ

# t̪iɾu ʈeːʋisuʈan pat̪t̪u muʈiʋaːna slaோkaŋkaɭaj n̪aːn t̪aʋiɾkkireːn

# ɾaːkʂasaɾkaɭum jakʂaɾkaɭum uɾuʋamarraʋaɾkaɭ aːnaːl peɾum t͡ʃakt̪i paɾit͡ʃukaɭ marrum aɻaku kaொɳʈaʋaɾkaɭ at̪eː t͡ʃamajam kaɾuɳajjuɭɭaʋaɾkaɭ

# iʋaj t̪iːja alajjum peːjkaɭin aːʋikaɭ

# jat̪aːjamaːn iɾaʋin kaɳkaːɳippukkup piraku eɲt͡ʃijiɾukkum uɳaʋu in̪t̪ijaːʋil it̪u an̪eːkamaːka maோt͡ʃamaːkiʋiʈum

# mikaʋum t͡ʃan̪t̪eːkat̪t̪irkuɾija n̪ampakat̪t̪anmajjin kaːɾaɳamaːka irut̪i slaோkaŋkaɭaj n̪aːn t̪aʋiɾkkireːn











t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in muʈiʋu kuʈʈanpeɾk pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin minput̪t̪akam an̪aːmat̪eːjaɾaːl

*** in̪t̪at̪ t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in muʈiʋu kuʈʈanpeɾk pakaʋat̪ kiːt̪ajjin minput̪t̪akam ***

***** in̪t̪a kaோppu  allat̪u  enru pejaɾiʈappaʈa ʋeːɳʈum *****
it̪uʋum palʋeːru ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭin anajt̪t̪u t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja kaோppukaɭum it̪il kaːɳappaʈum
///////

d͡ʒeːt͡ʃi pajjaɾs t̪ajaːɾit̪t̪uɭɭaːɾ al hejinsin  pat̪ippu

put̪uppikkappaʈʈa pat̪ippukaɭ mun̪t̪ajja pat̪ippaj maːrrum  paɻajja pat̪ippukaɭ
marupejaɾiʈappaʈum

paொt̪u ʈaொmajn at͡ʃt͡ʃu pat̪ippukaɭil iɾun̪t̪u paʈajppukaɭaj uɾuʋaːkkuʋat̪u illaj enru aɾt̪t̪am
in̪t̪a paʈajppukaɭil oɾuʋaɾ junajʈeʈ sʈeːʈs pat̪ippuɾimaj perruɭɭaːɾ enaʋeː arakkaʈʈaɭaj
marrum n̪iːŋkaɭ illaːmal at̪aj ameɾikkaːʋil n̪akaleʈut̪t̪u ʋin̪ijaோkikka muʈijum
anumat̪i marrum kaːppuɾimaj ɾaːjalʈi t͡ʃelut̪t̪aːmal t͡ʃirappu ʋit̪ikaɭ
in̪t̪a uɾimat̪t̪in paொt̪uʋaːna pajanpaːʈʈu ʋit̪imurajkaɭil kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭaj n̪akaleʈut̪t̪u ʋin̪ijaோkit̪t̪al
t̪iʈʈam  kaɾut̪t̪u marrum ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj paːt̪ukaːkka t̪iʈʈam
kuʈʈanpeɾk oɾu pat̪iʋut͡ʃejjappaʈʈa ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj n̪iːŋkaɭ iɾun̪t̪aːl pajanpaʈut̪t̪appaʈaːmal iɾukkalaːm
n̪iːŋkaɭ kurippiʈʈa anumat̪ijajp peraːt̪a ʋaɾaj minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭukkaːna kaʈʈaɳam n̪iːŋkaɭ enraːl
in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akat̪t̪in n̪akalkaɭukku iɳaŋka kaʈʈaɳam et̪uʋum ʋat͡ʃuːlikka ʋeːɳʈaːm
ʋit̪ikaɭ mikaʋum eɭit̪aːnat̪u in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akat̪t̪aj n̪iːŋkaɭ en̪t̪a n̪aோkkat̪t̪irkaːkaʋum pajanpaʈut̪t̪alaːm
ʋaɻit̪t̪aோnral paʈajppukaɭ arikkajkaɭ n̪ikaɻt͡ʃt͡ʃikaɭ marrum
aːɾaːjt͡ʃt͡ʃi aʋaj maːrrappaʈʈu at͡ʃt͡ʃiʈappaʈʈu kaொʈukkappaʈalaːm  n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃejjalaːm
paொt̪u ʈaொmajn minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭuʈan n̪aʈajmurajjil et̪ajjum marupakiɾʋu enpat̪u
ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj uɾimat̪t̪irku uʈpaʈʈat̪u kurippaːka ʋaɳikam
marupakiɾʋu



*** t̪aொʈaŋku muɻu uɾimam ***

muɻu t̪iʈʈam kuʈʈanpeɾk uɾimam
in̪t̪ap paʈajppaj ʋin̪ijaோkikkum mun allat̪u pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪arku mun it̪ajp paʈikkaʋum

ilaʋat͡ʃat̪t̪aj ʋiɭampaɾappaʈut̪t̪um t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem paɳijajp paːt̪ukaːkka
in̪t̪a ʋeːlajjajp pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪an muːlam allat̪u ʋin̪ijaோkippat̪an muːlam minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭin ʋin̪ijaோkam
allat̪u t̪iʈʈam enra t͡ʃaொrraொʈaɾuʈan t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja ʋeːru en̪t̪a ʋeːlajjum
 muɻu t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in anajt̪t̪u ʋit̪imurajkaɭukkum iɳaŋka oppukkaொɭkiriːɾkaɭ
 uɾimam in̪t̪ak kaோppu allat̪u aːnlajnil kiʈajkkum
/


piɾiʋu  paொt̪u pajanpaːʈʈu ʋit̪imurajkaɭ marrum marupakiɾʋu t̪iʈʈam 
minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭ

eː kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in en̪t̪ap pakut̪ijajjum paʈippat̪an muːlam allat̪u pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪an muːlam
minnaɳu ʋeːlaj n̪iːŋkaɭ paʈit̪t̪u puɾin̪t̪u oppukkaொɳʈiːɾkaɭ enru kurippiʈukiriːɾkaɭ
in̪t̪a uɾimam marrum ariʋut͡ʃaːɾ t͡ʃaொt̪t̪in anajt̪t̪u ʋit̪imurajkaɭajjum eːrkaʋum
ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj/pat̪ippuɾimaj oppan̪t̪am n̪iːŋkaɭ oppukkaொɭɭaʋillaj enraːl anajt̪t̪ajjum kaʈajppiʈikka ʋeːɳʈum
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭaj n̪iːŋkaɭ pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪aj n̪irut̪t̪iʋiʈʈu t̪iɾumpaʋum allat̪u aɻikkaʋum ʋeːɳʈum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭin anajt̪t̪u n̪akalkaɭum uŋkaɭ ʋat͡ʃam uɭɭat̪u
t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in n̪akalajp peruʋat̪arku allat̪u at̪arkaːna aɳukalajp peruʋat̪arku n̪iːŋkaɭ kaʈʈaɳam t͡ʃelut̪t̪inaːl
 minnaɳu ʋeːlaj marrum n̪iːŋkaɭ kaʈʈuppaʈuʋat̪arku oppukkaொɭɭaʋillaj
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭinpaʈi n̪iːŋkaɭ an̪t̪a n̪apaɾiʈamiɾun̪t̪u paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpap peralaːm allat̪u
pat̪t̪i  il kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭapaʈi n̪iːŋkaɭ jaːɾukku kaʈʈaɳam t͡ʃelut̪t̪iniːɾkaɭ

pi   enpat̪u pat̪iʋu t͡ʃejjappaʈʈa ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj at̪u maʈʈum iɾukkalaːm
elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlajjil pajanpaʈut̪t̪appaʈum allat̪u en̪t̪a ʋakajjilum t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja n̪apaɾkaɭaːl
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭukku kaʈʈuppaʈuʋat̪aj oppukkaொɭkireːn oɾu t͡ʃila uɭɭana
peɾumpaːlaːna   elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlajkaɭil n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃejjakkuːʈija ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in muɻu ʋit̪imurajkaɭukku iɳaŋkaːmal kuːʈa paːɾkkaʋum
pat̪t̪i  kiːɻeː t̪iʈʈat̪t̪il n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃejjakkuːʈija pala ʋiʂajaŋkaɭ uɭɭana
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭajp pinparrinaːl  elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejjum
marrum t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minnaɳukkaːna ilaʋat͡ʃa et̪iɾkaːla aɳukalajp paːt̪ukaːkka ut̪aʋuŋkaɭ
ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejkirat̪u kiːɻeː uɭɭa pat̪t̪i  ajp paːɾkkaʋum

t͡ʃi t̪iʈʈam kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkija kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj t̪i arakkaʈʈaɭaj
allat̪u  pɾaːd͡ʒekʈʈin t͡ʃeːkaɾippil oɾu t̪aொkuppu pat̪ippuɾimaj perruɭɭat̪u
 minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭ eːrakkurajja anajt̪t̪u t̪anippaʈʈa ʋeːlajkaɭum
t͡ʃeːkaɾippu ameɾikkaːʋil paொt̪u kaɭat̪t̪il uɭɭat̪u oɾu enraːl
t̪anippaʈʈa ʋeːlaj ameɾikkaːʋil paொt̪u kaɭat̪t̪il uɭɭat̪u marrum n̪iːŋkaɭ
junajʈeʈ sʈeːʈsil uɭɭat̪u uŋkaɭajt̪ t̪aʈukka n̪aːŋkaɭ uɾimaj kaோɾaʋillaj
ʋaɻit̪t̪aோnralaj n̪akaleʈut̪t̪al ʋin̪ijaோkit̪t̪al n̪ikaɻt̪t̪ut̪al kaːʈt͡ʃippaʈut̪t̪ut̪al allat̪u uɾuʋaːkkut̪al
pɾaːd͡ʒekʈ kuʈʈanpeɾk parrija anajt̪t̪u kurippukaɭum iɾukkum ʋaɾaj ʋeːlajjin aʈippaʈajjil t͡ʃejalpaʈukirat̪u
akarrappaʈukinrana n̪it͡ʃt͡ʃajamaːka n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪iʈʈat̪t̪irku aːt̪aɾaʋaɭippiːɾkaɭ enru n̪ampukiraோm
kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem n̪aோkkam minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭukkaːna ilaʋat͡ʃa aɳukalaj uːkkuʋikkirat̪u
t͡ʃut̪an̪t̪iɾamaːka pakiɾt̪al t̪iʈʈam  ʋit̪imurajkaɭukku iɳaŋka ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejkirat̪u
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem pejaɾaj ʋajt̪t̪iɾuppat̪arkaːna in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪am
ʋeːlaj in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭukku n̪iːŋkaɭ eɭit̪aːka iɳaŋka muʈijum
in̪t̪a ʋeːlajjaj at̪an iɳajkkappaʈʈa muɻu t̪iʈʈat̪t̪uʈan at̪eː ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪il ʋajt̪t̪iɾut̪t̪al
kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem uɾimat̪t̪aj marraʋaɾkaɭuʈan kaʈʈaɳam illaːmal pakiɾum paோt̪u

 n̪iːŋkaɭ iɾukkum iʈat̪t̪in pat̪ippuɾimajt͡ʃ t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭum n̪iɾʋakikkinrana
in̪t̪a ʋeːlajjaj n̪iːŋkaɭ enna t͡ʃejja muʈijum peɾumpaːlaːna n̪aːʈukaɭil pat̪ippuɾimajt͡ʃ t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭ uɭɭana
maːrrat̪t̪in n̪ilajjaːna n̪ilaj n̪iːŋkaɭ ameɾikkaːʋirku ʋeɭijeː iɾun̪t̪aːl t͡ʃaɾipaːɾkkaʋum
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭukku kuːʈut̪alaːka uŋkaɭ n̪aːʈʈin t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭ
pat̪iʋirakkuʋat̪arku mun n̪akaleʈuppat̪arku mun kaːʈt͡ʃippaʈut̪t̪ut̪al n̪ikaɻt̪t̪ut̪al ʋin̪ijaோkam t͡ʃejt̪al allat̪u
in̪t̪a ʋeːlaj allat̪u ʋeːru eːt̪eːnum t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in aʈippaʈajjil ʋaɻit̪t̪aோnral paʈajppukaɭaj uɾuʋaːkkut̪al
 ʋeːlaj arakkaʈʈaɭaj it̪u t̪aொʈaɾpaːka en̪t̪ap piɾat̪in̪it̪it̪t̪uʋat̪t̪ajjum aɭikkaʋillaj
ajkkija n̪aːʈukaɭukku ʋeɭijeː uɭɭa en̪t̪aʋaொɾu paʈajppin pat̪ippuɾimaj n̪ilaj
maːn̪ilaŋkaɭil

i pɾaːd͡ʒekʈ kuʈʈanpeɾk parrija anajt̪t̪u kurippukaɭajjum n̪iːŋkaɭ akarraːt̪a ʋaɾaj

i pinʋaɾum ʋaːkkijam t͡ʃejalil uɭɭa iɳajppukaɭuʈan allat̪u pira uʈanaʈi
aɳukal muɻu   uɾimam mukkijamaːkat̪ t̪aோnra ʋeːɳʈum
kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in en̪t̪ap piɾat̪ijum ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejjum paோt̪ellaːm en̪t̪a ʋeːlajjum
puɾaːd͡ʒekʈ kuʈʈanpeɾk enra t͡ʃaொrraொʈaɾ t̪aோnrum allat̪u t̪iʈʈam enra t͡ʃaொrraொʈaɾ t̪aோnrum
kuʈʈanpeɾk t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajjat̪u aɳukappaʈʈat̪u kaːʈʈappaʈʈat̪u n̪ikaɻt̪t̪appaʈʈat̪u paːɾkkappaʈʈat̪u
n̪akaleʈukkappaʈʈat̪u allat̪u ʋin̪ijaோkikkappaʈʈat̪u

in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akam en̪t̪a iʈat̪t̪ilum en̪t̪a t͡ʃelaʋum illaːmal eʋaɾum pajanpaʈut̪t̪akkuːʈijat̪u
kiʈʈat̪t̪aʈʈa en̪t̪a kaʈʈuppaːʈukaɭum illaj n̪iːŋkaɭ at̪aj n̪akaleʈukkalaːm kaொʈukkalaːm allat̪u kaொʈukkalaːm
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk uɾimat̪t̪in ʋit̪imurajkaɭin kiːɻ at̪aj miːɳʈum pajanpaʈut̪t̪aʋum
in̪t̪a minput̪t̪akat̪t̪uʈan allat̪u  il aːnlajnil

i oɾu t̪anippaʈʈa t̪iʈʈamaːna  minnaɳu ʋeːlaj perappaʈʈaːl
paொt̪u ʈaொmajnil iɾun̪t̪u at̪ajk kurikkum ariʋippu illaj
pat̪ippuɾimajt̪aːɾaɾin anumat̪ijuʈan iʈukajjiʈappaʈʈat̪u paʈajppaj n̪akaleʈukka muʈijum
marrum ameɾikkaːʋil uɭɭa jaːɾukkum en̪t̪a kaʈʈaɳamum t͡ʃelut̪t̪aːmal ʋin̪ijaோkikkappaʈʈat̪u
allat̪u kaʈʈaɳam n̪iːŋkaɭ oɾu ʋeːlajjaj marupakiɾʋu t͡ʃejt̪aːl allat̪u at̪arkaːna aɳukalaj ʋaɻaŋkinaːl
  enra t͡ʃaொrraொʈaɾuʈan t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja allat̪u t̪aோnrum
ʋeːlaj n̪iːŋkaɭ pat̪t̪ikaɭ  in t̪eːʋajkaɭukku iɳaŋka ʋeːɳʈum
 muːlam allat̪u ʋeːlajjajp pajanpaʈut̪t̪uʋat̪arkaːna anumat̪ijajp peraʋum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj  allat̪u
i

 oɾu t̪anippaʈʈa t̪iʈʈam  minnaɳu ʋeːlaj iʈukajjiʈappaʈʈaːl
pat̪ippuɾimajt̪aːɾaɾin anumat̪ijuʈan uŋkaɭ pajanpaːʈu marrum ʋin̪ijaோkam
 mut̪al  ʋaɾajjilaːna iɾaɳʈu pat̪t̪ikaɭukkum meːlum eːt̪eːnum kuːʈut̪alaːkaʋum iɳaŋka ʋeːɳʈum
pat̪ippuɾimajt̪aːɾaɾaːl ʋit̪ikkappaʈʈa ʋit̪imurajkaɭ kuːʈut̪al ʋit̪imurajkaɭ iɳajkkappaʈum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem uɾimat̪t̪uʈan iʈukajjiʈappaʈʈa anajt̪t̪u paʈajppukaɭukkum
pat̪ippuɾimajt̪aːɾaɾin anumat̪i in̪t̪ap paɳijin t̪aொʈakkat̪t̪il kaːɳappaʈʈat̪u

i kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈam muɻuʋat̪ajjum t̪uɳʈikkaʋaோ allat̪u piɾikkaʋaோ allat̪u akarraʋaோ ʋeːɳʈaːm
in̪t̪ap paʈajppin uɾima ʋit̪imurajkaɭ allat̪u it̪an oɾu pakut̪ijajk kaொɳʈa kaோppukaɭ
t̪iʈʈam  uʈan t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja ʋeːlaj allat̪u ʋeːru eːt̪eːnum ʋeːlaj

 it̪aj n̪akaleʈukkaʋaோ kaːʈt͡ʃippaʈut̪t̪aʋaோ n̪ikaɻt̪t̪aʋaோ ʋin̪ijaோkikkaʋaோ allat̪u maruʋin̪ijaோkikkaʋaோ ʋeːɳʈaːm
minnaɳu ʋeːlaj allat̪u in̪t̪a minnaɳu ʋeːlajjin en̪t̪ap pakut̪ijum illaːmal
pat̪t̪i  il kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭa ʋaːkkijat̪t̪aj mukkijamaːkak kaːʈʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃejalil uɭɭa iɳajppukaɭ allat̪u t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in muɻu ʋit̪imurajkaɭukkaːna uʈanaʈi aɳukal
 uɾimam

i in̪t̪a ʋeːlajjaj n̪iːŋkaɭ en̪t̪a pajnaɾijilum maːrri ʋin̪ijaோkikkalaːm
t͡ʃuɾukkappaʈʈa kurikkappaʈʈa uɾimajjarra allat̪u t̪anijuɾima ʋaʈiʋam uʈpaʈa
t͡ʃaொl t͡ʃejalaːkkam allat̪u ujaɾ uɾaj ʋaʈiʋam iɾuppinum n̪iːŋkaɭ aɳukalaj ʋaɻaŋkinaːl allat̪u
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem paɳijin n̪akalkaɭaj ʋeːru ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪il ʋin̪ijaோkikkaʋum
piɭajn ʋeɳɳilaː  allat̪u at̪ikaːɾappuːɾʋa pat̪ippil pajanpaʈut̪t̪appaʈum pira ʋaʈiʋam
at̪ikaːɾappuːɾʋa t̪iʈʈam  iɳajjat̪aɭat̪t̪il  ʋeɭijiʈappaʈʈat̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ kuːʈut̪al t͡ʃelaʋu kaʈʈaɳam allat̪u pajanaɾukku en̪t̪a t͡ʃelaʋum illaːmal ʋaɻaŋka ʋeːɳʈum
n̪akal n̪akalaj eːrrumat̪i t͡ʃejʋat̪arkaːna ʋaɻimuraj allat̪u n̪akalajp peruʋat̪arkaːna ʋaɻimuraj
kaோɾikkaj at̪an at͡ʃal pɭajn ʋeɳɳilaː  allat̪u marraʋarril ʋeːlaj
ʋaʈiʋam en̪t̪a maːrru ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪ilum muɻu t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem iɾukka ʋeːɳʈum
pat̪t̪i  il kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭapaʈi uɾimam

i aɳukal paːɾppat̪u kaːʈt͡ʃippaʈut̪t̪ut̪al aːkijaʋarrukku kaʈʈaɳam ʋat͡ʃuːlikka ʋeːɳʈaːm
en̪t̪a t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem paɳikaɭajt͡ʃ t͡ʃejt̪al n̪akaleʈut̪t̪al allat̪u ʋin̪ijaோkit̪t̪al
n̪iːŋkaɭ pat̪t̪i  allat̪u  uʈan iɳaŋkaʋillaj enraːl

i n̪akalkaɭukku allat̪u ʋaɻaŋkuʋat̪arku n̪iːŋkaɭ n̪ijaːjamaːna kaʈʈaɳam ʋat͡ʃuːlikkalaːm
t̪iʈʈam  minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭukkaːna aɳukal allat̪u ʋin̪ijaோkam ʋaɻaŋkappaʈukirat̪u
an̪t̪a

 n̪iːŋkaɭ perum maொt̪t̪a laːpat̪t̪il % ɾaːjalʈi kaʈʈaɳam t͡ʃelut̪t̪ukiriːɾkaɭ
t̪iʈʈam  ʋeːlajkaɭin pajanpaːʈu murajjajp pajanpaʈut̪t̪i kaɳakkiʈappaʈukirat̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ eːrkanaʋeː uŋkaɭ paொɾun̪t̪akkuːʈija ʋaɾikaɭaj kaɳakkiʈa pajanpaʈut̪t̪ukiriːɾkaɭ kaʈʈaɳam aːkum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾajjin uɾimajjaːɭaɾukku kaʈanpaʈʈuɭɭat̪u aːnaːl aʋaɾ
kku in̪t̪ap pat̪t̪ijin kiːɻ ɾaːjalʈikaɭaj n̪ankaொʈajjaːka ʋaɻaŋka oppukkaொɳʈaːɾ
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkija kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj ɾaːjalʈi kaொʈuppanaʋukaɭ
oʋʋaொɾu t̪eːt̪ijajjum t̪aொʈaɾn̪t̪u  n̪aːʈkaɭukkuɭ t͡ʃelut̪t̪a ʋeːɳʈum
uŋkaɭ kaːlamuraj ʋaɾijajt̪ t̪ajaːɾikkaʋum allat̪u t͡ʃaʈʈappuːɾʋamaːka t̪ajaːɾ t͡ʃejja ʋeːɳʈum
t̪iɾumpukirat̪u ɾaːjalʈi kaொʈuppanaʋukaɭ t̪eɭiʋaːkak kurikkappaʈa ʋeːɳʈum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭajkku anuppappaʈʈat̪u
piɾiʋu  il kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭa mukaʋaɾi n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ parrija t̪akaʋal
t̪iʈʈam kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj

 ariʋikkum pajanaɾaːl t͡ʃelut̪t̪appaʈʈa en̪t̪ap paɳat̪t̪ajjum muɻumajjaːkat̪ t̪iɾumpap peruʋiːɾkaɭ
ɾat͡ʃiːt̪u kiʈajt̪t̪a  n̪aːʈkaɭukkuɭ n̪iːŋkaɭ eɻut̪t̪uppuːɾʋamaːka allat̪u minnaɲt͡ʃal muːlam
muɻu t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋit̪imurajkaɭaj eːrkaʋillaj
uɾimam at̪t̪akajja pajanaɾaj n̪iːŋkaɭ t̪iɾumpap pera ʋeːɳʈum allat̪u
ijarpijal uːʈakat̪t̪il uɭɭa paʈajppukaɭin anajt̪t̪u n̪akalkaɭajjum aɻikkaʋum
marrum anajt̪t̪u pajanpaːʈu marrum pira n̪akalkaɭukkaːna anajt̪t̪u aɳukalaj n̪irut̪t̪aʋum
t̪iʈʈam  ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejkirat̪u

 n̪iːŋkaɭ pat̪t̪i  kku iɳaŋka en̪t̪aʋaொɾu muɻu paɳat̪t̪ajjum t̪iɾumpap perukiriːɾkaɭ
oɾu ʋeːlaj allat̪u maːrru n̪akal oɾu kurajpaːʈu iɾun̪t̪aːl paɳam
minnaɳu ʋeːlaj  n̪aːʈkaɭukkuɭ kaɳʈarijappaʈʈu uŋkaɭukku ariʋikkappaʈum
ʋeːlajjin ɾat͡ʃiːt̪u

 in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in marra ellaː ʋit̪imurajkaɭukkum n̪iːŋkaɭ ilaʋat͡ʃamaːka iɳaŋkukiriːɾkaɭ
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem paɳikaɭ ʋin̪ijaோkam

i n̪iːŋkaɭ kaʈʈaɳam ʋat͡ʃuːlikka ʋiɾumpinaːl allat̪u t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋin̪ijaோkikkaʋum
elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlaj allat̪u ʋeːlajkaɭin kuɻu amajkkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪aj ʋiʈa ʋeʋʋeːru ʋit̪imurajkaɭil
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪il n̪iːŋkaɭ eɻut̪t̪uppuːɾʋamaːka anumat̪i pera ʋeːɳʈum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj marrum majkkeːl
haːɾʈ t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾajjin uɾimajjaːɭaɾ t̪aொʈaɾpu kaொɭɭaʋum
kiːɻeː uɭɭa piɾiʋu  il amajkkappaʈʈuɭɭa aʈit̪t̪aɭam

eஃp

eஃp t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭ marrum paɳijaːɭaɾkaɭ kaɳit͡ʃamaːna aɭaʋu t͡ʃelaʋu t͡ʃejkiraːɾkaɭ
aʈajjaːɭam kaːɳaʋum pat̪ippuɾimaj aːɾaːjt͡ʃt͡ʃi t͡ʃejjaʋum paʈijeʈut̪t̪al marrum t͡ʃaɾipaːɾt̪t̪al
kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈat̪t̪aj uɾuʋaːkkuʋat̪il paொt̪u ʈaொmajn t͡ʃejalpaʈukirat̪u
t͡ʃeːkaɾippu in̪t̪a mujart͡ʃikaɭ iɾun̪t̪apaோt̪ilum t̪iʈʈam  minnaɳu
paʈajppukaɭ marrum aʋaj t͡ʃeːmikkappaʈum uːʈakam aːkijaʋaj iɾukkalaːm
kurajpaːʈukaɭ muɻumajjaʈajjaːt̪a t̪ullijamarra allat̪u
t͡ʃit̪ajn̪t̪a t̪aɾaʋu ʈiɾaːnskiɾipʂan piɻajkaɭ pat̪ippuɾimaj allat̪u pira ariʋud͡ʒiːʋi
t͡ʃaொt̪t̪u miːral kurajpaːʈuɭɭa allat̪u t͡ʃeːt̪amaʈajn̪t̪a ʋaʈʈu allat̪u pira uːʈakam 
kaɳini ʋajɾas allat̪u t͡ʃeːt̪appaʈut̪t̪um allat̪u paʈikka muʈijaːt̪a kaɳini kurijiːʈukaɭ
uŋkaɭ upakaɾaɳaŋkaɭ

eஃp ʋaɾajjarukkappaʈʈa ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪am t͡ʃeːt̪aŋkaɭin maruppu  uɾimajjajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa
pat̪t̪i  t̪iʈʈat̪t̪il ʋiʋaɾikkappaʈʈuɭɭa maːrriːʈu allat̪u paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpap perut̪al
kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in uɾimajjaːɭaɾ
 ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj marrum oɾu t̪iʈʈat̪t̪aj ʋin̪ijaோkikkum ʋeːru en̪t̪a t̪aɾappinaɾum
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in kiːɻ  elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlaj anajt̪t̪ajjum marukkaʋum
t͡ʃaʈʈappuːɾʋa uʈpaʈa t͡ʃeːt̪aŋkaɭ t͡ʃelaʋukaɭ marrum t͡ʃelaʋukaɭukku uŋkaɭukkaːna paொruppu
kaʈʈaɳam kaʋanakkurajʋukkaːna t̪iːɾʋukaɭ et̪uʋum uŋkaɭiʈam illaj enpat̪aj oppukkaொɭkiriːɾkaɭ kaɳʈippaːnat̪u
paொruppu ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪at̪t̪aj miːrut̪al allat̪u oppan̪t̪a miːral iʋaj t̪aʋiɾa
pat̪t̪i  il ʋaɻaŋkappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u arakkaʈʈaɭaj enpat̪aj n̪iːŋkaɭ oppukkaொɭkiriːɾkaɭ t̪i
ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj uɾimajjaːɭaɾ marrum in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in kiːɻ en̪t̪a ʋin̪ijaோkast̪aɾkaɭum iɾukka maːʈʈaːɾkaɭ
uɳmajjaːna n̪eːɾaʈijaːna marajmukamaːna t̪aொʈaɾt͡ʃt͡ʃijaːna t̪aɳʈanajkkuɾija allat̪u
it̪upaோnra t͡ʃaːt̪t̪ijakkuːrukaɭ kurit̪t̪u n̪iːŋkaɭ ariʋippaj ʋaɻaŋkinaːlum t̪art͡ʃejalaːna t͡ʃeːt̪aŋkaɭ
t͡ʃeːt̪am

eஃp maːrrut̪al allat̪u paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpap peruʋat̪arkaːna ʋaɾajjarukkappaʈʈa uɾimaj  n̪iːŋkaɭ kaɳʈarin̪t̪aːl
in̪t̪a elakʈɾaːnik ʋeːlaj kiʈajt̪t̪a  n̪aːʈkaɭukkuɭ kurajjalaːm
anuppuʋat̪an muːlam n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃelut̪t̪ija paɳat̪t̪aj eːt̪eːnum iɾun̪t̪aːl t̪iɾumpap peruŋkaɭ
n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋeːlajjajp perra n̪apaɾukku eɻut̪t̪uppuːɾʋa ʋiɭakkam n̪iːŋkaɭ enraːl
oɾu ijarpijal uːʈakat̪t̪il ʋeːlaj kiʈajt̪t̪at̪u n̪iːŋkaɭ miːʈijam t̪iɾumpa ʋeːɳʈum
uŋkaɭ eɻut̪t̪u ʋiɭakkam uŋkaɭukku ʋaɻaŋkija n̪apaɾ allat̪u n̪iruʋanam
kurajpaːʈuɭɭa ʋeːlaj  kku pat̪ilaːka maːrru n̪akalaj ʋaɻaŋka t̪eːɾn̪t̪eʈukkalaːm
t̪iɾumpap perut̪al n̪iːŋkaɭ ʋeːlajjaj minnaɳu murajjil perriɾun̪t̪aːl n̪apaɾ allat̪u n̪iruʋanam
at̪aj uŋkaɭukku ʋaɻaŋkinaːl uŋkaɭukku iɾaɳʈaːʋat̪u ʋaːjppaj ʋaɻaŋkalaːm
paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpap peruʋat̪arkup pat̪ilaːka minnaɳu murajjil ʋeːlajjajp peruŋkaɭ iɾaɳʈaːʋat̪u piɾat̪i enraːl
meːlum kurajpaːʈuʈajjat̪u meːlum illaːmal eɻut̪t̪uppuːɾʋamaːka paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpappera kaோɾalaːm
t͡ʃikkalaj t͡ʃaɾit͡ʃejja ʋaːjppukaɭ

eஃp ʋaɾajjarukkappaʈʈa maːrriːʈu allat̪u paɳat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪iɾumpap peruʋat̪arkaːna uɾimajjajt̪ t̪aʋiɾa
pat̪t̪i  il in̪t̪a ʋeːlaj uŋkaɭukku uɭɭapaʈijeː ʋaɻaŋkappaʈukirat̪u ʋeːru et̪uʋum illaj
en̪t̪a ʋakajjaːna ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪aŋkaɭ ʋeɭippaʈajjaːna allat̪u marajmukamaːka uʈpaʈa aːnaːl ʋaɾamparrat̪u
en̪t̪aʋaொɾu n̪aோkkat̪t̪irkaːkaʋum ʋaɾt̪t̪akam allat̪u uʈart̪akut̪ikkaːna ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪aŋkaɭ

 t͡ʃila maːn̪ilaŋkaɭ t͡ʃila marajmukamaːna maruppukaɭaj anumat̪ippat̪illaj
ut̪t̪aɾaʋaːt̪aŋkaɭ allat̪u t͡ʃila ʋakajjaːna t͡ʃeːt̪aŋkaɭin ʋilakku allat̪u ʋaɾampu
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪il kurippiʈappaʈʈuɭɭa eːt̪eːnum maruppu allat̪u ʋaɾampu miːrinaːl
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪irku paொɾun̪t̪akkuːʈija maːn̪ila t͡ʃaʈʈam oppan̪t̪am
muːlam anumat̪ikkappaʈʈa at̪ikapaʈt͡ʃa maruppu allat̪u ʋaɾampukku ʋiɭakkam
paொɾun̪t̪akkuːʈija maːn̪ila t͡ʃaʈʈam eːt̪eːnum t͡ʃellaːt̪a t̪anmaj allat̪u t͡ʃejalpaʈut̪t̪a muʈijaːt̪a t̪anmaj
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪at̪t̪in ʋit̪imuraj miːt̪amuɭɭa ʋit̪ikaɭaj ɾat̪t̪u t͡ʃejjaːt̪u

eஃp iɻappiːʈu  n̪iːŋkaɭ arakkaʈʈaɭajjaj iːʈut͡ʃejt̪u n̪aʈat̪t̪a oppukkaொɭkiriːɾkaɭ
ʋaɾt̪t̪aka mut̪t̪iɾaj uɾimajjaːɭaɾ arakkaʈʈaɭajjin en̪t̪a mukaʋaɾ allat̪u paɳijaːɭaɾ eʋaɾum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭin n̪akalkaɭaj ʋaɻaŋkut̪al
in̪t̪a oppan̪t̪am marrum urpat̪t̪ijuʈan t̪aொʈaɾpuʈajja en̪t̪a t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭum
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭin ʋiɭampaɾam marrum ʋin̪ijaோkam
t͡ʃaʈʈak kaʈʈaɳam uʈpaʈa anajt̪t̪u paொruppukaɭ t͡ʃelaʋukaɭ marrum t͡ʃelaʋukaɭiliɾun̪t̪u paːt̪ippillaːt̪at̪u
n̪iːŋkaɭ t͡ʃejjum pinʋaɾuʋanaʋarril iɾun̪t̪u n̪eːɾaʈijaːkaʋaோ allat̪u marajmukamaːkaʋaோ eɻukirat̪u
allat̪u eːrpaʈak kaːɾaɳam a in̪t̪a allat̪u eːt̪eːnum t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋin̪ijaோkam
ʋeːlaj  maːrram maːrram allat̪u t͡ʃeːɾt̪t̪al allat̪u n̪iːkkut̪al
pɾaːd͡ʒekʈ kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ʋeːlaj marrum i n̪iːŋkaɭ eːrpaʈut̪t̪um eːt̪eːnum kurajpaːʈu


piɾiʋu  kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈat̪t̪in paɳi parrija t̪akaʋal

t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem ilaʋat͡ʃa ʋin̪ijaோkat̪t̪irku ot̪t̪at̪aːka uɭɭat̪u
palʋeːru ʋakajjaːna kaɳinikaɭaːl paʈikkakkuːʈija ʋaʈiʋaŋkaɭil minnaɳu ʋeːlajkaɭ
kaːlaːʋat̪ijaːna paɻajja n̪aʈut̪t̪aɾa ʋajat̪u marrum put̪ija kaɳinikaɭ uʈpaʈa at̪u uɭɭat̪u
n̪uːrrukkaɳakkaːna t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭin mujart͡ʃi marrum n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ kaːɾaɳamaːka
ʋaːɻkkajjin anajt̪t̪u t̪aɾappu makkaɭum

t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭ marrum t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭukku ʋaɻaŋka n̪it̪i ut̪aʋi
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiemaj aʈajʋat̪arku aʋaɾkaɭukkut̪ t̪eːʋajjaːna ut̪aʋi mukkijamaːnat̪u
ilakkukaɭ marrum t̪iʈʈam  t͡ʃeːkaɾippu urut̪i
ʋaɾum t̪alajmurajkaɭukku ilaʋat͡ʃamaːka kiʈajkkum  il t̪iʈʈam
    paːt̪ukaːppaj ʋaɻaŋkuʋat̪arkaːka uɾuʋaːkkappaʈʈat̪u
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem marrum et̪iɾkaːla t͡ʃan̪t̪at̪ijinaɾukkaːna n̪iɾan̪t̪aɾa et̪iɾkaːlam
t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj parri meːlum arija
uŋkaɭ mujart͡ʃikaɭ marrum n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ eʋʋaːru ut̪aʋakkuːʈum piɾiʋu  marrum ajp paːɾkkaʋum
marrum arakkaʈʈaɭaj t̪akaʋal pakkat̪t̪aj  il kaːɳalaːm


pakut̪i  t̪iʈʈam kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppakam parrija t̪akaʋal
arakkaʈʈaɭaj

t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj oɾu ilaːpa n̪aோkkamarrat̪u
 kalʋi n̪iruʋanam t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭin kiːɻ eːrpaːʈu t͡ʃejjappaʈʈuɭɭat̪u
mit͡ʃit͡ʃippi maːn̪ilam marrum uɭn̪aːʈʈaːl ʋaɾi ʋilakku an̪t̪ast̪u ʋaɻaŋkappaʈʈat̪u
ʋaɾuʋaːj t͡ʃeːʋaj arakkaʈʈaɭajjin  allat̪u kuːʈʈaːʈt͡ʃi ʋaɾi aʈajjaːɭam
eɳ  kuʈʈanpeɾk t̪iʈʈat̪t̪irkaːna paŋkaɭippukaɭ
ilakkija kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭajkku muɻu aɭaʋil ʋaɾi ʋilakku uɳʈu
ameɾikka kuːʈʈaːʈt͡ʃi t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭ marrum uŋkaɭ maːn̪ila t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭaːl anumat̪ikkappaʈukirat̪u

arakkaʈʈaɭajjin mut̪anmaj aluʋalakam  melan ʈaːkʈaɾ es
   aːnaːl at̪an t̪annaːɾʋalaɾkaɭum uːɻijaɾkaɭum t͡ʃit̪ariʋiʈʈanaɾ
pala iʈaŋkaɭil at̪an ʋaɳika aluʋalakam  il amajn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u
ʋaʈakku  meːrku t͡ʃaːlʈ leːk t͡ʃiʈʈi     minnaɲt͡ʃal
t̪aொʈaɾpu iɳajppukaɭ marrum t͡ʃamiːpat̪t̪ija t̪aொʈaɾput̪ t̪akaʋalajk kaːɳalaːm
arakkaʈʈaɭajjin iɳajjat̪aɭam marrum / il at̪ikaːɾappuːɾʋa pakkam

kuːʈut̪al t̪aொʈaɾput̪ t̪akaʋalukku
ʈaːkʈaɾ kiɾikaோɾi pi n̪ijuːpi
t̪alajmaj n̪iɾʋaːki marrum ijakkunaɾ
 @

piɾiʋu  kuʈʈanpeɾk t̪iʈʈat̪t̪irkaːna n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ parrija t̪akaʋal
ilakkijak kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj

t̪iʈʈam  t͡ʃaːɾn̪t̪uɭɭat̪u marrum paɾan̪t̪a illaːmal ʋaːɻa muʈijaːt̪u
at̪an paɳijaj n̪irajʋeːrra paொt̪u aːt̪aɾaʋajjum n̪ankaொʈajkaɭajjum paɾappijat̪u
paொt̪u ʈaொmajn marrum uɾimam perra paʈajppukaɭin eɳɳikkajjaj at̪ikaɾikkalaːm
paɾan̪t̪a aɭaʋil aɳukakkuːʈija ijan̪t̪iɾam paʈikkakkuːʈija ʋaʈiʋat̪t̪il ilaʋat͡ʃamaːka ʋin̪ijaோkikkappaʈukirat̪u
kaːlaːʋat̪ijaːna upakaɾaɳaŋkaɭ uʈpaʈa upakaɾaɳaŋkaɭin ʋaɾit͡ʃaj pala t͡ʃirija n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ
$ mut̪al $ ʋaɾaj ʋaɾi ʋilakkukaɭajp paɾaːmaɾippat̪il kurippaːka mukkijamaːnat̪u
 uʈan an̪t̪ast̪u

arakkaʈʈaɭaj oɻuŋkupaʈut̪t̪um t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭukku iɳaŋka urut̪ipuːɳʈuɭɭat̪u
ajkkija n̪aːʈʈin anajt̪t̪u  maːn̪ilaŋkaɭilum t̪aொɳʈu n̪iruʋanaŋkaɭ marrum t̪aொɳʈu n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ
maːn̪ilaŋkaɭil iɳakkat̪ t̪eːʋajkaɭ oɾeː maːt̪iɾijaːnaʋaj alla at̪arku oɾu t̪eːʋaj
kaɳit͡ʃamaːna mujart͡ʃi at̪ika aːʋaɳaŋkaɭ marrum t͡ʃan̪t̪ikka marrum t̪aொʈaɾa pala kaʈʈaɳaŋkaɭ
in̪t̪a t̪eːʋajkaɭuʈan iʈaŋkaɭil n̪ankaொʈajkaɭaj n̪aːŋkaɭ kaோɾuʋat̪illaj
iɳaŋkuʋat̪arkaːna eɻut̪t̪uppuːɾʋa urut̪ippaʈut̪t̪al eŋkaɭukku kiʈajkkaʋillaj t͡ʃejja
n̪ankaொʈajkaɭaj anuppaʋum allat̪u et̪arkum iɳakkat̪t̪in n̪ilajjajt̪ t̪iːɾmaːnikkaʋum
kurippiʈʈa maːn̪ilat̪t̪ajp paːɾʋajjiʈaʋum /

at̪eːt͡ʃamajam n̪aːŋkaɭ iɾukkum maːn̪ilaŋkaɭil iɾun̪t̪u paŋkaɭippukaɭajp pera muʈijaːt̪u marrum kaோɾa muʈijaːt̪u
kaோɾikkaj t̪eːʋajkaɭaj puːɾt̪t̪i t͡ʃejjaʋillaj en̪t̪a t̪aʈajjum eŋkaɭukkut̪ t̪eɾijaːt̪u
at̪t̪akajja maːn̪ilaŋkaɭil uɭɭa n̪ankaொʈajjaːɭaɾkaɭiʈamiɾun̪t̪u kaோɾappaʈaːt̪a n̪ankaொʈajkaɭaj eːrrukkaொɭʋat̪arku et̪iɾaːka
n̪ankaொʈaj ʋaɻaŋkuʋat̪arkaːna t͡ʃalukajkaɭuʈan eŋkaɭaj aɳukaʋum

t͡ʃaɾʋat̪eːt͡ʃa n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ n̪anrijuʈan eːrrukkaொɭɭappaʈukinrana aːnaːl eŋkaɭaːl t͡ʃejja muʈijaːt̪u
perappaʈʈa n̪ankaொʈajkaɭukku ʋaɾiʋit̪ippu t̪aொʈaɾpaːna eːt̪eːnum arikkajkaɭ
ameɾikkaːʋirku ʋeɭijeː ameɾikka t͡ʃaʈʈaŋkaɭ maʈʈumeː n̪amat̪u t͡ʃirija uːɻijaɾkaɭaj t͡ʃat̪uppukkuɭɭaːkkukinrana

t̪arpaோt̪ajja n̪ankaொʈajkku t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾk iɳajjap pakkaŋkaɭajp paːɾkkaʋum
murajkaɭ marrum mukaʋaɾikaɭ n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ palaʋarril eːrrukkaொɭɭappaʈukinrana
kaːt͡ʃaோlajkaɭ aːnlajn kaʈʈaɳaŋkaɭ marrum kiɾeʈiʈ kaːɾʈu n̪ankaொʈajkaɭ uɭɭiʈʈa ʋaɻikaɭ
n̪ankaொʈaj aɭikka t̪ajaʋut͡ʃejt̪u t͡ʃelka /


piɾiʋu  kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem elakʈɾaːnik t̪iʈʈam parrija paொt̪uʋaːna t̪akaʋal
ʋeːlaj t͡ʃejkirat̪u

peːɾaːt͡ʃiɾijaɾ majkkeːl es haːɾʈ kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem t̪iʈʈat̪t̪ajt̪ t̪aோrruʋit̪t̪aʋaɾ
t͡ʃut̪an̪t̪iɾamaːka pakiɾn̪t̪u kaொɭɭakkuːʈija minnaɳu paʈajppukaɭin n̪uːlakat̪t̪in kaɾut̪t̪u
jaːɾuʈanum n̪aːrpat̪u aːɳʈukaɭaːka aʋaɾ t̪iʈʈat̪t̪aj t̪ajaːɾit̪t̪u ʋin̪ijaோkit̪t̪aːɾ
kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭ t̪annaːɾʋa aːt̪aɾaʋin t̪aɭaɾʋaːna n̪eʈʋaொɾk maʈʈumeː

t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭ peɾumpaːlum pala at͡ʃt͡ʃiʈappaʈʈaʋarriliɾun̪t̪u uɾuʋaːkkappaʈukinrana
pat̪ippukaɭ iʋaj anajt̪t̪um ameɾikkaːʋil paொt̪u ʈaொmajnaːka urut̪ippaʈut̪t̪appaʈʈuɭɭana
pat̪ippuɾimaj ariʋippu t͡ʃeːɾkkappaʈaːʋiʈʈaːl enaʋeː n̪aːm aʋat͡ʃijam illaj
minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭaj eːt̪eːnum kurippiʈʈa kaːkit̪a pat̪ippirku iɳaŋka ʋajt̪t̪iɾuŋkaɭ

mukkija  t̪eːʈal ʋat͡ʃat̪ijajk kaொɳʈa eŋkaɭ iɳajjat̪aɭat̪t̪il peɾumpaːlaːnaோɾ t̪aொʈaŋkukinranaɾ



in̪t̪a iɳajjat̪aɭam t̪iʈʈa kuʈʈanpeɾkʈiem parrija t̪akaʋalkaɭaj uɭɭaʈakkijat̪u
pɾaːd͡ʒekʈ kuʈʈanpeɾk ilakkijat̪t̪irku n̪ankaொʈaj aɭippat̪u uʈpaʈa
kaːppaka arakkaʈʈaɭaj eŋkaɭin put̪ija minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭaj eʋʋaːru t̪ajaːɾippat̪u marrum eppaʈi t͡ʃejʋat̪u
put̪ija minput̪t̪akaŋkaɭajp parri arija eŋkaɭ minnaɲt͡ʃal t͡ʃejt̪imaʈalukku kuɻut͡ʃeːɾaʋum
